### [1] [Bayesian Sequential Verification for Budget-Aware Quantum Program Testing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15601v1)
*Lei Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出贝叶斯序贯验证方法，通过自适应测量降低量子程序验证的测量成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子程序验证依赖固定预算模拟器测试，成本高且不适用于噪声后端，缺乏统计显式与预算感知的方法。

Method: 将贝叶斯序贯验证形式化为基于参考的贝叶斯假设检验工作流，从参考源导出先验，随证据积累批次更新决策。

Result: 在Qiskit上对贝尔态和QAOA-MaxCut的评估表明，当成功概率超过阈值时，相比固定预算基线大幅降低测量成本。

Conclusion: 贝叶斯序贯验证是一种实用的量子程序验证工作流，为未来量子持续集成流水线提供基础。

中文摘要：量子程序通常产生概率分布而非确定性输出，使得验证本质上是统计性的，并且在真实硬件上成本越来越高。在实践中，开发者仍经常依赖在模拟器上使用固定预算的测试，这种方法简单但耗时，且不适合噪声后端。目前缺少一种既明确统计性质又考虑预算的验证方法。本文将贝叶斯序贯验证形式化为一种基于参考的贝叶斯假设检验工作流，其中先验来源于明确的参考源，例如有限次数的参考运行或基于理想态向量计算，并且随着测量证据的积累，逐批次更新验证决策。该方法在Qiskit上对两个互补的工作负载进行了评估：贝尔态和QAOA-MaxCut。两个案例研究的结果均表明，当程序的成功概率超过目标阈值时，与固定预算基线相比，贝叶斯序贯验证可以大幅降低测量成本。这些发现将贝叶斯序贯验证定位为量子程序的一种实用验证工作流。该方法为未来的量子持续集成流水线奠定了基础，这些流水线需要可靠且考虑预算的通过/失败决策，并激励在真实量子硬件上进行验证。

Original abstract: Quantum programs often produce probability distributions rather than deterministic outputs, making verification inherently statistical and increasingly costly on real hardware. In practice, developers still frequently rely on testing with fixed shot budgets on simulators, which are simple but time-consuming and poorly suited to noisy backends. What is missing is a verification approach that is both statistically explicit and budget-aware.
  This paper formulates Bayesian sequential verification as a reference-based Bayesian hypothesis testing workflow in which priors are derived from explicit reference sources, such as finite-shot reference runs or ideal/statevector-based computation, and verification decisions are updated batch by batch as measurement evidence accumulates.
  This approach is evaluated in Qiskit on two complementary workloads: Bell-state and QAOA-MaxCut. Across both case studies, the results show that Bayesian sequential verification can substantially reduce measurement costs compared to fixed-budget baselines when the success probability of the program exceeds the target threshold.
  The findings position Bayesian sequential verification as a practical verification workflow for quantum programs. The approach provides a foundation for future quantum continuous-integration pipelines that require reliable, budget-aware pass/fail decisions and motivates validation on real quantum hardware.

</details>


### [2] [Position: Early-Stage Quality Assurance in Annotation Pipelines Is More Cost-Effective Than Late-Stage Validation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15714v1)
*Sunil Kothari,Sumukha Sharma Thoppanahalli Chandramouli,Naman Khandelwal,Parth Kulshreshtha,Ashi Jain,Kriti Banka,Tanuja Chintada,Venkata Triveni,Gulipalli Praveen Kumar,Manish Mehta,Tao Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文主张机器学习标注流程应引入"左移"原则，早期质量保证比后期验证更能降低成本与错误率，并提出验证时机分类与误差传播模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据质量瓶颈限制基础模型改进，但现有研究仅关注验证方法而忽视时机；借鉴软件工程"左移"原则，早期检测缺陷成本远低于后期。

Method: 提出三种QA触发点分类（T0预标注、T1后标注、T2审核后），构建参数化误差传播模型，并调查47篇近期论文中QA时机的报告情况。

Result: 仅有4%的论文报告验证时机，表明存在巨大差距；模型揭示了时机对错误率和成本的影响机制。

Conclusion: 应报告QA时机配置、平台将其作为一等参数、开展受控实验测量阶段检测率。

中文摘要：这篇立场论文认为，机器学习社区应优先关注标注流程中的早期质量保证，而非当前普遍采用的后期验证实践。数据质量瓶颈日益成为基础模型改进的限制因素，然而质量保证研究几乎完全聚焦于验证方法而非验证时机。验证何时进行，而不仅仅采用何种方法，从根本上决定了错误率和标注成本。这种对时机的忽视令人费解，因为软件工程中已确立的“左移”原则通过实证研究表明，后期阶段检测到的缺陷成本乘数为4-100倍（Boehm, 1981; Shull et al., 2002）。标注流程展现出类似的动态：在标注开始前捕获的错误成本远低于审核周期完成后发现的错误。我们提出了一个三种质量保证触发点的分类法，即预标注（T0）、后标注（T1）和审核后（T2），将标注工作流分解为离散的验证机会。一个参数化错误传播模型形式化了时机何时影响最终错误率而何时仅影响经济性，使时机成为可测量的设计变量而非事后配置。对47篇近期论文的调查显示，仅有4%报告了验证发生的时间，这一差距在相邻领域已证明时机的影响下尤为惊人。如果没有对质量保证时机的明确关注，社区可能会在优化验证方法的同时忽视了可能最重要的结构变量。落实这一立场需要三个步骤：研究人员应在验证方法之外同时报告质量保证时机配置；标注平台应将时机暴露为一等参数；社区应运行受控实验直接测量各阶段检测率。

Original abstract: This position paper argues that the machine learning community should prioritize early-stage quality assurance in annotation pipelines over the prevailing practice of late-stage validation. Data quality bottlenecks increasingly limit foundation model improvement, yet quality assurance research focuses almost exclusively on validation methods rather than validation timing. When validation occurs, not merely what methods are employed, fundamentally determines both error rates and annotation costs. This temporal neglect is puzzling given the well-established "shift-left" principle from software engineering, where empirical studies demonstrate 4--100x cost multipliers for defects detected in later stages (Boehm, 1981; Shull et al., 2002). Annotation pipelines exhibit analogous dynamics: errors caught before annotation begins cost a fraction of those discovered after review cycles complete. We propose a taxonomy of three QA trigger points, namely pre-annotation (T0), post-annotation (T1), and post-review (T2), that decompose annotation workflows into discrete validation opportunities. A parametric error-propagation model formalizes when timing affects final error rates versus only economics, making timing a measurable design variable rather than a configuration afterthought. A survey of 47 recent papers reveals that only 4% report when validation occurs, a striking gap given timing's demonstrated impact in adjacent fields. Without explicit attention to QA timing, the community risks optimizing validation methods while ignoring the structural variable that may matter most. Acting on this position requires three steps: researchers should report QA timing configurations alongside validation methods; annotation platforms should expose timing as a first-class parameter; and the community should run controlled experiments that measure stage-specific detection rates directly.

</details>


### [3] [BootstrapAgent: Distilling Repository Setup into Reusable Agent Knowledge](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15815v1)
*Sihan Fu,Oucheng Liu,Shiyuan Wang,Jin Shi,Chengkun Wei*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: BootstrapAgent通过多代理框架将仓库启动过程中的探索知识提炼为可复用的合约，显著提升启动成功率和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代码代理处理仓库需要昂贵的启动过程，且探索产生的知识无法跨会话复用。

Method: 提出BootstrapAgent多代理框架，通过证据提取、结构化规划、Docker确定性验证、追踪驱动修复生成.bootstrap合约，并引入干净回放的热修复和带健全性检查的增量修复。

Result: 在三个基准上成功率92.9%，优于基线10%以上，下游令牌使用减少25.9%，构建时间减少22.3%。

Conclusion: BootstrapAgent能有效将仓库启动知识持久化并复用，提升代码代理的效率和成功率。

中文摘要：代码代理越来越多地帮助开发者处理不熟悉的仓库，但每个这样的任务都依赖于一个昂贵的先决条件：将仓库启动到一个可用的开发状态。这个过程需要大量的试错探索，然而产生的知识——已解决的依赖、修复策略——被困在单个对话中，无法供未来的代理使用。因此，我们将仓库启动形式化为一个可复用的启动知识问题，并引入BootstrapAgent，一个多代理框架，它将启动探索过程中发现的启发式方法提炼成一个持久的、可验证的、代理可消费的.bootstrap合约。通过证据提取、结构化规划、基于Docker的确定性验证和追踪驱动的修复，BootstrapAgent生成一个涵盖环境设置、诊断检查、最小验证和累积修复知识的合约。我们进一步提出了带干净回放的热修复以加速迭代调试而不牺牲冷启动可重现性，以及带健全性检查的增量修复以防止奖励黑客攻击。在三个基准上的实验表明，BootstrapAgent实现了92.9%的成功率，优于基线超过10%，同时将下游代理的令牌使用量减少了25.9%，构建时间减少了22.3%。我们的代码可在https://github.com/Vossera/BootstrapAgent获取。

Original abstract: Code agents increasingly help developers work with unfamiliar repositories, but every such task depends on a costly prerequisite: bootstrapping the repository into a usable development state. This process requires substantial trial-and-error exploration, yet the resulting knowledge--resolved dependencies, repair strategies--stays trapped in a single conversation, unavailable to future agents. We therefore formulate repository bootstrapping as a reusable startup knowledge problem and introduce BootstrapAgent, a multi-agent framework that distills the heuristics discovered during bootstrap exploration into a persistent, verifiable, agent-consumable .bootstrap contract. Through evidence extraction, structured planning, deterministic Docker-based verification, and trace-driven repair, BootstrapAgent generates a contract covering environment setup, diagnostic checks, minimal verification, and accumulated repair knowledge. We further propose warm repair with clean replay to accelerate iterative debugging without sacrificing cold-start reproducibility, and a delta repair with sanity check to prevent reward hacking. Experiments on three benchmarks show that BootstrapAgent achieves a 92.9% success rate, outperforming the baseline by over 10% while reducing downstream agent token usage by 25.9% and build time by 22.3%. Our code is available at https://github.com/Vossera/BootstrapAgent.

</details>


### [4] [RoadmapBench: Evaluating Long-Horizon Agentic Software Development Across Version Upgrades](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15846v2)
*Xinbo Xu,Ruihan Yang,Haiyang Shen,Wendong Xu,Bofei Gao,Ruoyu Wu,Kean Shi,Weichu Xie,Xuanzhong Chen,Ming Wu,Jason Zeng,Michael Heinrich,Elvis Zhang,Liang Chen,Kuan Li,Baobao Chang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了RoadmapBench基准，包含115个基于实际开源版本升级的长期编码任务，评估发现最强模型仅解决39.1%，表明长期软件开发仍远未解决。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准多聚焦单问题错误修复，无法反映实际中跨文件、多目标的长期开发挑战。

Method: 从17个仓库和5种语言的实际版本升级中构建115个任务，每个任务提供源代码快照和多目标路线图指令，并评估13个前沿模型。

Result: 最强模型Claude-Opus-4.7解决39.1%，最弱5.2%，与现有bug-fix基准的显著对比。

Conclusion: 长期软件开发仍然是 largely unsolved problem。

中文摘要：编码智能体越来越多地部署在实际的软件开发中，其中单个版本迭代需要跨多个文件的数月协调工作。然而，现有的大多数基准主要关注来自Python仓库的单问题错误修复，评估结果简单为通过/失败，因此未能捕捉到实际工程规模下的长期、多目标开发。为弥补这一缺口，我们提出了RoadmapBench，这是一个包含115个长期编码任务的基准，这些任务基于17个仓库和5种编程语言的实际开源版本升级。每个任务将智能体置于源版本的代码快照上，并提供一个多目标路线图指令，要求其实现目标版本中引入的功能，中位修改量为51个文件中的3700行代码。我们对13个前沿模型进行了系统评估，发现即使是最强的Claude-Opus-4.7也只解决了39.1%的任务，而最弱的仅达到5.2%，这与现有的错误修复基准形成鲜明对比，表明长期软件开发仍然是一个 largely unsolved problem。

Original abstract: Coding agents are increasingly deployed in real software development, where a single version iteration requires months of coordinated work across many files. However, most existing benchmarks focus predominantly on single-issue bug fixes from Python repositories, with coarse pass/fail evaluation outcomes, and thus fail to capture long-horizon, multi-target development at real engineering scale. To address this gap, we present RoadmapBench, a benchmark of 115 long-horizon coding tasks grounded in real open-source version upgrades across 17 repositories and 5 programming languages. Each task places the agent on a source-version code snapshot and provides a multi-target roadmap instruction requiring it to implement the functionality introduced in the target version, with a median modification of 3,700 lines across 51 files. We conduct a systematic evaluation on thirteen frontier models and find that even the strongest, Claude-Opus-4.7, resolves only 39.1% of tasks, while the weakest achieves merely 5.2%, in stark contrast to existing bug-fix benchmarks, suggesting that long-horizon software development remains a largely unsolved problem.

</details>


### [5] [From Text to DSL: Evaluating Grammar-Based Model Generation Using Open LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15865v1)
*Junaid Baber,Nicolas Hili,Didier Schwab,Léo Challier,Cécilia Satrin*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 评估开源LLM在少样本提示下生成DSL模型的能力，发现小型模型（如gemma3:12b、mistral:7b-instruct）可达到接近大型模型的性能，提供成本效益高的替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖大型专有LLM，成本高且部署受限，需要探索更易获取的开源小模型。

Method: 使用0.5B到32B参数的开源LLM，仅通过少样本提示生成符合DSL的UI和数据模型，评估语法有效性、语义完整性和模型间引用一致性。

Result: 在39个LLM的评估中，紧凑模型（如gemma3:12b、mistral:7b-instruct）在质量上接近或匹配更大模型，展示出良好性能。

Conclusion: 小型开源LLM适用于MDE中的DSL生成，是封闭LLM的成本效益高且可部署的替代方案。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在自动化模型驱动软件工程任务方面展现出越来越大的潜力，特别是从自然语言生成符合领域特定语言（DSL）的模型。然而，大多数现有方法依赖于大型专有模型，其高成本和有限的可部署性阻碍了更广泛的采用。在本文中，我们评估了不同规模（0.5B到32B参数）的开源LLM是否能够仅通过少样本提示（无需微调）生成符合DSL的模型。我们的评估聚焦于模型驱动工程（MDE）的关键要求，包括语法有效性、语义完整性和模型间引用一致性。我们在先前工作的基础上进行了扩展，从基于固定预定义数据模式（“数据模型”）生成用户界面模型（本文中称为“UI模型”）转向完全从头生成UI和数据模型。这一转变有两个目的：首先，它突出了LLM推断领域特定关系并在多个互连模型间保持一致性的能力；其次，通过测试不同性质和结构角色的DSL生成，使我们能够推广先前的发现。我们的结构化评估结合了自动解析和专家反馈，涉及39个LLM，揭示了几个紧凑模型（例如gemma3:12b、mistral:7b-instruct）在质量上接近甚至匹配更大的模型。这些发现证明了在MDE工作流中使用更小、开源LLM进行符合语法的DSL生成的可行性，为封闭LLM提供了一种成本效益高且可部署的替代方案。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown increasing potential in automating model-driven software engineering tasks, particularly in generating models conforming to Domain Specific Languages (DSLs) from natural language. While most existing approaches rely on large proprietary models, their high cost and limited deployability hinder broader adoption.
  In this paper, we evaluate whether open-source LLMs of varying sizes (0.5B to 32B parameters) can generate DSL-conformant models using only few-shot prompting, without any fine-tuning. Our evaluation focuses on key model-driven engineering (MDE) requirements, including syntactic validity, semantic completeness, and inter-model reference consistency.
  We extend our prior work by moving from generating user interface models (referred to as "UI models" in this paper) over fixed, predefined data schemas ("data models") to generating both the UI and data models entirely from scratch. This shift serves two purposes: first, it highlights the LLM's ability to infer domain-specific relationships and maintain consistency across multiple interconnected models; second, it allows us to generalize earlier findings by testing DSL generation across models of different natures and structural roles. Our structured evaluation combines automatic parsing and expert feedback across 39 LLMs, revealing that several compact models (e.g., \texttt{gemma3:12b}, \texttt{mistral:7b-instruct}) approach or match the quality of much larger models.
  These findings demonstrate the feasibility of using smaller, open-source LLMs for grammar-conformant DSL generation in MDE workflows, offering a cost-effective and deployable alternative to closed LLMs.

</details>


### [6] [XSearch: Explainable Code Search via Concept-to-Code Alignment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16046v2)
*Yiming Liu,Ruofan Liu,Yun Lin,Zicong Zhang,Weiyu Kong,Pengnian Qi,Xiao Cheng,Weinan Zhang,Qianxiang Wang,Linpeng Huang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出XSearch，通过将代码搜索重新表述为演绎概念对齐问题，实现了本质可解释的代码搜索，大幅提升了分布外泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语义代码搜索方法虽在基准数据集上表现良好，但可解释性和泛化能力差，尤其在分布偏移下性能严重下降，且无法提供检索结果的解释。

Method: XSearch将代码搜索视为演绎概念对齐问题：先识别查询中的功能概念，再显式对齐到代码语句，训练编码器时使用概念对齐目标，检索时通过显式匹配实现。

Result: 在CodeSearchNet上使用GraphCodeBERT训练，XSearch在分布外基准上将性能从0.02提升至0.33（提升15倍），优于八个最先进检索器及参数高达7B的基线；用户研究显示概念对齐解释提升了检索结果评估的速度和准确性。

Conclusion: XSearch通过概念对齐的可解释框架有效提升了代码搜索的分布外泛化能力和可解释性，验证了演绎对齐比归纳嵌入更适合代码搜索任务。

中文摘要：语义代码搜索已在学术界和工业界广泛采用。这些方法将自然语言查询和代码片段嵌入到共享的嵌入空间中，并基于向量相似性检索结果。尽管在基准数据集上表现出色，但它们通常存在可解释性和泛化能力差的问题。检索到的代码可能看似语义相似，却缺少查询的关键功能要求，同时无法提供为何检索到该结果的解释。此外，这种失败在分布偏移下变得更加严重，模型难以泛化到未见过的基准。在这项工作中，我们提出了XSearch，一个本质可解释的代码搜索框架。我们的关键见解是，依赖全局嵌入相似性，现有检索器本质上采取了归纳的观点。它们学习统计模式，而非真正理解查询的功能需求。我们通过将代码搜索重新表述为演绎概念对齐问题来解决这个问题。XSearch（i）识别查询中的功能概念，（ii）明确地将它们与相应的代码语句对齐。这种先解释后预测的设计产生了固有的概念级解释，并减轻了损害分布外泛化的捷径学习。我们使用明确的概念对齐目标训练编码器，并通过查询概念和代码语句之间的显式匹配进行检索。实验表明，使用GraphCodeBERT（125M参数）在CodeSearchNet上训练，XSearch在八个最先进的检索器上将分布外基准的性能从0.02提高到0.33（15倍），并且持续优于参数高达7B的基于编码器和解码器的基线。一项用户研究表明，概念对齐解释使用户能够更快、更准确地评估检索结果。

Original abstract: Semantic code search has been widely adopted in both academia and industry. These approaches embed natural-language queries and code snippets into a shared embedding space and retrieve results based on vector similarity. Despit strong performance on benchmark datasets, they often suffer from poor explainability and generalization. Retrieved code may appear semantically similar yet miss critical functional requirements of the query, while providing no explanation of why the result was retrieved. Moreover, such failures become more severe under distribution shift, where models struggle to generalize to unseen benchmarks. In this work, we propose XSearch, an intrinsically explainable code search framework. Our key insight is that by relying on global embedding similarity, existing retrievers inherently take an inductive view. They learn statistical patterns rather than truly understanding the query's functional requirements. We address this problem by reformulating code search as a deductive concept alignment problem. XSearch (i) identifies functional concepts in the query and (ii) explicitly aligns them with corresponding code statements. This explain-then-predict design produces inherent concept-level explanations and mitigates shortcut learning that harms out-of-distribution generalization. We train an encoder with explicit concept-alignment objectives and perform retrieval through explicit matching between query concepts and code statements. Experiments show that, trained on CodeSearchNet using GraphCodeBERT (125M parameters), XSearch improves performance on out-of-distribution benchmarks from 0.02 to 0.33 (15x) over eight state-of-the-art retrievers, and consistently outperforms both encoder- and decoder-based baselines with up to 7B parameters. A user study demonstrates that concept-alignment explanations enable users to evaluate retrieved results faster and more accurately.

</details>


### [7] [The Dangers of Non-Self-Fixed Architecture Technical Debt and Its Impact on Time-to-Fix](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16133v1)
*Edi Sutoyo,Paris Avgeriou,Andrea Capiluppi*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过在Apache开源项目中分析自修复与非自修复架构技术债务的偿还动态，发现非自修复债务在多人参与时更易长期未解决，建议增加引入者参与并记录设计原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ATD的偿还责任（谁偿还）以及自修复与非自修复ATD在修复时间上的差异尚未被充分研究，已有研究缺乏实证证据。

Method: 使用Apache项目数据，通过Jira与版本控制历史重建ATD生命周期，采用描述性统计、非参数检验和生存分析比较自修复与非自修复ATD的偿还动态。

Result: 自修复与非自修复ATD具有不同的偿还动态；非自修复ATD在变更涉及多个开发者时更可能长期未解决。

Conclusion: 维护者应识别高风险ATD项，通过增加引入者参与和记录设计原理来降低交接成本。

中文摘要：技术债务（TD）是指开发人员优先考虑短期交付而非质量改进工作时产生的长期成本。架构技术债务（ATD）产生于架构决策（如技术选择、模式或分解）优先考虑近期进展而非未来的可维护性和可演化性。由于ATD影响系统的核心结构并通过架构依赖关系传播，因此其修复通常比局部代码级债务更昂贵且更具破坏性。尽管ATD已被广泛研究，但偿还责任的一个重要且未被充分探讨的方面是谁执行偿还。先前的工作关于ATD中偿还责任及其与修复时间的关系提供的实证证据有限。我们实证研究了自修复ATD（即引入者也偿还债务）并与大型Apache开源项目中的非自修复ATD进行对比。我们通过追踪Jira工件到版本控制历史来重建ATD生命周期，以识别引入和偿还时间点并分配开发者角色。我们针对三个研究问题进行了探讨：自修复ATD的普遍性、自修复与非自修复项在修复时间上的差异，以及与代码变更和协作度量相关的因素如何影响偿还速度。通过描述性统计、非参数检验和生存分析，我们发现自修复和非自修复ATD表现出不同的偿还动态，以及在ATD受影响文件上变更共享方式的差异。特别是，当变更分布在许多开发者之间时，非自修复ATD更可能长期未解决。这些结果为维护者提供了可操作的指导，以识别高风险ATD项，并通过在可能时增加引入者的参与以及在偿还期间记录设计原理来减少交接成本。

Original abstract: Technical Debt (TD) refers to the long-term costs incurred when developers prioritize short-term delivery over quality-improving work. Architectural Technical Debt (ATD) arises when architectural decisions (e.g., technology choices, patterns, or decomposition) prioritize near-term progress over future maintainability and evolvability. Because ATD affects a system's core structure and propagates through architectural dependencies, it is often more expensive and disruptive to remediate than localized code-level debt. Although ATD has been widely studied, an important but underexplored aspect of repayment is who performs it. Prior work provides limited empirical evidence on repayment responsibility in ATD and its relationship to time-to-fix.
  We empirically study self-fixed ATD, where the introducer also repays the debt, and contrast it with non-self-fixed ATD in large Apache open-source projects. We reconstruct ATD lifecycles by tracing Jira artifacts to version-control history to identify introduction and repayment points and attribute developer roles. We address three research questions on the prevalence of self-fixed ATD, time-to-fix differences between self-fixed and non--self-fixed items, and how factors related to code change and collaboration metrics relate to repayment speed. Using descriptive statistics, non-parametric tests, and survival analysis, we show that self-fixed and non--self-fixed ATD exhibit distinct repayment dynamics and differences in how changes are shared on ATD-affected files. In particular, non--self-fixed ATD is more likely to remain unresolved longer when changes are spread across many developers. These results provide actionable guidance for maintainers to identify high-risk ATD items and to reduce handoff costs by increasing introducer involvement when possible and documenting the design rationale during repayment.

</details>


### [8] [Customizing an LLM for Enterprise Software Engineering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16517v2)
*Aditya Kini,Satish Chandra,Milad Hashemi,Saksham Thakur,Aditya Pandey,Vincent Nguyen,Marc Brockschmidt,Franjo Ivančić,Danny Tarlow,Parthasarathy Ranganathan,Petros Maniatis,Ahmed Omran,Zaheer Abbas,Anita Gergely,Martin Sevenich,Gufeng Zhang,Amy Hua,Alexander Frömmgen*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文介绍了Gemini for Google (GfG)，一个为Google内部软件工程生态系统定制的LLM，通过专有数据集和中期训练策略，在A/B测试中显著提升了开发效率，并提供了企业模型适配的全面指南。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 企业软件开发过程中产生的数据可用于定制LLMs，以优化企业特定的软件工程任务，但现有前沿模型缺乏针对性，需要有效的定制方法。

Method: 使用万亿令牌的专有数据集，对Gemini进行持续预训练和后训练，采用中期训练策略减轻灾难性遗忘，并在Google内部部署进行大规模A/B测试。

Result: 在29,000名开发人员的盲法A/B研究中，GfG使每轮平均迭代次数减少23%，代码存活率提高约17%。

Conclusion: 通过定制化的模型适配方法，可以显著提升企业软件工程效率，且该方法具有可复制性，适用于其他组织利用内部数据。

中文摘要：企业软件开发是一个持续的演进过程，其特点是增量添加、架构修订、生产部署和严格的维护。这些活动会产生宝贵的数据，现代LLMs可以针对这些数据进行微调，从而为企业软件工程解锁额外的工具可能性。虽然前沿的LLMs已经非常强大，但这种定制化形式为企业特定优化提供了一条有吸引力的路径。我们介绍了Gemini for Google (GfG)，这是Gemini专为Google内部软件工程生态系统定制的版本。本文详细介绍了该模型的端到端开发过程，从策划一个万亿令牌的专有数据集到实现一种能够减轻灾难性遗忘的中期训练策略。在一项涉及29,000名开发人员的大规模盲法A/B研究中，Gemini for Google显著优于基线：每轮平均迭代次数减少了23%，代码存活率提高了约17%。除指标外，我们还提供了一个全面的企业模型适配蓝图，涵盖：(1)从软件工程数据中提取高价值信号，(2)数据准备策略，(3)全栈模型调优（持续预训练和后训练），以及(4)下游应用程序的部署。我们相信这种方法为其他组织释放其内部工程数据的全部潜力提供了一条可复制的路径。

Original abstract: Enterprise software development is a continuous evolutionary process, characterized by incremental additions, architectural revisions, production deployments and rigorous maintenance. These activities generate valuable data that modern LLMs could be finetuned on, to unlock additional tool possibilities for enterprise software engineering. While frontier LLMs are already very capable, this form of customization offers a compelling path for enterprise-specific optimization.
  We introduce Gemini for Google (GfG)}, an adaptation of Gemini specialized for Google's internal software engineering ecosystem. This paper details the model's end-to-end development, from curating a trillion-token proprietary dataset to implementing a mid-training strategy that mitigates catastrophic forgetting. In a large-scale blind A/B study across 29,000 developers, Gemini for Google significantly outperformed baselines: reducing the mean number of iterations per turn by 23\%, and increasing code survival rates by about 17%. Beyond metrics, we provide a comprehensive blueprint for enterprise model adaptation, covering: (1)The extraction of high-value signals from software engineering data, (2)Data preparation strategies, (3)Full-stack model tuning (continued pre-training and post-training), and (4)The deployment of downstream applications. We believe this methodology offers a replicable path for other organizations to unlock the full potential of their internal engineering data.

### [9] [TARIPlay: A Test Framework for AR Applications based on Interactive Area Tracking in Playback Videos](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16544v1)
*Seyed Amir Mousavi,Xiaoyin Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: TARIPlay通过分析回放视频并识别交互区域，实现了AR应用的自动化测试，显著提高了分支覆盖率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AR应用测试面临环境易变、动态交互区域难以识别等挑战，现有工具如Monkey覆盖率低。

Method: TARIPlay框架通过检测、跟踪、过滤回放视频中的交互区域，基于稳定性和可见性标准生成测试机会，并驱动自动化测试引擎。

Result: 在四个开源AR应用上，TARIPlay的分支覆盖率达到55.8%，优于Monkey的41.98%。

Conclusion: TARIPlay有效提升了AR应用自动化测试的覆盖率，并能评估回放视频质量。

中文摘要：随着增强现实（AR）越来越深入地融入日常生活，确保AR应用的质量、安全和可靠性日益重要。然而，AR应用对自动化测试提出了独特挑战。与传统移动应用中的静态GUI布局不同，AR应用从周围环境中获取交互界面，而环境是易变且非确定性的。最近的进展如ARCore Playback和ARKit Replay允许开发者通过录制和回放增强视频来重用真实世界场景，使自动化AR测试更加可行。然而，使用回放视频引入了两个主要挑战：测试输入必须精确计时，且视频中的交互区域是动态、不规则且难以识别的。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了TARIPlay，一个分析回放视频以检测、跟踪和过滤随时间变化的合适交互区域的框架，用于自动化测试。具体来说，TARIPlay基于稳定性和可见性等标准识别可行的测试机会，然后将这些信息提供给自动化测试引擎以模拟用户交互。我们使用四个开源AR应用和九个回放视频进行了实验。评估结果显示，TARIPlay在AR相关代码的测试覆盖率上显著优于现有工具Monkey（分支覆盖率55.8%对比41.98%），并且还可以用于评估回放视频对测试适用性的质量。

Original abstract: As Augmented Reality (AR) becomes more and more embedded in daily life, ensuring the quality, safety, and reliability of AR applications is increasingly important. However, AR apps present unique challenges for automated testing. Unlike static GUI layouts in traditional mobile apps, AR apps acquire their interaction interface from the surrounding environment, which is volatile and non-deterministic. Recent advancements like ARCore Playback and ARKit Replay allow developers to reuse real-world scenarios by recording and playing back enriched videos, enabling more feasible automated AR testing. However, using playback videos introduces two major challenges: test inputs must be timed precisely, and interactive areas in the video are dynamic, irregular, and difficult to identify. To address these challenges, we propose TARIPlay, a framework that analyzes playback videos to detect, track, and filter proper interactive areas over time for automated testing. In particular, TARIPlay identifies viable test opportunities based on criteria like stability and visibility, then feeds this information to an automated testing engine to simulate user interactions. We perform an experiment with four open-source AR apps and nine playback videos. Evaluation results show that TARIPlay significantly outperforms the existing tool Monkey in test coverage (55.8% over 41.98% on branch coverage) of AR-related code, and can also be used to assess the quality of playback videos for testing suitability.

### [10] [LLM-based vs. Search-based Merge Conflict Resolution: An Empirical Study of Competing Paradigms](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16646v1)
*Heleno de Souza Campos Junior,Leonardo Gresta Paulino Murta*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 首次直接比较LLM和SBSE两种范式解决软件合并冲突的效果，发现LLM擅长不平衡冲突但受限于非英文和大输入，SBSE泛化能力强且擅长平衡冲突，提出混合系统方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解LLM和SBSE两种范式的相对优势和劣势，为实际工具选择提供依据。

Method: 使用MergeGen（LLM）和SBCR（SBSE）对数千个Java、C#、JavaScript、TypeScript的真实冲突进行实验对比。

Result: LLM擅长不平衡冲突，但处理非英文和大输入时效果差；SBSE泛化性好，擅长平衡冲突。

Conclusion: 两种范式各有优劣，应开发混合系统结合两者优势。

中文摘要：背景：软件合并冲突的解决正受到两种竞争范式的重塑：基于大型语言模型（LLM）的生成式方法和基于搜索的软件工程（SBSE）的优化方法。虽然这两种范式的工具都显示出前景，但它们的相对优势、劣势和权衡尚未得到充分理解。目标：本文首次进行深入的实证研究，直接比较这两种范式，以识别它们在实际场景中的能力和局限性。方法：我们评估了MergeGen（一种最先进的基于LLM的工具）与SBCR（一种采用随机重启爬山算法（RRHC）的新型SBSE方法）。比较使用了来自Java、C#、JavaScript和TypeScript开源项目的数千个真实冲突。结果：我们的发现揭示了基本的权衡。LLM范式通过利用学习到的模式擅长解决内容不平衡的冲突，但在处理非英文内容和大型输入时遇到困难，可能导致截断或空分辨率。相反，SBSE范式在数据集上表现出更好的泛化能力，并且在平衡冲突上表现最佳，突显其作为稳健、数据无关替代方案的潜力。结论：两种范式都不是万能药。我们的发现强调了依赖于上下文的优势，并推动了混合系统的开发，该系统结合LLM和SBSE方法的互补能力，以创建更稳健和可靠的合并冲突解决工具。

Original abstract: Context: The resolution of software merge conflicts is being reshaped by two competing paradigms: generative approaches based on Large Language Models (LLMs) and optimization approaches from Search-Based Software Engineering (SBSE). While tools from both paradigms have shown promise, their relative strengths, weaknesses, and trade-offs are not yet well understood.
  Objective: This paper presents the first in-depth empirical study directly comparing these paradigms to identify their capabilities and limitations in real-world scenarios.
  Method: We evaluated MergeGen, a state-of-the-art LLM-based tool, against SBCR, a novel SBSE approach employing a Random Restart Hill Climbing (RRHC) algorithm. The comparison used thousands of real-world conflicts from open-source projects written in Java, C#, JavaScript, and TypeScript.
  Results: Our findings reveal fundamental trade-offs. The LLM paradigm excels at resolving conflicts with imbalanced content by leveraging learned patterns. However, it struggles with non-English content and large inputs, which can lead to truncated or empty resolutions. Conversely, the SBSE paradigm demonstrates superior generalization across datasets and performs best on balanced conflicts, highlighting its potential as a robust, data-independent alternative.
  Conclusions: Neither paradigm is a silver bullet. Our findings highlight context-dependent strengths and motivate the development of hybrid systems that combine the complementary capabilities of LLM and SBSE approaches to create more robust and reliable merge conflict resolution tools.

</details>

### [12] [What's Inside a GitHub Repository? An Empirical Study on the Contents of 10K Projects](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16701v2)
*Andre Hora,João Eduardo Montandon,Diego Elias Costa*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 对10,000个GitHub仓库的十年演变分析揭示了标准工件整合、CI/CD平台更替、配置格式变化、Dockerfile增长及LLM/AI内容的兴起。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对GitHub上实际仓库内容缺乏了解，需要通过实证分析揭示其真实构成和长期趋势。

Method: 分析10,000个GitHub仓库的文件、目录和扩展名，并追踪其十年间的演变。

Result: 发现五大主要变化：标准工件巩固、GitHub Actions主导、配置格式变迁、Dockerfile增长、LLM/AI内容涌现。

Conclusion: 开源演化受GitHub标准影响加深，技术兴衰明显，该研究为挖掘软件仓库研究提供了支撑。

中文摘要：GitHub是最大的代码托管平台，拥有数百万个跨多种技术的仓库。尽管如此，人们对GitHub仓库在现实世界中的实际内容知之甚少。本文提出了一项初步的实证分析，以更好地理解真实世界GitHub仓库的内容。我们分析了10,000个GitHub仓库中的文件、目录和扩展名，以及它们十年来的演变。我们的结果显示了过去十年GitHub的主要变化：（1）README.md、.gitignore和LICENSE作为标准工件的整合；（2）GitHub Actions作为主导的CI/CD平台的崛起；（3）TOML、YAML和JSON等配置格式的增长，以及XML的下降；（4）新趋势，如Dockerfile的增长；（5）与LLM和生成式AI相关的新兴内容（例如AGENTS.md和CLAUDE.md）。基于我们的发现，我们讨论了其影响，包括开源不仅有机地发展，而且越来越受到GitHub标准的引导，技术的兴衰，以及对挖掘软件仓库研究的潜在支持。

Original abstract: GitHub is the largest code hosting platform, with millions of repositories spanning multiple technologies. Despite this, little is known about the actual contents of GitHub's repositories in the wild. This paper presents an initial empirical analysis to better understand the contents of real-world GitHub repositories. We analyze the files, directories, and extensions present in 10,000 GitHub repositories, as well as their evolution over ten years. Our results show major changes in GitHub over the last decade: (1) the consolidation of README.md, .gitignore, and LICENSE as standard artifacts; (2) the rise of GitHub Actions as the dominant CI/CD platform; (3) the growth of configuration formats such as TOML, YAML, and JSON, alongside a decline in XML; (4) new trends, such as the growth of Dockerfile; and (5) emerging content related to LLMs and generative AI (e.g., AGENTS.md and CLAUDE.md). Based on our findings, we discuss implications, including that open source is not only evolving organically but also increasingly guided by GitHub's standards, the rise and fall of technologies, and the potential support for mining software repository studies.

</details>


### [13] [AI Policy, Disclosure, and Human in the Loop: How Are Contribution Guidelines Adapting to GenAI?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16706v2)
*Andre Hora,Romain Robbes*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过分析1000个GitHub仓库中的118个AI政策，发现78%允许AI辅助贡献，51%要求披露，74%要求人类参与，表明大多数政策积极但强调披露和人类参与。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI改变了软件开发，开源项目需要制定AI使用政策，但目前缺乏对政策内容和最佳实践的明确了解。

Method: 分析了1000个流行的GitHub仓库，从中识别出118个针对贡献者的AI政策，并进行统计分类。

Result: 78%的政策允许AI辅助贡献，22%明确不鼓励；51%要求披露AI使用；74%要求人类参与。

Conclusion: 大多数开源项目对GenAI持积极态度，但AI披露和人类参与是贡献过程的基本要求，对开发者和研究者有重要启示。

中文摘要：生成式人工智能（GenAI）近年来已经改变了软件开发。由于代码生成的便利性，开源项目迎来了贡献的增长。为了应对GenAI的崛起，开源项目开始实施关于在贡献中使用AI的政策。然而，开源项目在多大程度上明确规定了AI辅助贡献是被允许还是禁止，以及贡献者的最佳实践，仍然不清楚。本文提供了一项初步的实证研究，探讨开源项目如何适应GenAI贡献。我们分析了1,000个流行的GitHub仓库，并识别了118个针对贡献者的AI政策。我们的结果显示：（1）78%的AI政策允许AI辅助的贡献，而22%明确不鼓励使用AI。（2）51%的AI政策要求披露AI辅助的贡献；（3）74%的AI政策要求在贡献过程中有人类参与。总体而言，我们发现大多数被分析的AI政策对GenAI的使用持积极态度。然而，AI披露和人类参与是贡献过程中的基本要素。最后，我们通过讨论对开发者和研究者的启示来总结。

Original abstract: Generative AI (GenAI) has recently transformed software development. Due to the ease of generating code, open source projects are experiencing a growth in contributions. To address the rise of GenAI, open source projects have begun implementing policies for AI usage in contributions. However, the extent to which open source specifies whether AI-assisted contributions are allowed or prohibited, along with the best practices for contributors, remains unclear. This paper provides an initial empirical study to explore how open source projects are adapting to GenAI contributions. We analyzed 1,000 popular GitHub repositories and identified 118 AI policies for contributors. Our results show that (1) 78% of the AI policies allow AI-assisted contributions, while 22% explicitly discourage AI use. (2) 51% of the AI policies require the disclosure of AI-assisted contributions; and (3) 74% of the AI policies require a human in the loop during contribution. Overall, we find that the majority of the analyzed AI policies are positive regarding the usage of GenAI. However, AI disclosure and human in the loop are fundamental in the contribution process. Finally, we conclude by discussing implications for developers and researchers.

</details>

### [14] [X-SYNTH: Beyond Retrieval -- Enterprise Context Synthesis from Observed Digital Human Attention](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15505v2)
*Guruprasad Raghavan,George Nychis,Rohan Narayana Murthy*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 企业上下文合成框架，关注agent任务中的行为模式，可迁移至agent设计

TL;DR: 提出X-SYNTH框架，利用数字人类注意力（行为模式）替代传统检索，将企业上下文合成的真线索率从9.5%提升至61.9%，假线索率从90.5%降至18.8%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有检索方法在需要深层组织知识的代理任务中表现不佳（低真线索率、高假线索率），且缺乏改进机制，因为行为模式等关键信息未被索引。

Method: 基于数字人类注意力，为每个个体建模数字孪生签名（DTS），针对每个查询动态选择七种注意力过滤器之一，通过四阶段流水线生成基于行为模式的排名上下文。

Result: 在销售线索任务中，未辅助的前沿模型TLR为9.5%、FLR为90.5%；结合X-SYNTH后TLR升至61.9%（6.5倍），FLR降至18.8%。

Conclusion: 企业上下文合成本质是相关性而非检索问题，数字人类注意力是最可靠的客观事实来源。

中文摘要：在企业运营中，AI代理任务所需的上下文分散在记录系统、静态信息存储和通信渠道中。存储的是系统状态，是对实际发生工作的有损表示。主流方法是通过将请求内容与存储内容进行匹配来检索；对于狭窄的请求来说效果很好。但合成质量取决于知道要呈现什么以及如何解释：每个组织、团队和个体特有的知识，存在于行为模式中，但不存在于任何检索索引中。对于向销售人员提出具有企业价值的线索这一代理任务，这种方法行不通：真实线索率低，虚假线索率高，而且模型没有改进机制。我们提出了X-SYNTH，一个以数字人类注意力为基础的企业上下文合成框架，数字人类注意力是每个工作者可数字观察的交互特征，编码了他们做了什么、做事的顺序以及隐式奖励信号。正面结果之前的行为痕迹与未产生正面结果的行为痕迹是可以区分的，无需外部标注。X-SYNTH将每个个体的行为基线建模为数字孪生签名（DTS），并为每个个体和每个查询选择七种注意力过滤器（比例、反向、差分、循环、比较、顺序和集体）中的一种，以识别因果相关的活动签名。一个四阶段流水线组装基于行为模式而非查询嵌入的排名上下文。一个前沿模型未辅助时达到9.5%的真实线索率（TLR）和90.5%的虚假线索率（FLR）。结合X-SYNTH后，TLR提升至61.9%（提高6.5倍），而FLR下降至18.8%。企业上下文合成不是一个检索问题。它是一个相关性问题，而数字人类注意力是其最可靠的客观事实。

Original abstract: In enterprise operations, the context required for an AI agent task is scattered across systems of record, static information stores, and communication channels. What is stored is system state, a lossy representation of the work that actually happened. The prevailing approach retrieves by matching request content to what is stored; for narrow requests this works well. But synthesis quality depends on knowing what to surface and how to interpret it: knowledge specific to each organization, team, and individual, present in behavioral patterns, absent from any retrieval index. For the agentic task of proposing enterprise-valuable leads to sellers, this approach breaks down: True Lead Rate is low, False Lead Rate is high, and the model has no mechanism to improve. We present X-SYNTH, a framework for enterprise context synthesis grounded in digital human attention, the digitally observable interaction signatures of each worker, encoding what they did, the sequence in which they did it, and implicit reward signals. Behavioral traces preceding positive outcomes are distinguishable from those that did not, without external labeling. X-SYNTH models each individual's behavioral baseline as a Digital Twin Signature (DTS) and selects among seven attention filters, Proportional, Inverse, Differential, Recurrent, Comparative, Sequential, and Collective, per individual and per query, to identify causally relevant activity signatures. A four-stage pipeline assembles ranked context grounded in behavioral patterns rather than query embeddings. A frontier model unaided achieves 9.5% True Lead Rate (TLR) with 90.5% False Lead Rate (FLR). Augmented with X-SYNTH, TLR rises to 61.9% (6.5x) while FLR falls to 18.8%. Enterprise context synthesis is not a retrieval problem. It is a relevance problem, and digital human attention is its most reliable ground truth.

</details>


### [15] [CAPS: Cascaded Adaptive Pairwise Selection for Efficient Parallel Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15513v1)
*Fangzhou Lin,Shuo Xing,Peiran Li,Siyuan Yang,Qianwen Ge,Kazunori Yamada,Ziming Zhang,Haichong Zhang,Zhengzhong Tu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM并行推理效率优化，涉及代码基准，直接关联coding agent推理加速

TL;DR: 提出CAPS框架，通过非均匀分配验证器计算（证据轴和分布轴）在成对自验证中大幅降低计算成本，同时保持或提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 成对自验证是并行推理中有效的聚合方法，但现有方法对每个问题执行大量完整的成对比较，计算成本高昂且缺乏选择性，需要更高效的验证器计算分配策略。

Method: CAPS是一个纯推理框架，沿证据轴（自适应减少每个候选的读取量）和分布轴（自适应选择比较对）非均匀分配验证器计算，通过四阶段级联（含可选救援子程序）实现，并导出闭式令牌成本公式。

Result: 在4个模型和5个基准的20个测试套件上，CAPS在14个套件中优于领先的成对验证器，同时仅用其25.4%的验证器令牌（代码任务），并在所有20个套件上优于逐点自验证。

Conclusion: CAPS显著降低了成对验证的计算成本，同时保持或提升性能，并提供了基于部分证据准确性的可解释诊断工具，用于评估级联适用性。

中文摘要：并行推理，即生成器采样多个候选解并由聚合器选择最佳解，是大语言模型中测试时扩展最有效的方式之一，而成对自验证已成为其最强的聚合原语。然而，成对验证代价高昂：每次判断都要完整读取两个解，且现有方法对每个问题执行数十次此类判断，而不考虑比较是否有信息量。我们提出CAPS（级联自适应成对选择），这是一个纯推理框架，它沿着两个正交轴非均匀地分配验证器计算：证据轴自适应地调整评判者看到每个候选的多少，分布轴自适应地调整比较在候选池中的分布。CAPS将这些实例化为一个四阶段级联（带有可选的救援子程序），并得到一个闭式验证器令牌成本，其中每个候选的边际成本相对于均匀全证据调度大致减半。在四个自验证模型（Qwen3-14B、GPT-OSS-20B、Qwen3-4B-Instruct/Thinking）和涵盖代码（LiveCodeBench-v5/v6、CodeContests）和数学（AIME 2025、HMMT 2025）的五个推理基准上，CAPS在20个套件中的14个上优于领先的成对验证器，同时仅使用其验证器令牌预算的25.4%（在代码上），并在所有20个套件上优于逐点自验证。权衡套件在验证器部分证据与全证据的准确性方面提供了一个可解释的诊断，为级联适用性提供了具体的部署前检查。

Original abstract: Parallel reasoning, where a generator samples many candidate solutions and an aggregator selects the best, is one of the most effective forms of test-time scaling in large language models, and pairwise self-verification has become its strongest aggregation primitive. Yet pairwise verification carries a heavy cost: each judgment reads two complete solutions in full, and existing methods perform tens of such judgments per problem regardless of whether the comparison is informative. We introduce CAPS (Cascaded Adaptive Pairwise Selection), an inference-only framework that allocates verifier compute non-uniformly along two orthogonal axes: an evidence axis that adapts how much of each candidate the judge sees, and a distribution axis that adapts how comparisons are spread across the pool. CAPS instantiates these into a four-stage cascade with an optional rescue subroutine, and admits a closed-form verifier-token cost in which the per-candidate marginal cost is roughly halved relative to uniform full-evidence schedules. On four self-verifying models (Qwen3-14B, GPT-OSS-20B, Qwen3-4B-Instruct/Thinking) and five reasoning benchmarks spanning code (LiveCodeBench-v5/v6, CodeContests) and math (AIME 2025, HMMT 2025), CAPS outperforms the leading pairwise verifier on 14 of 20 suites while using 25.4% of its verifier-token budget on code, and outperforms pointwise self-verification on all 20. The trade-off suites admit an interpretable diagnostic in terms of the verifier's accuracy at partial versus full evidence, providing a concrete pre-deployment check for cascade suitability.

</details>


### [16] [RTL-BenchMT: Dynamic Maintenance of RTL Generation Benchmark Through Agent-Assisted Analysis and Revision](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15537v1)
*Jing Wang,Shang Liu,Hangan Zhou,Zhiyao Xie*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent框架自动维护RTL生成基准，直接涉及coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出RTL-BenchMT框架，自动识别和修复RTL基准测试中的缺陷与过拟合案例，降低人工维护成本并开源精炼基准套件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前RTL基准测试存在缺陷案例和过拟合问题，纯手工维护成本高且难以解决。

Method: 提出RTL-BenchMT自动化智能体框架，包含自动识别与修正缺陷案例、自动检测与更新过拟合案例两大功能。

Result: 生成精炼的基准测试套件，并开源给社区。

Conclusion: RTL-BenchMT能有效降低人工维护成本，提升RTL基准测试质量。

中文摘要：本文介绍了RTL-BenchMT，一个用于动态维护RTL生成基准测试的智能体框架。大型语言模型（LLM）辅助的自动RTL生成是EDA研究中最重要的方向之一。然而，当前的RTL基准测试面临两个关键挑战：（1）基准测试中存在缺陷的案例，（2）对基准测试的过拟合。这两个挑战仅靠人工工程努力难以解决。为了解决这些问题并系统性地降低人工维护成本，我们提出了一个自动化智能体框架RTL-BenchMT。RTL-BenchMT专注于两个关键应用：（1）自动识别和修正有缺陷的基准测试案例，（2）自动检测和更新过拟合案例。在RTL-BenchMT的帮助下，我们对缺陷案例和过拟合案例进行了深入的彻底分析，并生成了一个精炼的基准测试套件，该套件将开源给社区。

Original abstract: This paper introduces RTL-BenchMT, an agentic framework for dynamically maintaining RTL generation benchmarks. Large Language Models (LLMs) assisted automated RTL generation is one of the most important directions in EDA research. However, current RTL benchmarks face two critical challenges: (1) flawed cases in the benchmarks and (2) overfitting to the benchmarks. Both challenges are difficult to resolve purely by manual engineering effort. To address these issues and systematically reduce human maintenance costs, we propose an automated agentic framework, RTL-BenchMT. RTL-BenchMT focuses on two key applications: (1) automatically identifying and revising flawed benchmark cases and (2) automatically detecting and updating overfitting cases. With the assistance of RTL-BenchMT, we conduct a thorough, in-depth analysis of flawed and overfitting cases and produce a refined benchmark suite that will be open-sourced to the community.

### [17] [DRS-GUI: Dynamic Region Search for Training-Free GUI Grounding](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15542v1)
*Yichao Liu,Huawen Shen,Liu Yu,Shiyu Liu,Zeyu Chen,Yu Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 使用MCTS规划进行GUI元素搜索，可迁移至agent规划方法。

TL;DR: 提出DRS-GUI，一种无需训练的动态区域搜索框架，通过模拟人类感知动作和MCTS规划，提升MLLM在复杂GUI中的指令相关元素定位能力，在ScreenSpot-Pro上提升14%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MLLM从高分辨率截图中准确识别与指令相关的UI元素存在困难，受人类动态调整感知范围的启发，旨在设计一种无需训练且能提升接地性能的框架。

Method: 提出DRS-GUI，包含轻量级UI Perceptor执行三种感知动作（聚焦、移动、分散），基于MCTS的Action Planner动态调度动作，并通过区域质量奖励筛选高相关区域。

Result: 在ScreenSpot-Pro上，DRS-GUI为Qwen2.5-VL-7B和UGround-V1-7B等MLLM带来14%的性能提升，显著增强接地性能和泛化能力。

Conclusion: DRS-GUI作为一种无需训练的框架，能有效提升MLLM在复杂GUI场景中的指令相关元素定位能力，具有较好的泛化性和兼容性。

中文摘要：基于多模态大语言模型（MLLM）的图形用户界面代理在理解和执行用户指令方面展现出了令人印象深刻的能力。然而，从充满无关UI组件的高分辨率截图中准确识别与指令相关的元素，对于现有方法仍然是一个挑战。受人类在复杂屏幕上动态调整感知范围以定位任务相关区域的启发，我们提出了DRS-GUI，一种无需训练的动态区域搜索框架，用于GUI接地，可以无缝集成到现有的MLLM中。DRS-GUI引入了一个轻量级的UI感知器，执行三种类似人类的感知动作（聚焦、移动和分散），逐步探索界面并生成区域提议。为了动态调度这些动作，我们进一步设计了一个基于蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）的动作规划器。采用区域质量奖励来评估和选择与指令高度相关的区域，有效剪枝冗余的UI元素。实验表明，在ScreenSpot-Pro上，DRS-GUI为通用和GUI专用的MLLM（Qwen2.5-VL-7B和UGround-V1-7B）带来了14%的提升，显著增强了接地性能和泛化能力。

Original abstract: GUI agents powered by Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have demonstrated impressive capability in understanding and executing user instructions. However, accurately grounding instruction-relevant elements from high-resolution screenshots cluttered with irrelevant UI components remains challenging for existing approaches. Inspired by how humans dynamically adjust their perceptual scope to locate task-related regions on complex screens, we propose DRS-GUI, a training-free dynamic region search framework for GUI grounding that can be seamlessly integrated into existing MLLMs. DRS-GUI introduces a lightweight UI Perceptor that performs three human-like perceptual actions (Focus, Shift, and Scatter) to progressively explore the interface and generate region proposals. To dynamically schedule these actions, we further design an Action Planner based on Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS). A region quality reward is employed to evaluate and select the highly instruction-relevant region, efficiently pruning redundant UI elements. Experiments demonstrate that DRS-GUI yields a 14\% improvement on ScreenSpot-Pro for general and GUI-specific MLLMs (Qwen2.5-VL-7B and UGround-V1-7B), significantly enhancing grounding performance and generalization.

</details>


### [18] [Position: Artificial Intelligence Needs Meta Intelligence -- the Case for Metacognitive AI](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15567v1)
*Sergei Chuprov,Richard D. Lange,Leon Reznik,Paulo Shakarian,Raman Zatsarenko,Dmitrii Korobeinikov*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 元认知AI设计原则，可启发agent自我监控与资源分配。

TL;DR: 提出将元认知作为AI设计原则，通过自我监控和资源分配提升准确性、安全性和效率，并在联邦学习中验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI系统缺乏对自身认知过程的反思和资源自适应的能力，导致效率低下和安全隐患，元认知策略可借鉴人类认知机制来改善。

Method: 基于资源理性AI和心理学元认知策略，设计系统自我监控与资源分配机制，并开发软件框架支持实验。

Result: 在联邦学习案例中，元认知原则提升了学习效率、效果和安全性。

Conclusion: 元认知可作为通用设计原则，为构建更准确、安全、高效的AI提供可行路径，并开放了若干理论和技术挑战。

中文摘要：这篇立场论文主张将元认知作为通用设计原则，以创建更准确、更安全、更高效的AI。元认知解决方案涉及系统监控自身状态，并根据每个问题实例的难度或错误成本明智地分配资源。我们既从以往关于资源理性AI的工作中汲取灵感，也从心理学和认知科学中充分记录的元认知策略中汲取灵感，识别出将这些策略嵌入AI设计的具体挑战，并强调了开放的理论和实现问题。我们通过联邦学习案例研究中的具体实例展示了这些原则如何提高学习效率、效果和安全性。我们还展示了如何通过一个专为社区设计、部署和实验元认知驱动AI应用而开发的新型软件框架将这些原则转化为实践。

Original abstract: This position paper argues for metacognition as a general design principle for creating more accurate, secure, and efficient AI. The metacognitive solution involves systems monitoring their own states and judiciously allocating resources depending on each problem instance's difficulty or cost of mistakes. Drawing inspiration both from past work on resource-rational AI and from well-documented metacognitive strategies in psychology and cognitive science, we identify specific challenges in embedding these strategies into AI design and highlight open theoretical and implementation problems. We showcase these principles through a tangible example of improved learning efficiency, effectiveness, and security in a Federated Learning (FL) case study. We show how these principles can be translated into practice with a novel software framework developed specifically to allow the community to design, deploy, and experiment with metacognition-enabled AI applications.

### [19] [STAR: A Stage-attributed Triage and Repair framework for RCA Agents in Microservices](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15581v1)
*Junle Wang,Xingchuang Liao,Wenjun Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM-based RCA agent修复框架，涉及stage-wise审计与自我修复，直接相关agent可靠性。

TL;DR: STAR通过将RCA工作流分解为四个可定位的阶段，并采用阶段审计、快/慢路由和反事实评估等策略，有效修复错误轨迹，提升根因定位和故障分类的准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于LLM的RCA智能体在微服务诊断中具有潜力，但错误会在推理链中传播，导致诊断不可靠，现有方法缺乏对错误位置的显式建模和修复机制。

Method: 提出STAR框架，将RCA分解为证据包、假设集、分析结构和决策报告四个阶段；基于LangGraph实现阶段审计、预算感知快/慢路由、反事实候选评估定位故障阶段，并进行阶段特定补丁和重放修复。

Result: 在公开基准和真实数据集上，STAR在根因定位和故障分类上优于基线；高准确率识别故障阶段，多数错误轨迹在一到两轮修复内纠正，快/慢路由和反事实评估贡献显著。

Conclusion: 显式建模RCA智能体的故障阶段是构建可靠、可调试且自我修复的智能体RCA系统的有效路径。

中文摘要：基于LLM的根因分析（RCA）智能体最近作为微服务AIOps中事件诊断的一种有前景的范式出现。然而，它们的可靠性仍然脆弱：早期证据收集、假设形成或因果分析中的错误可能通过推理轨迹传播，并最终破坏最终诊断。在本文中，我们提出了STAR，一个用于修复错误RCA轨迹的《阶段归因分类与修复》框架。STAR将RCA工作流明确分解为四个结构化阶段，即证据包（EP）、假设集（HS）、分析结构（AS）和决策报告（DR），并将智能体故障视为可阶段定位的推理错误，而非整体端到端错误。基于LangGraph构建，STAR执行阶段级审计、预算感知的快/慢路由、通过反事实候选评估进行决定性阶段定位，以及阶段特定的补丁和重放修复。我们在一个公开的大规模基准和一个真实世界生产数据集上，使用两种RCA智能体工作流和三个基础模型对STAR进行了评估。实验结果表明，STAR在根因定位和故障类型分类上均持续优于强基线。此外，STAR以高准确率识别决定性故障阶段，在一到两轮重放内修复大多数初始错误的轨迹，并从快/慢路由和反事实阶段评估中显著受益。这些结果表明，显式建模RCA智能体在何处失败，是实现可靠、可调试且可自我修复的智能体RCA系统的有效途径。

Original abstract: LLM-based root cause analysis (RCA) agents have recently emerged as a promising paradigm for incident diagnosis in microservice AIOps. However, their reliability remains fragile: an error in early evidence collection, hypothesis formulation, or causal analysis can propagate through the reasoning trace and eventually corrupt the final diagnosis. In this paper, we present \textbf{STAR}, a \emph{Stage-attributed Triage and Repair} framework for repairing erroneous RCA traces. STAR explicitly decomposes an RCA workflow into four structured stages, namely \emph{Evidence Package} (EP), \emph{Hypothesis Set} (HS), \emph{Analysis Structure} (AS), and \emph{Decision Report} (DR), and treats agent failure as a stage-localizable reasoning bug rather than a monolithic end-to-end error. Built on top of LangGraph, STAR performs stage-wise auditing, budget-aware \emph{Fast/Slow Routing}, \emph{decisive stage localization via counterfactual candidate evaluation}, and stage-specific patch-and-replay repair.
  We evaluate STAR on a public large-scale benchmark and a real-world production dataset, using two RCA agent workflows and three foundation models. Experimental results show that STAR consistently improves both root cause localization and fault type classification over strong baselines. Moreover, STAR identifies the decisive faulty stage with high accuracy, repairs most initially incorrect traces within one or two replay rounds, and benefits substantially from both Fast/Slow Routing and counterfactual stage evaluation. These results suggest that explicitly modeling \emph{where} an RCA agent fails is an effective path toward reliable, debuggable, and self-repairing agentic RCA systems.

### [20] [See Before You Code: Learning Visual Priors for Spatially Aware Educational Animation Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15585v1)
*Yuejia Li,Ke He,Junheng Li,Shutong Chen,Jingkang Xia,Zhiyue Su,Junchi Zhang,Mang Ye*

TL;DR: 提出OmniManim框架，通过显式视觉规划解决教育动画生成中的渲染缺陷问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型生成教育动画代码时，渲染结果常有视觉缺陷，且无法从代码直接检测，需要渲染后反馈。

Method: 提出OmniManim框架，包含共享场景状态、显式视觉规划、结构化渲染后诊断和局部修复；视觉规划模块通过粗到精边界框去噪和插值感知优化生成关键帧布局。

Result: 在EduRequire-500上，OmniManim在渲染质量上优于基线方法。

Conclusion: 显式视觉规划是提升渲染质量的关键，特别是粗空间先验、边界框细化和插值感知优化。

中文摘要：大型语言模型可以为教育动画生成可执行代码，但生成的渲染结果常常表现出视觉缺陷，包括元素重叠、未对齐和动画连续性中断。这些缺陷仅凭代码无法可靠检测，只有在执行后才会显现。我们将此问题形式化为渲染反馈感知的约束代码生成：给定自然语言规范，模型必须生成可执行代码，其渲染输出需满足仅在渲染后才能评估的结构化质量标准。为了解决该问题，我们引入了OmniManim，一种基于共享场景状态、显式视觉规划、结构化渲染后诊断和局部修复的渲染反馈感知教育动画生成框架。在OmniManim中，视觉智能体是一个任务特定的视觉规划模块：它通过由粗到精的边界框去噪预测稀疏关键帧布局，并优化一个插值感知目标以减少由下游动画插值引起的中间帧失败。我们还构建了两个数据集ManimLayout-1K和EduRequire-500，并提供可复现的评估协议，涵盖可执行性、教学质量、视觉质量和效率。在EduRequire-500上，OmniManim在测量的渲染质量上优于单一模型基线和现有的多智能体框架。系统的消融研究进一步验证了显式视觉规划，特别是其粗空间先验、边界框细化和插值感知优化，是这些提升的核心。

Original abstract: Large language models can generate executable code for educational animations, but the resulting renders often exhibit visual defects, including element overlap, misalignment, and broken animation continuity. These defects cannot be reliably detected from the code alone and become apparent only after execution. We formalize this problem as render-feedback-aware constrained code generation: given a natural language specification, the model must generate executable code whose rendered output satisfies structured quality criteria that can be evaluated only after rendering. To address this problem, we introduce OmniManim, a render-feedback-aware educational animation generation framework built around a shared scene state, explicit visual planning, structured post-render diagnostics, and localized repair. Within OmniManim, the Vision Agent is a task-specific visual planning module: it predicts sparse keyframe layouts with coarse-to-fine bounding-box denoising and optimizes an interpolation-aware objective to reduce intermediate-frame failures induced by downstream animation interpolation. We further construct two datasets, ManimLayout-1K and EduRequire-500, and provide a reproducible evaluation protocol covering executability, instructional quality, visual quality, and efficiency. On EduRequire-500, OmniManim improves measured render quality over both single-model baselines and existing multi-agent frameworks. Systematic ablation studies further verify that explicit visual planning, especially its coarse spatial prior, bounding-box refinement, and interpolation-aware optimization, is central to these gains.

### [21] [TopoEvo: A Topology-Aware Self-Evolving Multi-Agent Framework for Root Cause Analysis in Microservices](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15611v1)
*Junle Wang,Xingchuang Liao,Wenjun Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent RCA框架，包含拓扑感知、多模态对齐和自演进机制，直接相关agent协作与推理。

TL;DR: TopoEvo是一个拓扑感知的自我进化多智能体框架，通过度量正交多模态对齐、向量量化离散化症状令牌和多智能体假设-证据-测试工作流，实现了准确的微服务根因分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微服务根因分析面临多模态可观测性噪声、级联故障放大和非平稳拓扑漂移的挑战，现有LLM方法拓扑无关且存在症状放大偏差。

Method: TopoEvo包含四个关键组件：度量正交多模态对齐（MOMA）减少模态冗余，向量量化（VQ）生成离散症状令牌，多智能体假设-证据-测试（HET）工作流验证传播一致解释，以及自我进化机制适应拓扑漂移。

Result: 实验表明TopoEvo在多个真实微服务场景下有效克服了症状放大偏差，准确识别根因并保持鲁棒性。

Conclusion: TopoEvo通过结合图表示学习和拓扑约束推理，显著提升了微服务根因分析的准确性和可解释性，并能适应动态环境。

中文摘要：微服务中的根因分析（RCA）面临挑战，原因是（i）嘈杂且异构的多模态可观测性（指标、日志、跟踪），（ii）级联故障传播放大下游症状，以及（iii）由自动缩放和滚动更新引起的非平稳拓扑漂移。最近的基于LLM的RCA代理可以生成基于工具的解释，但它们通常与拓扑无关，并遭受症状放大偏差，将根因误归因于显著的下游受害者。我们提出TopoEvo，一个拓扑感知的自我进化多智能体框架，将图表示学习与结构化的、拓扑约束的推理相结合。TopoEvo首先引入了度量正交多模态对齐（MOMA），它将度量嵌入分解为互补的子空间，并对比对齐日志和跟踪，以减少模态冗余和稀疏性，为图编码产生稳定的节点表示。然后它应用向量量化（VQ）将拓扑增强状态离散化为带有症状词典的可审计症状令牌，实现可靠的检索和令牌级证据基础。在这些离散拓扑线索之上，TopoEvo执行多智能体假设-证据-测试（HET）工作流，以显式验证传播一致的解释，并将初始异常与放大的下游症状分开。最后，自我进化机制刷新分层事件记忆，并执行保守的测试时适应，使用高置信度伪标签以在漂移下保持鲁棒性。

Original abstract: Root cause analysis (RCA) in microservices is challenging due to (i) noisy and heterogeneous multimodal observability (metrics, logs, traces), (ii) cascading failure propagation that amplifies downstream symptoms, and (iii) non-stationary topology drift induced by autoscaling and rolling updates. Recent LLM-based RCA agents can generate tool-grounded explanations, yet they often remain topology-agnostic and suffer from \emph{symptom-amplification bias}, misattributing the root cause to salient downstream victims. We propose \textbf{TopoEvo}, a topology-aware self-evolving multi-agent framework that couples graph representation learning with structured, topology-constrained reasoning. TopoEvo first introduces \emph{Metric-orthogonal Multimodal Alignment} (MOMA), which decomposes metric embeddings into complementary subspaces and contrastively aligns logs and traces to reduce modality redundancy and sparsity, yielding stable node representations for graph encoding. It then applies \emph{Vector Quantization} (VQ) to discretize topology-enhanced states into auditable \emph{symptom tokens} with a symptom lexicon, enabling reliable retrieval and token-level evidence grounding. On top of these discrete topology cues, TopoEvo performs a multi-agent \emph{Hypothesis--Evidence--Test} (HET) workflow to explicitly verify propagation-consistent explanations and separate initiating anomalies from amplified downstream symptoms. Finally, a \emph{Self-Evolving Mechanism} refreshes hierarchical incident memory and performs conservative test-time adaptation with high-confidence pseudo-labels to maintain robustness under drift.

</details>


### [22] [ColPackAgent: Agent-Skill-Guided Hard-Particle Monte Carlo Workflows for Colloidal Packing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15625v1)
*Lijie Ding,Changwoo Do*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出MCP工具和技能驱动的agent框架，可迁移至其他领域agent设计。

TL;DR: 提出了ColPackAgent框架，通过MCP服务器和代理技能实现自主胶体堆积模拟，使LLM能可靠执行科学工作流，而非仅描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用LLM代理缺乏专用模拟工具和工作流指令，倾向于描述而非可靠执行胶体堆积模拟工作流，因此需要一种框架来桥接这一差距。

Method: ColPackAgent通过MCP工具服务器暴露自定义colpack Python包（封装HOOMD-blue硬粒子蒙特卡洛），并利用编码了四阶段工作流合约的代理技能，支持交互式、端到端或程序驱动的模拟执行。

Result: 在多个胶体堆积示例（3D立方体、2D二元系统、2D硬球冻结）上成功演示；通过17个阶段特定提示在多个LLM上建立了性能基准。

Conclusion: 将领域Python包与MCP工具和可移植代理技能相结合，为将模拟工具包转变为代理辅助研究工作流提供了实用途径。

中文摘要：我们提出了ColPackAgent，一个通过模型上下文协议（MCP）工具服务器和代理技能自主运行胶体堆积蒙特卡洛模拟的代理框架，无论是作为独立代理还是集成到现有代理系统中。通过利用MCP服务器和代理技能，ColPackAgent执行胶体堆积模拟的结构化工作流程，这对相行为、自组装和材料设计研究至关重要。在没有专用模拟工具和工作流指令的情况下，通用大语言模型（LLM）代理倾向于描述此类工作流而非可靠地执行它们。MCP服务器暴露了一个自定义的colpack Python包，该包封装了HOOMD-blue硬粒子蒙特卡洛模拟，而技能则编码了一个四阶段工作流合约。ColPackAgent可以交互式地执行工作流（带人类反馈）、从端到端提示自主执行，或按照提供的程序文件进行自动研究。我们通过几个胶体堆积模拟示例展示了该系统在不同模式下的表现，例如3D立方体颗粒、2D圆盘和胶囊的二元系统，以及使用自动研究的2D硬球冻结转变。我们还使用17个阶段特定提示，在多个LLM模型上比较了该工作流的性能。该基准测试提供了不同模型在遵循设置、规划和分析工作流方面可靠性的阶段级检查。这些结果共同表明，将领域Python包与MCP工具和可移植代理技能相结合，为将模拟工具包转变为代理辅助的研究工作流提供了一条实用途径。

Original abstract: We introduce ColPackAgent, an agent framework that autonomously runs Monte Carlo simulations of colloidal packing through a Model Context Protocol (MCP) tool server and an agent skill, whether as a standalone agent or inside an existing agent system. By harnessing the MCP server and agent skill, ColPackAgent executes a structured workflow for colloidal packing simulations, which are central to studies of phase behavior, self-assembly, and materials design. Without dedicated simulation tools and workflow instructions, general-purpose Large Language Model (LLM) agents tend to describe such workflows rather than execute them reliably. The MCP server exposes a custom-built colpack Python package that wraps HOOMD-blue hard-particle Monte Carlo, and the skill encodes a four-stage workflow contract. ColPackAgent can carry out the workflow interactively with human feedback, autonomously from an end-to-end prompt, or as autoresearch following a provided program file. We demonstrate the system in different modes with several colloidal packing simulation examples such as cube particles in 3D, a binary system of disks and capsules in 2D, and the 2D hard-disk freezing transition using autoresearch. We also compare model performance on this workflow across a panel of LLMs with 17 stage-specific prompts. This benchmark provides a stage-level check of how reliably different models follow the setup, planning, and analysis workflow. Together, these results show that pairing a domain Python package with MCP tools and a portable agent skill provides a practical route for turning a simulation toolkit into an agent-assisted research workflow.

### [23] [PRISM: Prompt Reliability via Iterative Simulation and Monitoring for Enterprise Conversational AI](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15665v1)
*Keshava Chaitanya,Jahnavi Gundakaram*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM对话agent的持续可靠性优化，方法可迁移至coding agent的prompt测试与修复。

TL;DR: PRISM是一个通过迭代模拟和监控来持续优化提示词可靠性的闭环框架，显著缩短提示词编写时间并提高生产可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有提示词优化框架仅将提示词质量视为一次性编译问题，无法检测和修复由LLM行为漂移引起的提示词回归，导致生产环境中的可靠性隐患。

Method: PRISM以自然语言需求、工具和记忆变量、初始提示词为输入，自动生成测试用例，在平台忠实环境中模拟多轮对话，使用LLM评判通过/失败，诊断失败根因并精确修复提示词，每日迭代运行。

Result: 在35个企业代理上评估，中位提示词编写时间从2天降至30分钟以内，生产可靠性达99%，能在24小时内检测并修复由LLM行为漂移引起的回归。

Conclusion: 持续的、模拟驱动的提示词优化对于实现大规模可靠的企业对话AI既是可行的，也是必要的。

中文摘要：在企业环境中部署由大型语言模型（LLM）驱动的对话代理需要提示词在启动时正确且能够承受生产环境中LLM的非确定性行为漂移。现有的提示词优化框架将提示词质量视为一次性编译问题，忽略了如何检测和修复由LLM行为静默变化引起的提示词回归这一同样关键的问题。我们提出PRISM（通过迭代模拟和监控实现提示词可靠性），这是一个闭环框架，将提示词工程视为持续的可靠性工程问题，而非一次性编写任务。PRISM输入包括自然语言描述的代理需求、一组配置的工具和记忆变量，以及初始提示词草稿。它自动从需求生成测试用例，在忠实于平台的LLM环境中模拟完整的多轮对话，使用LLM作为评判者评估通过/失败，诊断失败的根本原因，并精确修复提示词——迭代直到所有测试通过。关键的是，PRISM设计为定期运行（每日），将LLM行为漂移视为首要可靠性问题。我们在Yellow.ai V3平台上对35个企业对话代理进行了为期三周的部署评估。PRISM将提示词编写的中位时间从2天缩短至30分钟以下，在所有评估的代理中达到99%的生产可靠性，并在24小时检测窗口内成功识别并修复由LLM行为漂移引起的生产回归。我们的结果表明，持续的、模拟驱动的提示词优化对于大规模可靠的企业对话AI既是可行的，也是必要的。

Original abstract: Deploying large language model (LLM)-driven conversational agents in enterprise settings requires prompts that are simultaneously correct at launch and resilient to the non-deterministic behavioral drift that characterizes production LLM deployments. Existing prompt optimization frameworks address prompt quality as a one-time compile-time problem, leaving open the equally critical question of how to detect and repair prompt regressions caused by silent LLM behavior changes over time. We present PRISM (Prompt Reliability via Iterative Simulation and Monitoring), a closed-loop framework that treats prompt engineering as a continuous reliability engineering problem rather than a one-time authorship task. PRISM takes as input plain-language agent requirements, a set of configured tools and memory variables, and an initial draft prompt. It automatically generates test cases from requirements, simulates full multi-turn conversations against a platform-faithful LLM environment, evaluates pass/fail using an LLM-as-judge, diagnoses root causes of failures, and surgically repairs the prompt -- iterating until all tests pass. Critically, PRISM is designed to run on a scheduled basis (daily), treating LLM behavioral drift as a first-class reliability concern. We evaluate PRISM across 35 enterprise conversational agents over a three-week deployment period on the Yellow.ai V3 platform. PRISM reduces median prompt authoring time from 2 days to under 30 minutes, achieves 99% production reliability across all evaluated agents, and successfully identifies and repairs production regressions caused by LLM behavioral drift within a 24-hour detection window. Our results suggest that continuous, simulation-driven prompt optimization is both tractable and necessary for reliable enterprise conversational AI at scale.

</details>


### [24] [ALSO: Adversarial Online Strategy Optimization for Social Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15768v2)
*Xiang Li,Liping Yi,Mingze Kong,Min Zhang,Zhongxiang Dai,QingHua Hu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 在线策略优化用于社交agent，涉及非平稳环境下的LLM agent在线学习，可迁移至agent优化。

TL;DR: 提出ALSO框架，将多智能体社会模拟中的在线策略优化建模为对抗性赌博机问题，通过轻量级神经替代模型预测奖励，实现动态环境下的有效适应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM社会智能体依赖静态人格，而离线强化学习和外部规划器不适用于非平稳环境，需要动态调整策略。

Method: 将多轮交互建模为对抗性赌博机问题，将静态人格和动态策略指令组合视为臂；引入轻量级神经替代模型预测奖励，实现样本高效探索。

Result: 在Sotopia基准上，ALSO优于静态基线和现有优化方法。

Conclusion: 验证了对抗性在线策略优化在构建鲁棒社会智能体方面的有效性。

中文摘要：社会模拟为研究社会智能提供了一个引人注目的测试平台，其中智能体通过多轮对话在变化的情境和策略性适应的对手下进行交互。这类环境本质上是非平稳的，要求智能体随时间动态调整其策略。然而，大多数基于大语言模型（LLM）的社会智能体依赖静态人格，而现有增强社会智能的方法（如离线强化学习或外部规划器）不适合这些设置，通常假设平稳性并产生大量训练开销。为了弥补这一差距，我们提出 ALSO（对抗性在线策略优化），这是多智能体社会模拟中首个在线策略优化框架。ALSO通过两个关键贡献推进社会适应。（1）ALSO将多轮交互建模为对抗性赌博机问题，其中静态人格和动态策略指令的组合被视为臂，为非平稳性提供了原则性解决方案，而无需依赖环境稳定性假设。（2）为了预测奖励并在多轮对话中泛化稀疏反馈，ALSO引入了一个轻量级神经替代模型，从交互历史中预测奖励，从而实现样本高效的探索和持续的在线适应。在Sotopia基准上的实验表明，ALSO在动态环境中始终优于静态基线和现有优化方法，验证了对抗性在线策略优化在构建鲁棒社会智能体方面的有效性。

Original abstract: Social simulation provides a compelling testbed for studying social intelligence, where agents interact through multi-turn dialogues under evolving contexts and strategically adapting opponents. Such environments are inherently non-stationary, requiring agents to dynamically adjust their strategies over time. However, most Large Language Model (LLM) based social agents rely on static personas, while existing approaches for enhancing social intelligence, such as offline reinforcement learning or external planners, are ill-suited to these settings, typically assuming stationarity and incurring substantial training overhead. To bridge this gap, we propose \textbf{ALSO} (\textbf{A}dversarial on\textbf{L}ine \textbf{S}trategy \textbf{O}ptimization), the first framework for online strategy optimization in multi-agent social simulation. ALSO advances social adaptation through two key contributions. (1) ALSO formulates multi-turn interaction as an adversarial bandit problem, where combinations of static personas and dynamic strategy instructions are treated as arms, providing a principled solution to non-stationarity without relying on environmental stability assumptions. (2) To predict rewards and generalize sparse feedback in multi-turn dialogues, ALSO introduces a lightweight neural surrogate to predict rewards from interaction histories, enabling sample-efficient exploration and continuous online adaptation. Experiments on the Sotopia benchmark demonstrate that ALSO consistently outperforms static baselines and existing optimization methods in dynamic environments, validating the effectiveness of adversarial online strategy optimization for building robust social agents.

### [25] [SaaS-Bench: Can Computer-Use Agents Leverage Real-World SaaS to Solve Professional Workflows?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15777v2)
*Kean Shi,Zihang Li,Tianyi Ma,Zengji Tu,Jialong Wu,Xinbo Xu,Qingyao Yang,Ruoyu Wu,Weichu Xie,Ming Wu,Jason Zeng,Michael Heinrich,Elvis Zhang,Liang Chen,Kuan Li,Baobao Chang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 计算机使用agent benchmark，评估真实SaaS工作流，直接涉及长程任务和规划，对agent评测有价值。

TL;DR: SaaS-Bench是一个基于真实SaaS系统的基准，包含106个长时任务，用于评估计算机使用代理。实验显示最强LLM代理端到端完成率低于4%，在规划、状态跟踪等方面存在严重局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建了23个可部署的SaaS系统（6个专业领域），设计106个基于真实工作场景的任务，采用加权验证检查点评估严格完成和部分进展，支持纯文本和多模态输入。

Result: 代表性LLM代理（包括最强模型）端到端任务完成率低于4%，在规划、状态跟踪、跨应用上下文维护和错误恢复方面表现不足。

Conclusion: 当前LLM代理在真实SaaS环境中能力严重不足，需要改进规划、状态管理和错误恢复等能力以应对复杂工作流。

中文摘要：计算机使用代理（CUA）正在迅速将大型语言模型（LLM）从基于文本的推理扩展到更复杂环境中的动作执行，例如网页浏览器和图形用户界面（GUI）。然而，现有的网页和GUI代理基准通常依赖简化设置、孤立任务或短时交互，这使得难以评估代理在真实专业工作流程中的能力。软件即服务（SaaS）环境是CUA评估的自然选择，因为它们承载了现代数字工作的很大一部分，并且天然涉及动态系统状态、跨应用协调、领域特定知识和长时依赖。为此，我们提出了SaaS-Bench，这是一个基于23个可部署SaaS系统构建的基准，涵盖六个专业领域，包含106个基于真实工作场景的任务。这些任务需要长时执行，涵盖纯文本和多模态设置，并通过加权验证检查点进行评估，这些检查点衡量严格的任务完成和部分进展。实验表明，代表性的基于LLM的代理在SaaS-Bench上表现困难，即使是最强的模型端到端完成的任务也不到4%，这暴露了在规划、状态跟踪、跨应用上下文维护和错误恢复方面的局限性。代码可在https://github.com/UniPat-AI/SaaS-Bench获取以进行复现。

Original abstract: Computer-Using Agents (CUAs) are rapidly extending large language models (LLMs) beyond text-based reasoning toward action execution in more complex environments, such as web browsers and graphical user interfaces (GUIs). However, existing web and GUI agent benchmarks often rely on simplified settings, isolated tasks, or short-horizon interactions, making it difficult to assess capabilities of agents in realistic professional workflows. Software-as-a-Service (SaaS) environments are a natural choice for CUA evaluation, as they host a large share of modern digital work and naturally involve dynamic system states, cross-application coordination, domain-specific knowledge, and long-horizon dependencies. To this end, we introduce SaaS-Bench, a benchmark built on 23 deployable SaaS systems across six professional domains, containing 106 tasks grounded in realistic work scenarios. These tasks require long-horizon execution, cover both text-only and multimodal settings, and are evaluated with weighted verification checkpoints that measure strict task completion and partial progress. Experiments show that representative LLM-based agents struggle on SaaS-Bench, with even the strongest model completing fewer than 4% of tasks end-to-end, exposing limitations in planning, state tracking, cross-application context maintenance, and error recovery. Code are available at https://github.com/UniPat-AI/SaaS-Bench for reproduction.

### [26] [Agentic Discovery of Neural Architectures: AIRA-Compose and AIRA-Design](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15871v1)
*Alberto Pepe,Chien-Yu Lin,Despoina Magka,Bilge Acun,Yannan Nellie Wu,Anton Protopopov,Carole-Jean Wu,Yoram Bachrach*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM agent自主设计神经网络架构，体现自我改进与工具使用，对agent设计有启发。

TL;DR: 提出AIRA双框架，让LLM代理自主搜索和设计神经网络架构，发现比人工设计更优的Transformer和混合模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索LLM代理自主设计基础模型的能力，推动递归自我改进。

Method: 提出AIRA-Compose（高层架构搜索）和AIRA-Design（低层机制实现）双框架，分别使用11个和20个代理。

Result: 发现的14种架构在预训练后优于Llama 3.2等基线，缩放效率更高；注意力机制接近SOTA。

Conclusion: AI代理能自主发现匹配或超越人工设计的架构，为递归自我改进奠定基础。

中文摘要：为了实现递归自我改进，我们研究LLM代理自主设计超越标准Transformer的基础模型。我们引入了一种双框架方法：AIRA-Compose用于高层架构搜索，AIRA-Design用于低层机制实现。AIRA-Compose使用11个代理在24小时预算内探索基本计算原语。代理评估百万参数候选，将顶级设计外推到3.5亿、10亿和30亿规模。这产生了两个家族的14种架构：AIRAformers（基于Transformer）和AIRAhybrids（Transformer-Mamba）。在10亿规模预训练后，这些架构持续优于Llama 3.2和Composer发现的基线。在下游任务中，AIRAformer-D和AIRAhybrid-D相对于Llama 3.2准确率分别提高了2.4%和3.8%。此外，AIRA-Compose发现了具有高效缩放前沿的模型：AIRAformer-C缩放速度比Llama 3.2和Composer的最佳Transformer分别快54%和71%，而AIRAhybrid-C的缩放速度比Nemotron-2快23%，比Composer的最佳混合模型快37%。AIRA-Design分配了20个代理来编写用于长程依赖的新型注意力机制和高性能训练脚本。在Long Range Arena基准测试中，代理设计的架构在文档匹配和文本分类任务上分别达到人类最先进水平的2.3%和2.6%以内。在Autoresearch基准测试中，Greedy Opus 4.5在固定时间预算下达到0.968验证字节每比特，超过了已发表的最小值。这些框架共同表明，AI代理可以自主发现匹配或超越手工设计基线的架构和算法优化。这为发现下一代基础模型建立了一个强大的范式，标志着向递归自我改进迈出了明确的一步。

Original abstract: Toward recursive self-improvement, we investigate LLM agents autonomously designing foundation models beyond standard Transformers. We introduce a dual-framework approach: AIRA-Compose for high-level architecture search, and AIRA-Design for low-level mechanistic implementation. AIRA-Compose uses 11 agents to explore fundamental computational primitives under a 24-hour budget. Agents evaluate million-parameter candidates, extrapolating top designs to 350M, 1B, and 3B scales. This yields 14 architectures across two families: AIRAformers (Transformer-based) and AIRAhybrids (Transformer-Mamba). Pre-trained at 1B scale, these consistently outperform Llama 3.2 and Composer-found baselines. On downstream tasks, AIRAformer-D and AIRAhybrid-D improve accuracy by 2.4% and 3.8% over Llama 3.2. Furthermore, AIRA-Compose finds models with highly efficient scaling frontiers: AIRAformer-C scales 54% and 71% faster than Llama 3.2 and Composer's best Transformer, while AIRAhybrid-C outscales Nemotron-2 by 23% and Composer's best hybrid by 37%. AIRA-Design tasks 20 agents with writing novel attention mechanisms for long-range dependencies and high-performing training scripts. On the Long Range Arena benchmark, agent-designed architectures reach within 2.3% and 2.6% of human state-of-the-art on document matching and text classification. On the Autoresearch benchmark, Greedy Opus 4.5 achieves 0.968 validation bits-per-byte under a fixed time budget, surpassing the published minimum. Together, these frameworks show AI agents can autonomously discover architectures and algorithmic optimizations matching or surpassing hand-designed baselines. This establishes a powerful paradigm for discovering next-generation foundation models, marking a clear step toward recursive self-improvement.

### [27] [Imperfect World Models are Exploitable](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15960v2)
*Logan Mondal Bhamidipaty,Esmeralda S. Whitammer,David Abel,Mykel J. Kochenderfer,Subramanian Ramamoorthy*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究世界模型的可利用性，对agent安全与规划有启发。

TL;DR: 本文提出了模型利用的定义，证明了在大策略集上利用不可避免，并引入宽松概念和安全视界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于奖励黑客行为的不可避免性证明不适用于模型利用，需要建立形式桥梁。

Method: 通过类比奖励黑客行为，发展通用理论，引入宽松利用概念，推导安全视界。

Result: 证明了大策略集上利用不可避免，且有限集上不可黑客条件无法阻止利用。

Conclusion: 建立了奖励黑客与模型利用的形式桥梁，阐明了世界模型安全规划的极限。

中文摘要：我们在强化学习中提出了一种新的模型利用定义。非正式地说，如果一个世界模型暗示某个策略应被严格偏好于另一个，而环境的真实转移模型则暗示相反，那么该世界模型就是可被利用的。我们将我们的定义与先前对奖励黑客行为的刻画进行类比，但展示了相关的不可避免性证明并不适用于利用。为了克服这一障碍，我们发展了一个关于奖励黑客行为和模型利用的通用理论，证明了在大策略集上利用本质上是不可避免的，并得出黑客行为作为特例的相应结论。不幸的是，我们还发现，保证有限策略集中不可黑客性的条件并没有相应的条件来阻止利用。因此，我们引入了一个宽松的利用概念，并推导了一个可以避免利用的安全视界。综合起来，我们的结果在奖励黑客行为和模型利用之间建立了一座形式桥梁，并阐明了在世界模型中安全规划的极限。

Original abstract: We propose a novel definition of model exploitation in reinforcement learning. Informally, a world model is exploitable if it implies that one policy should be strictly preferred over another while the environment's true transition model implies the reverse. We analogize our definition with a prior characterization of reward hacking but show that the associated proof of inevitability does not transfer to exploitation. To overcome this obstruction, we develop a general theory of reward hacking and model exploitation that proves that exploitation is essentially unavoidable on large policy sets and yields the corresponding claim for hacking as a special case. Unfortunately, we also find that the conditions that guarantee unhackability in finite policy sets have no counterpart that precludes exploitation. Consequently, we introduce a relaxed notion of exploitation and derive a safe horizon within which it can be avoided. Taken together, our results establish a formal bridge between reward hacking and model exploitation and elucidate the limits of safe planning in world models.

</details>


### [28] [PAGER: Bridging the Semantic-Execution Gap in Point-Precise Geometric GUI Control](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15963v1)
*Jingxuan Wei,Xi Bai,Shan Liu,Caijun Jia,Zheng Sun,Xinglong Xu,Siyuan Li,Linzhuang Sun,Bihui Yu,Conghui He,Cheng Tan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: GUI agent，提出拓扑感知规划和像素级执行，直接相关coding agent。

TL;DR: 本文识别了精确敏感GUI任务，提出PAGE Bench基准和PAGER代理，通过依赖结构规划和像素级执行，缩小了语义-执行差距，实现点精确GUI控制的SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GUI代理依赖宽容区域范式，在精确几何构建中微小误差导致级联故障，缺乏点级精度和误差传播鲁棒性。

Method: 提出PAGER：拓扑感知代理，分解为依赖结构规划和像素级执行；采用像素级监督微调建立可执行语法，精确对齐强化学习（状态条件几何反馈）缓解暴露偏差。

Result: PAGER在PAGE Bench上任务成功率比最强通用基线高4.1倍，步骤成功率从<9%提升至>62%。

Conclusion: PAGER有效解决精确敏感GUI任务中的语义-执行差距，达到点精确GUI控制的最优性能。

中文摘要：大型视觉语言模型显著推进了GUI代理，使得在Web、移动和桌面界面上的可执行交互成为可能。然而这些进展很大程度上依赖于一种宽容的区域范式，其中同一组件内的许多邻近像素仍然有效。精确几何构建打破了这一假设：操作必须落在连续画布空间上的点，而不是宽容区域。由于几何基元具有本体依赖性，局部坐标误差可能导致级联的拓扑故障，扭曲下游对象并使最终构建无效。我们将此机制识别为精确敏感的GUI任务，需要点级精度、几何感知验证以及对依赖驱动的误差传播的鲁棒性。为了对其进行基准测试，我们引入了PAGE Bench，包含4,906个问题和超过224K个过程监督的像素级GUI操作。我们进一步提出了PAGER，一个拓扑感知的代理，将构建分解为依赖结构规划和像素级执行。像素级监督微调建立了可执行的操作语法，而精确对齐的强化学习通过状态条件的几何反馈缓解了展开引起的暴露偏差。实验揭示了一个显著的语义-执行差距：通用多模态模型可以超过88%的动作类型准确率，但任务成功率低于6%。PAGER缩小了这一差距，与最强的评估通用基线相比，任务成功率提高了4.1倍，并将GUI专业代理的步骤成功率从低于9%提高到超过62%，为精确点GUI控制建立了新的最先进水平。

Original abstract: Large vision-language models have significantly advanced GUI agents, enabling executable interaction across web, mobile, and desktop interfaces. Yet these gains largely rely on a forgiving region-tolerant paradigm, where many nearby pixels inside the same component remain valid. Precise geometric construction breaks this assumption: actions must land on points in continuous canvas space rather than tolerant regions. Because geometric primitives carry ontological dependencies, a local coordinate error can induce cascading topological failures that distort downstream objects and invalidate the final construction. We identify this regime as precision-sensitive GUI tasks, requiring point-level accuracy, geometry-aware verification, and robustness to dependency-driven error propagation. To benchmark it, we introduce PAGE Bench, with 4,906 problems and over 224K process-supervised, pixel-level GUI actions. We further propose PAGER, a topology-aware agent that decomposes construction into dependency-structured planning and pixel-level execution. Pixel-grounded supervised tuning establishes executable action grammar, while precision-aligned reinforcement learning mitigates rollout-induced exposure bias through state-conditioned geometric feedback. Experiments reveal a pronounced Semantic-Execution Gap: general multimodal models can exceed 88% action type accuracy yet remain below 6% task success. PAGER closes this gap, delivering 4.1x higher task success than the strongest evaluated general baseline and raising step success rate from below 9% for GUI-specialized agents to over 62%, establishing a new state of the art for point-precise GUI control.

</details>

Original abstract: We study event-graph substrates: a class of world models that represent agent state as an append-only log of typed RDF triples and answer counterfactual queries by forking the log under a structured intervention vocabulary. Substrates are inspectable at the triple level, support exact counterfactuals, and transfer across domains without learned components. We formalize the class, prove a duality between explanatory and counterfactual queries that reduces both to the same causal-ancestor traversal, and evaluate a 1,400-line CLEVRER-DSL interpreter atop a domain-agnostic substrate runtime at full CLEVRER validation scale (n=75,618). The substrate exceeds the NS-DR symbolic oracle on all four per-question categories (by 9.89, 20.26, 17.65, and 0.80 percentage points), and exceeds the parametric ALOE baseline on descriptive and explanatory while lagging on predictive and counterfactual. We also introduce twin-EventLog, a 500-specification Park-canonical Smallville counterfactual benchmark on which the substrate exceeds Llama-3.1-8B with full context by 18.80 points joint accuracy.

### [30] [Learning Bilevel Policies over Symbolic World Models for Long-Horizon Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15975v2)
*Dillon Z. Chen,Till Hofmann,Toryn Q. Klassen,Sheila A. McIlraith*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 双层级策略与符号世界模型用于长程规划，通用agent方法。

TL;DR: 提出BISON系统，通过结合低级模仿学习和高级符号抽象的双层策略，实现高效的长时域规划，在MetaWorld基准上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模仿学习难以生成长时域计划，而符号抽象擅长长时域规划，因此结合两者以构建能可靠解决长时域问题的具身AI代理。

Method: 采用双层策略$(π^{\mathrm{hl}}, π^{\mathrm{ll}})$：$π^{\mathrm{ll}}$从低级示范中学习神经策略，$π^{\mathrm{hl}}$从低级示范的符号抽象结合归纳泛化构建符号策略，并在BISON系统中实现。

Result: 在扩展MetaWorld基准上，BISON在泛化到更长时域和更多物体的问题上优于VLA和端到端方法，训练和推理更高效；忽略低级执行时，高级策略可在1分钟内解决含10,000个物体的高级问题。

Conclusion: BISON通过双层策略有效结合低级模仿学习和高级符号抽象，显著提升了长时域规划的性能和效率。

中文摘要：我们应对构建能够可靠解决长时域规划问题的具身AI代理的挑战。从示范中模仿学习在训练机器人解决需要精细运动控制和低级（LL）连续环境操作的各种复杂任务方面已显示出有效性。然而，仅通过模仿学习生成长期规划仍然是一项困难的工作。相比之下，高级（HL）符号抽象促进了高效且可解释的长期规划。我们提出结合LL模仿学习在操作和控制方面的优势，以及HL符号抽象在长期规划方面的优势。我们通过双层策略($π^{\mathrm{hl}}, π^{\mathrm{ll}}$)实现这一想法，该策略由从LL示范中学习的神经策略$π^{\mathrm{ll}}$和从LL示范的符号抽象结合归纳泛化构建的HL符号策略$π^{\mathrm{hl}}$组成。我们在BISON系统中实现了这些想法。在扩展的MetaWorld基准上的实验表明，BISON能够泛化到比VLA和端到端方法更长的时域和更多物体的问题，并且在训练和推理中具有更高的时间和内存效率。值得注意的是，当忽略LL执行时，BISON的HL策略可以在不到一分钟内解决包含10,000个相关物体的HL问题。项目页面：https://dillonzchen.github.io/bison

Original abstract: We tackle the challenge of building embodied AI agents that can reliably solve long-horizon planning problems. Imitation learning from demonstrations has shown itself to be effective in training robots to solve a diversity of complex tasks requiring fine motor control and manipulation over low-level (LL), continuous environments. Yet, it remains a difficult endeavour to generate long-horizon plans from imitation learning alone. In contrast, high-level (HL), symbolic abstractions facilitate efficient and interpretable long-horizon planning. We propose to combine the strengths of LL imitation learning for manipulation and control, and HL symbolic abstractions for long-horizon planning. We realise this idea via \emph{bilevel policies} of the form $(π^{\mathrm{hl}}, π^{\mathrm{ll}})$, consisting of a neural policy $π^{\mathrm{ll}}$ learned from LL demonstrations, and an HL symbolic policy $π^{\mathrm{hl}}$ that is constructed from symbolic abstractions of the LL demonstrations combined with inductive generalisation. We implement these ideas in the BISON system. Experiments on extended MetaWorld benchmarks demonstrate that BISON generalises to long horizons and problems with greater numbers of objects than those solved by VLA and end-to-end methods, and is more time and memory efficient in training and inference. Notably, when ignoring LL execution, BISON's HL policies can solve HL problems with 10,000 relevant objects in under a minute. Project page: https://dillonzchen.github.io/bison
