### [31] [ScreenSearch: Uncertainty-Aware OS Exploration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16024v1)
*Michael Solodko,Justin Wagle*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 不确定性感知桌面探索，类似agent探索与规划方法。

TL;DR: ScreenSearch通过结合结构屏幕检索与模糊感知图赌博机，实现了大规模桌面GUI探索，揭示了新颖性与模糊性之间的权衡，并强调了状态身份、提案质量和模糊感知搜索的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 桌面GUI代理面临部分可观测性问题：相似屏幕可能对应不同状态，局部合理动作导致不同结果。需要同时扩展可达前沿和减少歧义。

Method: 提出ScreenSearch，包含结构屏幕检索与去重层（将UIA树转为位置感知特征，稀疏索引与元数据过滤）以及模糊感知PUCT图赌博机（基于匹配动作结果分散性定义模糊信号，与前沿奖励结合驱动探索）。

Result: 在11个桌面应用中收集超100万张截图和3万去重状态，发现存在新颖性-模糊性权衡，且更强的提案先验能提升唯一状态发现。

Conclusion: 有效探索需要兼顾状态身份、提案质量和模糊感知搜索，单纯减少模糊性不足以作为目标。

中文摘要：桌面GUI代理在部分可观测性下运行：视觉上相似的屏幕可能对应于不同的底层工作流状态，因此局部合理的操作可能导致截然不同的结果。我们将其视为计算机/操作系统状态探索问题，其中有效行为需要同时扩展可达前沿并在承诺之前减少模糊性。我们提出ScreenSearch，一个结合结构屏幕检索与去重以及模糊感知PUCT图赌博机的系统，用于大规模桌面探索。检索层将UIA树转换为位置感知的结构特征，通过稀疏令牌搜索和元数据过滤器索引相关屏幕，并在虚拟机工作节点之间维护共享的去重状态图。在此图之上，我们基于匹配动作结果分散性定义了一个可扩展的模糊信号。如果相似屏幕在相同动作签名下产生不同下一状态，则应进一步探测该状态，而非将其视为已解决。我们利用此信号与前沿奖励一起驱动大规模探索和共享图上的重放起始策略评估。在11个桌面应用中，ScreenSearch收集了超过100万张截图和超过3万个去重状态，产生了具有显著跨应用和应用内多样性的探索语料库。在固定的重放起始切片上，我们观察到明显的新颖性-模糊性权衡：某些策略快速减少模糊性但发现少量前沿。因此，仅减少模糊性不足以作为探索目标。附录消融实验表明，更强的提案先验可以在语料库构建期间显著改善唯一状态发现。这些结果表明，在决定何时探测与何时提交时，状态身份、提案质量和模糊感知搜索都很重要。

Original abstract: Desktop GUI agents operate under partial observability: visually similar screens can correspond to different underlying workflow states, so locally plausible actions can lead to sharply different outcomes. We frame this as a problem of computer/OS state exploration, where effective behavior requires both expanding the reachable frontier and reducing ambiguity before committing. We present ScreenSearch, a system that combines structural screen retrieval and deduplication with an ambiguity-aware PUCT graph-bandit for large-scale desktop exploration. The retrieval layer converts UIA trees into location-aware structural features, indexes related screens through sparse token search and metadata filters, and maintains a shared deduplicated state graph across VM workers. On top of this graph, we define a scalable ambiguity signal based on matched-action outcome dispersion. If similar screens produce different next states under the same action signature, the state should be probed further rather than treated as resolved. We use this signal together with frontier rewards to drive large-scale exploration and replay-start policy evaluation over the shared graph. Across 11 desktop applications, ScreenSearch collects over 1M screenshots and over 30K deduplicated states, yielding large exploration corpora with substantial cross-application and within-application diversity. On a fixed replay-start slice, we observe a clear novelty--ambiguity trade-off: some policies reduce ambiguity quickly while discovering little frontier. Ambiguity reduction alone is therefore not a sufficient exploration objective. Appendix ablations show that stronger proposal priors can materially improve unique-state discovery during corpus building. These results suggest that state identity, proposal quality, and ambiguity-aware search all matter when deciding when to probe and when to commit.

### [32] [Sign-Separated Asymmetric Finite-Time Error Analysis of Q-Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16103v2)
*Donghwan Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: Q-learning误差理论分析，对agent训练算法有理论启发，但非直接方法。

TL;DR: 研究了Q-learning中过估计偏差导致的正负误差非对称收敛，证明了正分量收敛慢于负分量，从而间接证实过估计偏差的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Q-learning的过估计偏差会损害学习性能，但现有收敛理论未能明确解释该机制，因此需要理论分析来揭示其非对称影响。

Method: 将Q-learning误差分解为正负分量，推导各自的有限时间收敛速率，并利用切换系统动力学分析步长界限。

Result: 正分量收敛速率指数包络慢于负分量，存在速率分离；构造实例显示实际轨迹中也出现该不对称性。

Conclusion: 文章从理论上证明过估计偏差会导致正负误差的非对称收敛，为理解Q-learning行为提供了新视角。

中文摘要：已知Q-learning会受到过估计偏差的影响：因为Bellman更新最大化噪声或不完善的动作价值估计，正误差可能被选择并传播，导致学习到的值超过真实最优值。这种偏差会减慢学习速度、降低策略质量，并使价值估计不可靠。尽管Q-learning的收敛性已被广泛研究，但明确反映这种过估计机制的收敛理论仍然有限。本文研究了由过估计偏差引起的Q-learning的非对称收敛行为。我们将Q-learning误差分解为其分量正部和负部，并推导出两个分量各自的有限时间速率。得到的证书可以为正分量分配比负分量更慢的指数包络。这种速率分离为最大值引起的过估计提供了间接的理论证据：正误差可以通过最大化步骤被放大，而负误差则允许与最优策略系统进行更尖锐的比较。这种分离是上界之间的差异，因此不一定对每个实际Q-learning轨迹都成立。尽管如此，我们构建了预测的不对称性出现在实际轨迹中的例子。分析给出了确定性和随机常步长界限，并阐明了过估计如何进入Q-learning的切换系统动力学。

Original abstract: Q-learning is known to suffer from overestimation bias: because the Bellman update maximizes noisy or imperfect action-value estimates, positive errors can be selected and propagated, causing learned values to exceed the true optimal values. This bias can slow learning, degrade policy quality, and make value estimates unreliable. Although the convergence of Q-learning has been studied extensively, convergence theory that explicitly reflects this overestimation mechanism remains limited. This paper studies the asymmetric convergence behavior of Q-learning induced by overestimation bias. We decompose the Q-learning error into its componentwise positive and negative parts and derive separate finite-time rates for the two components. The resulting certificates can assign a slower exponential envelope to the positive component than to the negative component. This rate separation provides indirect theoretical evidence for max-induced overestimation: positive errors can be amplified through the maximization step, whereas negative errors admit a sharper comparison with an optimal-policy system. The separation is a difference between upper bounds, so it need not hold for every realized Q-learning trajectory. Nevertheless, we construct examples in which the predicted asymmetry appears in the actual trajectory. The analysis gives deterministic and stochastic constant-step-size bounds and clarifies how overestimation enters the switching-system dynamics of Q-learning.

</details>


### [33] [ShopGym: An Integrated Framework for Realistic Simulation and Scalable Benchmarking of E-Commerce Web Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16116v1)
*Chinmay Savadikar,Mingyu Zhao,Yuanzheng Zhu,Han Li,Shuang Xie,Alberto Castelo,Tianfu Wu,Lingyun Wang*

TL;DR: 提出ShopGym框架，通过ShopArena将真实店铺转为可控沙盒，ShopGuru合成多样任务，解决电商agent评估中真实性与可控性的矛盾，验证合成与真实环境表现正相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计ShopGym框架，包含ShopArena（模拟层：将真实种子店铺匿名化并分阶段生成自包含沙盒商店）和ShopGuru（任务合成层：基于店铺目录、导航、政策等合成七类基准任务），生成可重置、可检查的评估工件。

Result: 通过224个任务在6个沙盒商店（3个合成数据+3个真实数据）上验证，合成店铺保留真实店铺的结构属性，且agent在合成店铺上的表现与真实店铺正相关。

中文摘要：开发和评估电子商务网络代理需要既能保留有意义任务结构又能实现可控、可重复和可扩展科学比较的环境。现有方法会强制产生权衡：真实店铺提供真实性但不稳定、难以检查且不可重复，而手工构建的沙盒基准测试提供控制但仅覆盖有限的布局、目录、政策和交互模式。我们认为核心瓶颈在于方法论：该领域缺乏一种可扩展的方式来构建既真实、多样、可控、可检查又可重复的评估设置。我们介绍了ShopGym，一个用于电子商务网络代理的真实模拟和可扩展基准测试的集成框架。ShopGym是一个构建电子商务模拟环境和基础基准任务的框架。其模拟层ShopArena通过匿名化店铺规格和分阶段验证的生成过程，将真实种子店铺转换为自包含的沙盒商店。在这些模拟商店之上，ShopGuru跨七个技能类别合成基准任务，将每个任务基于店铺的目录、导航结构、政策和交互能力。ShopArena和ShopGuru共同产生自包含、可重置、可检查和稳定的评估工件，保留与购物任务相关的结构属性和代理评估信号。我们通过基于图的结构分析和基于代理的行为评估验证了该框架，使用了224个跨六个沙盒商店（三个使用合成数据构建，三个使用真实数据）生成的任务。我们的结果表明，合成商店保留了真实店铺的关键结构属性，且代理在合成商店上的表现与在真实商店上的表现呈正相关。

Original abstract: Developing and evaluating e-commerce web agents requires environments that preserve meaningful task structure while enabling controllable, reproducible, and scalable scientific comparison. Existing methodologies force a tradeoff: live storefronts provide realism but are non-stationary, difficult to inspect, and irreproducible, while hand-built sandbox benchmarks provide control but cover only a narrow range of layouts, catalogs, policies, and interaction patterns. We argue that the core bottleneck is methodological: the field lacks a scalable way to construct evaluation settings that are simultaneously realistic, diverse, controllable, inspectable, and reproducible. We introduce ShopGym, an integrated framework for realistic simulation and scalable benchmarking of e-commerce web agents. ShopGym is a framework for constructing e-commerce simulation environments and grounded benchmark tasks. Its simulation layer, ShopArena, converts live seed storefronts into self-contained sandbox shops through anonymized shop specifications and a staged, validated generation process. On top of these simulated storefronts, ShopGuru synthesizes benchmark tasks across seven skill categories, grounding each task in the shop's catalog, navigation structure, policies, and interaction affordances. Together, ShopArena and ShopGuru produce self-contained, resettable, inspectable, and stable evaluation artifacts that preserve structural properties and agent-evaluation signals relevant to shopping tasks. We validate the framework through graph-based structural analysis and agent-based behavioral evaluation with 224 generated tasks across six sandbox shops: three constructed with synthetic data and three with real data. Our results show that the synthetic shops preserve key structural properties of live storefronts, with agent performance on synthetic shops positively correlated with performance on live storefronts.

### [34] [Property-Guided LLM Program Synthesis for Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16142v2)
*André G. Pereira,Augusto B. Corrêa,Jendrik Seipp*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 属性引导LLM程序合成，直接相关代码生成agent的反馈循环

TL;DR: 提出属性引导的LLM程序合成方法，通过反例反馈显著减少生成和评估成本，在PDDL规划领域实现更高效的启发式函数合成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM程序合成依赖数值评分，缺乏失败原因指导，导致大量无效生成和高昂的LLM推理与评估成本。本研究旨在通过属性引导和具体反例反馈来降低成本并提升程序质量。

Method: 采用属性引导的LLM程序合成：检查候选程序是否满足形式化定义的性质；一旦违反则提前终止评估，并向LLM提供反例。在PDDL规划中，要求LLM合成直接启发式函数，并通过反例引导的修复循环迭代优化。

Result: 在十个PDDL规划领域上，合成的启发式函数在几乎所有测试任务中有效直接；与最佳先前方法相比，平均每领域生成程序数减少七倍，无需搜索即可解决更多任务，且计算量降低数个数量级。

Conclusion: 对于存在可验证属性问题，属性引导的LLM合成能显著降低成本并提高程序质量。

中文摘要：大语言模型（LLMs）在程序合成方面取得了显著成功，能够发现超越先前解决方案的程序。然而，这些方法依赖简单的数值分数来指示程序质量，例如解决方案的值或通过的测试数量。由于分数无法提供程序失败的原因，系统必须生成并评估大量候选程序，希望其中一些能成功，这增加了LLM推理和评估成本。我们研究了一种不同的方法：属性引导的LLM程序合成。我们不是评估后给程序打分，而是检查候选程序是否满足形式化定义的属性。当属性被违反时，我们提前停止评估，并向LLM提供一个具体的反例，精确展示程序失败的方式。这种反馈大幅减少了程序生成数量和评估成本，并能引导LLM生成更强的程序。我们在PDDL规划领域评估了该方法，要求LLM合成直接启发式函数：通过严格改进的转移可达的每个状态都有一个严格改进的后继状态。具有该属性的启发式函数引导爬山算法直接到达目标状态。一个反例引导的修复循环生成一个候选程序，在训练集上检查属性，并返回第一个违反属性的案例。我们在十个规划领域上使用分布外测试集进行了评估。合成的启发式函数在几乎所有测试任务上都有效直接，并且与先前最佳生成方法相比，我们的方法平均每个领域生成的程序数量减少了七倍，在不使用搜索的情况下解决了更多任务，并且评估候选程序所需的计算量降低了几个数量级。只要问题存在可验证的属性，属性引导的LLM合成就能降低成本并提高程序质量。

Original abstract: LLMs have shown impressive success in program synthesis, discovering programs that surpass prior solutions. However, these approaches rely on simple numeric scores to signal program quality, such as the value of the solution or the number of passed tests. Because a score offers no guidance on why a program failed, the system must generate and evaluate many candidates hoping some succeed, increasing LLM inference and evaluation costs. We study a different approach: property-guided LLM program synthesis. Instead of scoring programs after evaluation, we check whether a candidate satisfies a formally defined property. When the property is violated, we stop the evaluation early and provide the LLM with a concrete counterexample showing exactly how the program failed. This feedback drastically reduces both the number of program generations and the evaluation cost, and can guide the LLM to generate stronger programs. We evaluate this approach on PDDL planning domains, asking the LLM to synthesize direct heuristic functions: every state reachable by strictly improving transitions has a strictly improving successor. A heuristic with this property leads hill-climbing algorithm directly to a goal state. A counterexample-guided repair loop generates one candidate program, checks the property over a training set, and returns the first case that violates the property. We evaluate our approach on ten planning domains with an out-of-distribution test set. The synthesized heuristics are effectively direct on virtually all test tasks, and compared to the best prior generation method our approach generates seven times fewer programs per domain on average, solves more tasks without using search, and requires several orders of magnitude less computation to evaluate candidates. Whenever a problem admits a verifiable property, property-guided LLM synthesis can reduce cost and improve program quality.

</details>


### [35] [Look Before You Leap: Autonomous Exploration for LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16143v1)
*Ziang Ye,Wentao Shi,Yuxin Liu,Yu Wang,Zhengzhou Cai,Yaorui Shi,Qi Gu,Xunliang Cai,Fuli Feng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM agent自主探索训练策略，通用agent学习方法

TL;DR: 提出Explore-then-Act范式，通过交替任务和探索训练以及Exploration Checkpoint Coverage度量，解决LLM智能体在陌生环境中的过早利用问题，从而提升泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于LLM的智能体在陌生环境中因过早利用而失败，自主探索能力未被充分研究。

Method: 定义Exploration Checkpoint Coverage度量；提出交替任务执行和探索轨迹的训练策略；提出Explore-then-Act范式，先探索后行动。

Result: 系统评估表明标准任务RL导致狭窄重复行为；新方法有效提升下游性能。

Conclusion: 系统性地探索对于构建可泛化和真实世界适用的智能体至关重要。

中文摘要：基于大型语言模型的智能体常常在陌生环境中失败，原因是过早利用：即在获取足够环境特定信息之前就依赖先验知识采取行动。我们认定自主探索是构建自适应智能体的一个关键但尚未充分探索的能力。为了形式化和量化这一能力，我们引入了探索检查点覆盖率（Exploration Checkpoint Coverage），这是一个可验证的度量标准，衡量智能体发现关键状态、对象和可供性（affordances）的广度。我们的系统评估表明，使用标准任务导向强化学习训练的智能体始终表现出狭窄和重复的行为，这阻碍了下游性能。为了解决这一限制，我们开发了一种训练策略，将任务执行轨迹和探索轨迹交替进行，每种轨迹通过其对应的可验证奖励进行优化。基于这种训练策略，我们提出了'先探索后行动'（Explore-then-Act）范式，将信息收集与任务执行解耦：智能体首先利用交互预算获取基于环境的知识，然后利用该知识完成任务解决。我们的结果表明，学习系统性地探索对于构建可泛化和真实世界适用的智能体是必不可少的。

Original abstract: Large language model based agents often fail in unfamiliar environments due to premature exploitation: a tendency to act on prior knowledge before acquiring sufficient environment-specific information. We identify autonomous exploration as a critical yet underexplored capability for building adaptive agents. To formalize and quantify this capability, we introduce Exploration Checkpoint Coverage, a verifiable metric that measures how broadly an agent discovers key states, objects, and affordances. Our systematic evaluation reveals that agents trained with standard task-oriented reinforcement learning consistently exhibit narrow and repetitive behaviors that impede downstream performance. To address this limitation, we develop a training strategy that interleaves task-execution rollouts and exploration rollouts, with each type of rollout optimized by its corresponding verifiable reward. Building on this training strategy, we propose the Explore-then-Act paradigm, which decouples information-gathering from task execution: agents first utilize an interaction budget to acquire grounded environmental knowledge, then leverage it for task resolution. Our results demonstrate that learning to systematically explore is imperative for building generalizable and real-world-ready agents.

### [36] [Formal Methods Meet LLMs: Auditing, Monitoring, and Intervention for Compliance of Advanced AI Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16198v1)
*Parand A. Alamdari,Toryn Q. Klassen,Sheila A. McIlraith*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM agent审计监控与干预，通用agent安全控制方法

TL;DR: 提出利用线性时序逻辑（LTL）结合形式化方法和机器学习，对AI系统（尤其是LLM）进行离线审计和在线监控，以检测和预防违反时间扩展行为约束的行为，实验证明该方法优于LLM基线，并能显著降低违规率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI治理需要有效监控和审计AI产品和服务，特别是检测违反时间扩展行为约束（如安全、规范等）的问题，而现有LLM在时间推理上存在局限性。

Method: 结合形式化方法（LTL语法和语义）与机器学习，提出离线审计、在线监控、预测性监控（基于采样）和干预性监控技术，用于黑盒LLM系统。

Result: 该方法在检测时间扩展约束违规方面优于LLM基线，小模型也能匹配或超越前沿LLM评判器；干预监控显著降低违规率且保持任务性能；LLM时间推理精度随事件距离、约束数量和命题数量增加而下降。

Conclusion: 基于LTL的形式化监控技术能有效提升AI系统的合规性和安全性，为AI治理提供实用方案。

中文摘要：我们研究了人工智能治理的一个特定维度：如何在人工智能开发生命周期中监控和审计人工智能赋能的产品和服务，从部署前测试到部署后审计。结合形式化方法的原理与最先进的机器学习，我们提出了使人工智能赋能产品和服务的开发者以及第三方人工智能开发者和评估者能够对黑盒先进人工智能系统（尤其是大型语言模型）进行离线审计和在线（运行时）监控产品特定（时间扩展）行为约束（如安全约束、规范、规则和法规）的技术。我们进一步提供了预测性监控的实用技术，例如基于抽样的方法，并引入了在运行时进行干预的监控器，以预防并可能缓解预测的违规行为。实验结果表明，通过利用线性时序逻辑的形式化语法和语义，我们提出的审计和监控技术在检测时间扩展行为约束违规方面优于大型语言模型基线方法；采用我们的方法，即使小模型标注者也能匹配或超越前沿的大型语言模型评判者。我们的预测性和干预性监控器显著降低了基于大型语言模型的代理的违规率，同时基本保持了任务性能。我们还通过控制实验表明，大型语言模型的时间推理在事件距离、约束数量和命题数量增加时，准确性显著下降。

Original abstract: We examine one particular dimension of AI governance: how to monitor and audit AI-enabled products and services throughout the AI development lifecycle, from pre-deployment testing to post-deployment auditing. Combining principles from formal methods with SoTA machine learning, we propose techniques that enable AI-enabled product and service developers, as well as third party AI developers and evaluators, to perform offline auditing and online (runtime) monitoring of product-specific (temporally extended) behavioral constraints such as safety constraints, norms, rules and regulations with respect to black-box advanced AI systems, notably LLMs. We further provide practical techniques for predictive monitoring, such as sampling-based methods, and we introduce intervening monitors that act at runtime to preempt and potentially mitigate predicted violations. Experimental results show that by exploiting the formal syntax and semantics of Linear Temporal Logic (LTL), our proposed auditing and monitoring techniques are superior to LLM baseline methods in detecting violations of temporally extended behavioral constraints; with our approach, even small-model labelers match or exceed frontier LLM judges. Our predictive and intervening monitors significantly reduce the violation rates of LLM-based agents while largely preserving task performance. We further show through controlled experiments that LLMs' temporal reasoning shows a pronounced degradation in accuracy with increasing event distance, number of constraints, and number of propositions.

### [37] [Context, Reasoning, and Hierarchy: A Cost-Performance Study of Compound LLM Agent Design in an Adversarial POMDP](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16205v1)
*Igor Bogdanov,Chung-Horng Lung,Thomas Kunz,Jie Gao,Adrian Taylor,Marzia Zaman*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 复合LLM agent设计成本效益研究，通用agent架构结论

TL;DR: 在对抗性POMDP中，程序化状态抽象和层次化分解比深层推理更有效，且推理工具与层次化结合会导致性能下降（推理级联）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺乏关于复合LLM代理设计选择（上下文表示、推理、分解）对性能与成本影响的指导。

Method: 在CybORG CAGE-2环境进行对照实验，变化上下文表示、推理工具和层次化分解，评估5个模型系列、6个模型、12种配置共3475回合，核算令牌成本。

Result: (1) 程序化状态抽象每令牌回报最高，提高76%；(2) 推理工具分布在层次结构中导致性能下降最多3.4倍，令牌使用增加1.8-2.7倍（推理级联）；(3) 无推理的层次化分解最佳，上下文工程比推理更划算。

Conclusion: 设计原则：投资于程序化基础设施和清晰的任务分解，而不是更深入的每个代理推理，因为这些策略在结合时可能会互相干扰。

中文摘要：在对抗性、部分可观察的序列环境中部署复合LLM代理需要处理几个设计维度：(1) 代理看到什么，(2) 它如何推理，以及 (3) 任务如何在组件之间分解。然而，实践者缺乏关于哪些设计选择能提高性能而哪些仅仅增加推理成本的指导。我们提出了一个在CybORG CAGE-2中的复合LLM代理设计的受控研究，这是一个建模为部分可观察马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP）的网络安全防御环境。奖励是非正的，因此所有配置都在失败缓解模式下运行。我们的评估涵盖五个模型系列、六个模型和十二种配置（3475个回合），并进行令牌级别的成本核算。我们变化上下文表示（原始观察 vs. 带有压缩历史的确定性状态跟踪层）、推理工具（自我提问、自我批评和自我改进工具，可选择思维链提示）以及层次化分解（整体式ReAct vs. 委托给专门子代理）。我们发现：(1) 程序化状态抽象提供了每令牌花费的最大回报（RPTS），平均回报比原始观察提高了高达76%。(2) 将推理工具分布在层次结构中相对于仅使用层次结构会降低性能，对于所有五个模型系列，平均回报最多差3.4倍，同时使用1.8-2.7倍的令牌。我们将这种破坏性模式称为推理级联。(3) 无推理的层次化分解对大多数模型实现了最佳绝对性能，并且上下文工程通常比推理更具成本效益。这些发现为结构化对抗性POMDP提出了一条设计原则：投资于程序化基础设施和清晰的任务分解，而不是更深入的每个代理推理，因为这些策略在结合时可能会互相干扰。

Original abstract: Deploying compound LLM agents in adversarial, partially observable sequential environments requires navigating several design dimensions: (1) what the agent sees, (2) how it reasons, and (3) how tasks are decomposed across components. Yet practitioners lack guidance on which design choices improve performance versus merely increase inference costs. We present a controlled study of compound LLM agent design in CybORG CAGE-2, a cyber defense environment modeled as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP). Reward is non-positive, so all configurations operate in a failure-mitigation mode. Our evaluation spans five model families, six models, and twelve configurations (3,475 episodes) with token-level cost accounting. We vary context representation (raw observations vs. a deterministic state-tracking layer with compressed history), deliberation (self-questioning, self-critique, and self-improvement tools, with optional chain-of-thought prompting), and hierarchical decomposition (monolithic ReAct vs. delegation to specialized sub-agents). We find that: (1) Programmatic state abstraction delivers the largest returns per token spent (RPTS), improving mean return by up to 76% over raw observations. (2) Distributing deliberation tools across a hierarchy degrades performance relative to hierarchy alone for all five model families, reaching up to 3.4$\times$ worse mean return while using 1.8-2.7$\times$ more tokens. We call this destructive pattern a deliberation cascade. (3) Hierarchical decomposition without deliberation achieves the best absolute performance for most models, and context engineering is generally more cost-effective than deliberation. These findings suggest a design principle for structured adversarial POMDPs: invest in programmatic infrastructure and clean task decomposition rather than deeper per-agent reasoning, as these strategies can interfere when combined.

### [38] [Confirming Correct, Missing the Rest: LLM Tutoring Agents Struggle Where Feedback Matters Most](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16207v1)
*Tahreem Yasir,Wenbo Li,Sam Gilson,Sutapa Dey Tithi,Xiaoyi Tian,Tiffany Barnes*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM辅导agent反馈质量评估，agent评测启发

TL;DR: LLM在辅导中诊断学生解决方案时，过度拒绝有效但次优方案并过度验证错误方案，准确诊断不一定产生可操作反馈，建议混合架构用知识图谱诊断、LLM支持对话。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 区分最优、有效但次优和错误的学生解决方案对于有效辅导至关重要，但LLM在辅导中的诊断精度尚未被系统评估。

Method: 构建包含7个LLM反馈代理的基准测试，使用命题逻辑知识图谱导出真实标签，在10,836个方案-反馈对和三种反馈条件下评估模型。

Result: 模型在最优步骤上表现接近天花板，但系统性地过度拒绝有效但次优推理并过度验证错误方案；这些失败跨模型和上下文存在，且准确诊断未能可靠产生教学可操作反馈。

Conclusion: LLM更适合混合架构，由知识图谱模型负责诊断，LLM负责开放式支架和对话支持。

中文摘要：有效的辅导需要区分最优、有效但次优以及不正确的学生解决方案，这一区分是智能辅导系统（ITS）的核心，但尚未在基于LLM的辅导系统中得到检验。随着LLM被越来越多地探索作为ITS的对话补充，评估其诊断精确性至关重要。我们提出了一个包含七个LLM反馈代理的基准测试，在命题逻辑中使用知识图谱导出的真实标签，涵盖10,836个方案-反馈对和三种反馈条件。模型在最优步骤上达到了近乎天花板的表现，但系统性地过度拒绝了有效但次优的推理，并过度验证了不正确的解决方案，而这正是自适应辅导最关键的环节。这些失败在所有模型中持续存在，无论解决方案上下文如何，表明是架构限制而非信息限制。此外，准确的诊断并不能可靠地产生具有教学可操作性的反馈，揭示了诊断判断与教学效果之间的差距。我们的发现表明，LLM更适合混合架构，其中基于知识图谱的模型处理诊断，而LLM支持开放式支架和对话。

Original abstract: Effective tutoring requires distinguishing optimal, valid but suboptimal, and incorrect student solutions, a distinction central to intelligent tutoring systems (ITS) but untested for LLM-based tutors. As LLMs are increasingly explored as conversational complements to ITS, evaluating their diagnostic precision is essential. We present a benchmark of seven LLM feedback agents in propositional logic using knowledge-graph-derived ground truth across 10,836 solution--feedback pairs and three feedback conditions. Models achieved near-ceiling performance on optimal steps but systematically over-rejected valid but suboptimal reasoning and over-validated incorrect solutions, precisely where adaptive tutoring matters most. These failures persisted across models regardless of solution context, suggesting architectural rather than informational limits. Moreover, accurate diagnosis did not reliably produce pedagogically actionable feedback, revealing a gap between diagnostic judgment and instructional effectiveness. Our findings suggest that LLMs are better suited for hybrid architectures where KG-grounded models handle diagnosis while LLMs support open-ended scaffolding and dialogue.

### [39] [FORGE: Self-Evolving Agent Memory With No Weight Updates via Population Broadcast](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16233v1)
*Igor Bogdanov,Chung-Horng Lung,Thomas Kunz,Jie Gao,Adrian Taylor,Marzia Zaman*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自进化agent记忆协议，无权重更新，直接相关agent记忆方法

TL;DR: FORGE是一种通过自生成记忆改进LLM智能体决策的无梯度分阶段种群协议，在CAGE-2任务上相比零样本和Reflexion基线显著提升性能，并降低重大失败率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究LLM智能体能否仅通过自生成的自然语言记忆（无梯度更新）来改进决策，弥补现有反射式学习方法的不足。

Method: FORGE采用分阶段种群协议，内循环将失败轨迹转化为规则/示例/混合记忆，外循环通过广播最佳记忆和毕业机制进化，无需梯度或更强模型。

Result: 在12种模型-表示条件下，FORGE的平均回报比零样本提升1.7-7.7倍，比Reflexion提升29-72%，重大失败率（低于-100）降至约1%。

Conclusion: 种群广播是关键机制；示例记忆性能最优，规则记忆成本效益高；较弱模型获益更大；证据限于CAGE-2 B线，跨家族结果为方向性指示。

中文摘要：LLM智能体能否通过自生成记忆（无需梯度更新）改进决策？我们提出了FORGE（失败优化反思毕业与进化），一种分阶段的、基于种群的协议，用于演化注入提示的自然语言记忆，适用于分层ReAct智能体。FORGE封装了一个类似Reflexion的内循环，其中专门的反思智能体（使用相同底层LLM，不蒸馏更强模型）将失败轨迹转化为可重用的知识产物：文本启发式（规则）、少样本示例（示例），或两者兼有（混合），外循环则在不同阶段之间将表现最佳实例的记忆传播到种群中，并通过毕业标准冻结收敛的实例。我们在CybORG CAGE-2上进行了评估，这是一个30步视界内针对B线攻击者的随机网络防御POMDP，所有四个测试的LLM家族（Gemini-2.5-Flash-Lite、Grok-4-Fast、Llama-4-Maverick、Qwen3-235B）均表现出强烈的负值、重尾零样本奖励。与零样本基线和Reflexion基线（孤立的单流学习）相比，FORGE在全部12种模型-表示条件下，平均评估回报比零样本提升1.7-7.7倍，比Reflexion提升29-72%，将重大失败率（低于-100）降至约1%。我们发现：（1）种群广播是关键机制，无毕业消融实验确认广播带来了性能提升，而毕业主要节省计算；（2）对于四种模型中的三种，示例实现了最强回报，规则提供了最佳成本-可靠性曲线，且token数减少约40%；（3）较弱的基线模型获益不成比例，表明FORGE可能缩小能力差距而非放大强模型。所有证据仅限于CAGE-2 B线；跨家族发现为方向性证据。

Original abstract: Can LLM agents improve decision-making through self-generated memory without gradient updates? We propose FORGE (Failure-Optimized Reflective Graduation and Evolution), a staged, population-based protocol that evolves prompt-injected natural-language memory for hierarchical ReAct agents. FORGE wraps a Reflexion-style inner loop, where a dedicated reflection agent (using the same underlying LLM, no distillation from a stronger model) converts failed trajectories into reusable knowledge artifacts: textual heuristics (Rules), few-shot demonstrations (Examples), or both (Mixed), with an outer loop that propagates the best-performing instance's memory to the population between stages and freezes converged instances via a graduation criterion. We evaluate on CybORG CAGE-2, a stochastic network-defense POMDP at a 30-step horizon against the B-line attacker, where all four tested LLM families (Gemini-2.5-Flash-Lite, Grok-4-Fast, Llama-4-Maverick, Qwen3-235B) exhibit strongly negative, heavy-tailed zero-shot rewards. Compared against both a zero-shot baseline and a Reflexion baseline (isolated single-stream learning), FORGE improves average evaluation return by 1.7-7.7$\times$ over zero-shot and by 29-72% over Reflexion in all 12 model-representation conditions, reducing major-failure rates (below $-100$) to as low as $\sim$1%. We find that (1) population broadcast is critical mechanism, with a no-graduation ablation confirming that broadcast carries the performance gains while graduation primarily saves compute; (2) Examples achieves the strongest returns for three of four models, Rules offers the best cost-reliability profile with $\sim$40% fewer tokens; and (3) weaker baseline models benefit disproportionately, suggesting FORGE may mitigate capability gaps rather than amplify strong models. All evidence is confined to CAGE-2 B-line; cross-family findings are directional evidence.

</details>


### [40] [Prospective multi-pathogen disease forecasting using autonomous LLM-guided tree search](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16238v1)
*Sarah Martinson,Michael P. Brenner,Martyna Plomecka,Brian P. Williams,Nicholas G. Reich,Zahra Shamsi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM树搜索自动生成疾病预测模型，含迭代优化和奖励纠正，可迁移至代码优化agent

TL;DR: 该系统利用LLM引导的树搜索自主生成传染病预测模型，在2025-2026美国呼吸道季节中，其集成模型性能与人类专家模型相当或更优，并能处理数据稀缺场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统传染病预测依赖人工模型筛选，劳动密集且难以扩展至细粒度区域或新病原体，急需自动化方法。

Method: 提出LLM引导的树搜索系统，迭代生成、评估和优化预测代码；使用自动评判人循环和优化对数尺度距离度量。

Result: 在2025-2026美国呼吸道季节，系统自主生成多种模型，集成性能匹配或超越CDC人工集成；在RSV冷启动场景表现良好；消融实验验证了防奖励黑客和结构保真设计。

Conclusion: 该框架通过自主将流行病学理论转化为代码，克服了建模劳动力瓶颈，实现了可扩展的专家级疾病预测。

中文摘要：传染病的概率预测对公共卫生至关重要，但这依赖于专家建模团队劳动密集型的模型人工筛选。这种定制开发限制了向细粒度地理分辨率或新兴病原体的可扩展性。在此，我们提出了一种自主系统，利用大型语言模型（LLM）引导的树搜索来迭代生成、评估和优化可执行的预测软件。在2025-2026年美国呼吸道季节的前瞻性实时评估中，该系统自主发现了针对流感、COVID-19和呼吸道合胞病毒（RSV）的方法多样模型。聚合这些机器生成的模型产生的集成模型在样本外持续匹配或优于黄金标准的人工筛选的疾病控制与预防中心（CDC）枢纽集成模型。该系统成功应对了RSV数据稀缺的“冷启动”场景。此外，受控的回顾性消融实验表明，优化对数尺度距离度量可防止奖励黑客行为，而自动化的评判人循环确保了复杂科学理论的结构保真度。通过将流行病学理论自主转化为准确、透明的代码，该框架克服了建模劳动力瓶颈，实现了前所未有的规模下专家级疾病预测的快速部署。

Original abstract: Probabilistic forecasting of infectious diseases is crucial for public health but relies on labor-intensive manual model curation by expert modeling teams. This bespoke development bottlenecks scalability to granular geographic resolutions or emerging pathogens. Here, we present an autonomous system using Large Language Model (LLM)-guided tree search to iteratively generate, evaluate, and optimize executable forecasting software. In a fully prospective, real-time evaluation during the 2025-2026 US respiratory season, the system autonomously discovered methodologically diverse models for influenza, COVID-19, and respiratory syncytial virus (RSV). Aggregating these machine-generated models yielded an ensemble that consistently matched or outperformed the gold-standard, human-curated Centers for Disease Control and Prevention (CDC) hub ensembles out-of-sample. The system successfully navigated data-scarce "cold start" scenarios for RSV. Moreover, controlled retrospective ablations revealed that optimizing log-scale distance metrics prevents reward hacking, while an automated judge-in-the-loop ensures structural fidelity to complex scientific theories. By autonomously translating epidemiological theory into accurate, transparent code, this framework overcomes the modeling labor bottleneck, enabling rapid deployment of expert-level disease forecasting at unprecedented scales.

### [41] [From Prompts to Protocols: An AI Agent for Laboratory Automation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16552v1)
*Angelos Angelopoulos,James F. Cahoon,Ron Alterovitz*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 实验室自动化AI agent，含agent循环、验证纠错，可迁移至代码优化agent的协议生成

TL;DR: 提出一个集成大语言模型的AI代理架构，用于自动化实验室方案的自然语言创建和监控，在模拟实验室中达到97%首次成功率并大幅减少界面操作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自动化实验室设置复杂，科学家需编写代码和管理配置文件，效率低下且门槛高，急需更直观的交互方式。

Method: 提出一种AI代理架构，将大语言模型集成到实验编排系统中，支持自然语言交互、自动验证与纠错，并结合可视化图形编辑器实现人机协同。

Result: 在三个模拟自动化实验室（化学、生物学、材料科学）中，AI代理首次尝试方案生成成功率为97%，界面操作减少一个数量级。

Conclusion: 该AI代理通过自然语言交互和自动化验证，显著简化了自动化实验室的协议创建与监控，提高了实验效率和易用性。

中文摘要：自动化科学实验室能够更快、更安全、更准确、更可重复地执行实验方案，加速新材料、药物等的发现和测试。然而，建立和运行自主实验室需要协调大量仪器和机器人，迫使科学家编写代码、管理配置文件并处理复杂的软件基础设施。我们提出了一种AI代理架构，将大语言模型与实验室编排相结合，使科学家能够使用自然语言交互式地创建和监控自动化实验室方案。该AI代理集成到实验编排系统（EOS）中，在具有自动验证和错误纠正的代理循环下运行，并支持完整的实验生命周期：创建方案、运行和监控方案及闭环优化活动，以及分析结果。一个可视化图形编辑器将方案呈现为交互式节点图，与AI代理的方案表示同步，实现在AI辅助和手动方案构建之间的无缝切换。在涵盖化学、生物学和材料科学的三个模拟自动化实验室上的评估显示，该AI代理实现了97%的首次尝试方案生成成功率，并且所需的界面操作减少了一个数量级。

Original abstract: Automating science laboratories enables faster, safer, more accurate, and more reproducible execution of protocols, accelerating the discovery and testing of new materials, drugs, and more. However, setting up and running autonomous labs requires coordinating numerous instruments and robots, forcing scientists to write code, manage configuration files, and navigate complex software infrastructure. We present an AI agent architecture that integrates large language models with laboratory orchestration, enabling scientists to interactively create and monitor automated lab protocols using natural language. Integrated into the Experiment Orchestration System (EOS), the AI agent operates under an agentic loop with automated validation and error correction, and supports the complete experimental lifecycle: creating protocols, running and monitoring both protocols and closed-loop optimization campaigns, and analyzing results. A visual graph editor renders protocols as interactive node-based diagrams synchronized with the AI agent's protocol representation, enabling seamless alternation between AI-assisted and manual protocol construction. Evaluated on three simulated automated labs spanning chemistry, biology, and materials science, the AI agent achieves a 97% first-attempt protocol generation success rate and an order of magnitude reduction in required interface actions.

</details>


### [42] [Skim: Speculative Execution for Fast and Efficient Web Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16565v2)
*Mike Wong,Kevin Hsieh,Suman Nath,Ravi Netravali*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: Web agent推测执行框架，大幅降本提效，对coding agent加速有直接迁移价值

TL;DR: Skim通过利用网站的可预测结构，使用快速路径处理大多数查询，将中位每任务成本降低1.9倍，延迟降低33.4%，且无精度损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前Web代理在每个任务步骤中都使用前沿模型推理、浏览器渲染和ReAct规划，导致高昂成本，而大多数查询实际上可以绕过这些重型组件。

Method: 离线分析器捕获网站模式，运行时通过模板匹配、URL合成和小模型提取答案，轻量验证器检测错误，错误时级联到完整代理。

Result: 在三个骨干代理上，中位每任务成本降低1.9倍，延迟降低33.4%，且无精度损失。

Conclusion: Skim表明，通过利用网站结构可以大幅降低Web代理的成本，同时保持准确性。

中文摘要：Skim是一个投机执行框架，用于利用目的构建网站的可预测结构。当今Web代理的昂贵开销并非任务固有的，而是代理的组成方式所致：前沿模型推理、浏览器渲染和ReAct风格的规划被应用于每个任务的每一步，无论其复杂性如何。Skim的关键观察是，网站对同一类型的查询强制执行稳定的URL模式、答案格式和任务到轨迹的映射，因此大多数查询可以完全绕过这些重型组件。一个离线分析器每个站点一次捕获这些模式。在运行时，Skim将每个查询匹配到模板，合成目标URL，并用小模型提取答案。一个轻量级验证器根据查询和模式对每个快速路径输出进行验证；罕见的错误推测会级联到完整代理，该代理由快速路径的最终URL热启动，以保留上游轨迹进度。在标准Web代理基准测试中，结合三个骨干代理（WebVoyager、AgentOccam、BrowserUse），Skim将中位每任务成本降低了1.9倍，延迟降低了33.4%，且无精度损失。

Original abstract: Skim is a speculative execution framework for web agents that exploits the predictable structure of purpose-built websites. Today's web-agent expense is not intrinsic to the tasks but a property of how agents are composed: frontier-model inference, browser rendering, and ReAct-style planning are applied to every step of every task regardless of complexity. Skim's key observation is that websites enforce stable URL patterns, answer formats, and task-to-trajectory mappings across queries of the same type, so most queries can bypass these heavyweight components entirely. An offline profiler captures these patterns once per site. At runtime, Skim matches each query to a template, synthesizes the destination URL, and extracts the answer with a small model. A lightweight verifier gates each fast-path output against the query and schema; rare misspeculations cascade to the full agent, warm-started by the fast path's final URL to preserve upstream trajectory progress. Across standard web-agent benchmarks paired with three backboneagents (WebVoyager, AgentOccam, BrowserUse), Skim reduces median per-task cost by 1.9x and latency by 33.4% with no accuracy loss.

</details>


### [43] [Counterparty Modeling is Not Strategy: The Limits of LLM Negotiators](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16575v1)
*Romain Cosentino,Sarath Shekkizhar,Adam Earle,Silvio Savarese*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM谈判agent的实证研究，分析策略缺陷，可迁移到agent设计。

TL;DR: LLM代理能推断对手偏好，但不会战略性地利用，导致谈判结果受初始锚点影响而低效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究LLM代理在多回合谈判中是否能利用对手偏好信息进行战略性报价和还盘。

Method: 在受控多属性谈判环境中，分析LLM代理在信息对称和不对称条件下的行为，包括偏好建模、让步策略和最终协议效率。

Result: LLM代理能准确建模偏好，但未能转化为战略优势；卖家更迁就；知情方在不对称条件下让步更弱；最终协议受初始锚点主导；明确要求策略性陈述未改进效率。

Conclusion: 当前LLM代理缺乏利用效用结构进行战略谈判的能力，需要改进以在复杂谈判中实现真正策略性协商。

中文摘要：谈判需要的不仅仅是推断对方想要什么：它需要利用这些信息在多轮对话中提出有利的报价和还盘。我们研究了大语言模型（LLM）代理在一个受控的多属性谈判环境中是否做到了这一点。我们发现，当前的LLM代理能够建模对手方的偏好，但并未可靠地将该知识转化为战略性谈判。当被提供谈判伙伴的偏好信息时，代理能够准确地建模并在其推理轨迹的早期就使用这些信息，但这并未可靠地改善知情方的结果。逐轮分析揭示了原因：代理常常根据他们认为对方看重的内容做出回应，但并未始终如一地将这些举动与自身高价值属性的收益相结合。卖家总体上更加迁就，在信息不对称条件下，知情方往往做出补偿较弱的让步。由于代理未能利用这种潜在的效用结构获得战略优势，他们的最终协议在很大程度上受表面级别的初始锚点而非实际效用权重的影响。最后，要求代理在提出报价之前明确陈述让步换取互惠的交易，这使得单个回合看起来更具战略性，但最终未能提高最终协议的效率。

Original abstract: Negotiation requires more than inferring what the other side wants: it requires using that information to make advantageous offers and counteroffers over multiple turns. We study whether large language model (LLM) agents do this in a controlled multi-attribute bargaining environment. We find that current LLM agents can model a counterparty's preferences, but do not reliably turn that knowledge into strategic bargaining. When given negotiating partner preference information, agents model it accurately and early in their reasoning traces, yet this does not reliably improve outcomes for the informed side. Turn-level analyses show why: agents often respond to what they believe the counterparty values, but do not consistently pair those moves with gains on their own high-value attributes. Sellers are more accommodating overall, and in asymmetric-information conditions, the informed side often makes the more weakly compensated concessions. Because agents fail to leverage this underlying utility structure for strategic advantage, their final agreements are heavily dictated by surface-level opening anchors rather than actual utility weights. Finally, requiring agents to explicitly state concession-for-reciprocity trades before making an offer makes individual turns look more strategic, but ultimately fails to improve the efficiency of the final agreements.

</details>

### [44] [Access Timing as Scaffolding: A Reinforcement Learning Approach to GenAI in Education](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15850v2)
*Janne Rotter,Pau Benazet i Montobbio,Davinia Hernández-Leo*

Main category: cs.CY

Selection reason: RL agent控制GenAI访问时机，通用agent方法可迁移至coding agent的访问控制。

TL;DR: 通过强化学习智能体策略性地控制GenAI访问时机，相比无限制或完全限制，能提升学习效果和元认知准确性，且无需显式支架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注如何教学性地使用GenAI，但缺乏对何时允许使用GenAI的实证研究，尤其是缺乏教学理论指导。

Method: 设计一个强化学习智能体，基于元认知、认知负荷和生产性失败理论决定学生访问GenAI的时机，并在105名大学生的混合方法受控实验中比较无限制、完全限制和RL条件下的学习效果。

Result: RL条件下学生的客观后测成绩和元认知准确性显著优于无限制条件，任务错误和时间少于完全限制条件；但自我报告元认知意识无显著差异。

Conclusion: 策略性控制GenAI访问时机是一种可操作、有理论依据且可扩展的教学策略，优于完全开放或完全禁止，为人类-AI学习系统设计提供了新方向。

中文摘要：近年来，生成式AI（GenAI）在教育环境中已普遍存在于大学生的日常生活中，尽管它可能在不加限制使用时引发过度依赖、元认知脱离和学习效果下降。先前大多数研究关注如何从教学法上为其使用提供支架，但关于何时允许使用现成GenAI的问题仍缺乏充分研究，且缺乏基于教学法的实证调查。我们将访问时机本身视为一种隐式支架，并通过强化学习（RL）智能体来操作化，该智能体决定学生何时应访问GenAI，其奖励函数基于元认知理论、认知负荷理论和生产性失败。在一项包含105名高等教育学生的混合方法受控实验室研究中，我们将该智能体对学习增益和元认知参与的影响与无限制使用和完全限制使用进行了比较。结果表明，在强化学习条件下策略性地安排GenAI访问时机，与无限制访问相比提高了客观后测成绩和元认知准确性，同时与完全限制相比减少了任务错误和任务时间，因此优于两种方法，无需显式元认知提示或结构化支架。然而，在自我报告的元认知意识方面，条件之间没有差异。总体而言，GenAI访问时机是一种可操作、有理论依据且可扩展的教学策略，优于完全无限制和完全禁止访问，与现成工具兼容且可能具有低采用门槛。这开启了一个新的研究领域，探索教育工作者如何促进访问时机以及如何在人机学习系统设计中实现它。

Original abstract: In recent years, generative AI (GenAI) in educational settings has become ubiquitous in university students' daily lives, despite its potential to induce over-reliance, metacognitive disengagement, and diminished learning when used unrestrictedly. While most prior research has focused on how to pedagogically scaffold its usage, the question of when to allow off-the-shelf GenAI remains understudied and lacks pedagogically grounded empirical investigation. We treat access timing itself as a form of implicit scaffolding and operationalize it through a reinforcement learning (RL) agent that decides when students should access GenAI, with a reward function grounded in metacognitive theory, cognitive load theory, and productive failure. In a mixed-methods controlled lab study with N=105 higher education students, we compared the agent's effect on learning gains and metacognitive engagement to unrestricted and fully restricted use. Results show that strategically timed GenAI access under the reinforcement learning condition improved objective post-test performance and metacognitive accuracy compared with unrestricted access, while reducing task errors and time on task relative to complete withholding, thus outperforming both approaches without the need for explicit metacognitive prompts or structured scaffolding. However, no between-condition differences emerged on self-reported metacognitive awareness. Overall, timing of GenAI access therefore is a tractable, theoretically grounded, and scalable pedagogical strategy that improves over completely unrestricted and withheld access, compatible with off-the-shelf tools and potentially low adoption barrier. This opens up a new research area that explores how access timing can be facilitated by educators and implemented in human-AI learning system design.

</details>

### [45] [Toward Natural and Companionable Virtual Agents via Cross-Temporal Emotional Modeling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15812v1)
*Feier Qin,Xiao Li,Yi Zheng,Haibin Huang,Hanyao Wang,Xiaoyu Wang,Yan Lu,Yuan Zhang*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: 跨时间情感建模用于陪伴型虚拟代理，属于通用LLM agent情感与长期交互方法，对agent设计有潜在启发。

TL;DR: CTEM框架通过跨时间情感建模，在长期陪伴对话中提升了自然性、连贯性和情感和谐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前陪伴代理缺乏跨时间情感建模，导致互动零散不真实。

Method: 提出了CTEM框架，将长期行为历史与即时情感表达链接，建立闭环更新机制，并实例化为Auri代理。

Result: 21天实地研究表明CTEM在感知自然性、连贯性和情感和谐上有提升。

Conclusion: 跨时间情感建模对于实现自然长期陪伴交互至关重要。

中文摘要：基础模型的最新进展使得对话代理能够追求持续陪伴而非仅仅完成任务。然而，大多数代理仍然无法支持自然、长期的类陪伴互动，导致用户体验显得零散且不真实。我们认为，当前代理忽视了代理社交行为和内部情感的跨时间建模：生成的行为很少影响代理的情绪状态，情绪状态也很少塑造后续行为。我们提出了跨时间情感建模（CTEM）框架，该框架将长期行为历史与即时情感表达联系起来。CTEM建立了一个闭环，其中过去的经历更新不断演化的情感状态；该状态调节即时互动；用户反馈不断修正记忆和情感状态，从而实现反思和预期。我们将CTEM实例化为Auri，一个即时通讯平台上的陪伴代理，并报告了一项为期21天的实地研究，表明CTEM在感知自然性、连贯性和情感和谐方面有所改进。

Original abstract: Recent advances in foundation models have enabled conversational agents that aim for sustained companionship rather than mere task completion. Yet most still remain unable to support natural, long-term companion-like interactions, resulting in experiences that feel episodic and inauthentic. We argue that current agents overlooked cross-temporal modeling of agents' social behaviors and internal emotions: generated behaviors rarely influence an agent's emotional state, and emotional states seldom shape subsequent behaviors. We present Cross-Temporal Emotion Modeling (CTEM), a framework that links long-term behavioral history to moment-to-moment emotional expression. CTEM establishes a closed loop where past experiences update an evolving emotional state; this state conditions immediate interactions; and user feedback continually revises both memory and emotional state, enabling reflection and anticipation. We instantiate CTEM as Auri, a companion agent on an instant-messaging platform, and report a 21-day in-the-wild study showing that CTEM shows improvements in perceived naturalness, coherence, and emotional harmony.

</details>


### [46] [SLIP & ETHICS: Graduated Intervention for AI Emotional Companions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15915v1)
*Minseo Kim*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: AI陪伴的安全分级干预方法，对agent安全设计有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 提出SLIP和ETHICS方法，通过渐进干预平衡AI情感陪伴的安全与融洽，实验显示有效但存在边界情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决AI情感陪伴中安全措施与用户体验之间的悖论，避免过度限制破坏信任或过于宽松导致伤害。

Method: 设计SLIP四阶段渐进干预协议，结合ETHICS信号分类法，通过情感强度与叙事动力指标生成干预；进行小规模用户部署与合成角色测试评估。

Result: 流动角色假阳性0%，危机角色呈现预期升级；高能量连续升高情景初期未触发干预（0/8），增强模型后检测率提升至6/8且维持0假阳性。

Conclusion: 渐进干预可作为设计方向来导航而非彻底解决安全-融洽张力，但仍需进一步验证与优化。

中文摘要：AI情感陪伴面临安全-融洽悖论：限制性安全措施可能损害支持性联盟，而宽松系统则面临用户伤害风险。我们提出SLIP（分层干预协议），一种四阶段渐进式方法论，从结构化定性指标——情感强度(a)和叙事动力(m)——以及ETHICS（人机交互上下文信号涌现分类法），一种“信号而非标签”分类法，推导出干预措施（无、软、硬）。一项结合小规模生产部署（N=68条目，10用户，10周）与合成角色电池测试（N=91，5种行为风险特征）的评估，实现了流动角色0%假阳性，并显示出危机导向角色中的预期升级模式。然而，初步结果显示，连续8天的高能量升高产生了零干预（0/8），暴露了“不病理化”原则与安全冲突的边界。随后的三模型压力测试表明，提高模型能力将检测率从0/8提升至6/8，同时在最大模型中保持0/10流动假阳性。初步解读，这些发现将渐进干预定位为一种设计方向，用于导航——而非解决——情感计算中的安全-融洽张力。

Original abstract: AI emotional companions face a safety-rapport paradox: restrictive safeguards can damage supportive alliance, while permissive systems risk user harm. We present SLIP (Staged Layers of Intervention Protocol), a four-stage graduated methodology deriving interventions (none, soft, hard) from structured qualitative indicators -- affect intensity (a) and narrative dynamism (m) -- alongside ETHICS (Emergent Taxonomy for Human-AI Interaction Context Signals), a "signals not labels" taxonomy. An evaluation combining a small-scale production deployment (N=68 entries, 10 users, 10 weeks) with a synthetic persona battery (N=91, 5 behavioral-risk profiles) achieved 0% false positives for the flow persona and showed expected escalation patterns in crisis-oriented personas. However, initial results showed that 8 consecutive days of high-energy elevation produced zero interventions (0/8), exposing a boundary where the "do not pathologize" principle conflicts with safety. A subsequent three-model stress test demonstrated that increased model capability improves detection from 0/8 to 6/8 while preserving 0/10 flow false positives in the largest model. Read as preliminary, these findings position graduated intervention as a design direction for navigating -- not resolving -- the safety-rapport tension in affective computing.

</details>


### [47] [Alignment Drift in Long-Term Human-LLM Interaction: A Mechanism-Oriented Framework](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16516v1)
*Xintong Yao*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: 分析长期人机交互对齐漂移机制，对agent长期任务设计有启发

TL;DR: 本文提出一个机制导向框架来描述长期人机交互中的对齐漂移现象，将其定义为递归交互过程而非模型侧失败。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏对长期交互中缓慢累积的对齐漂移现象的理解和描述机制。

Method: 提出机制导向框架，定义信号A/B区别，通过反馈循环和子模式选择解释漂移发展，划分三个交互区域并识别边界条件。

Result: 成功将对齐漂移框定为递归交互过程，为长期人机交互研究提供概念基础。

Conclusion: 对齐漂移应被视为交互层面的动态过程，而非孤立模型问题，该框架有助于未来研究和控制此类漂移。

中文摘要：长期与基于LLM的系统交互可能会产生对齐漂移：一个逐渐的过程，其中系统输出变得较少受用户当前消息的约束，而更多受到先前交互历史的影响，同时仍然显得有帮助、连贯和响应迅速。这个过程难以检测，因为用户的主观体验可能会随着系统变得更熟悉、有用和协调而改善。现有关于人-LLM交互的研究主要集中在短期任务表现、孤立输出或单实例对齐问题上，留下了缓慢且累积的交互层面动态未被充分描述。本文提出了一个机制导向的框架来描述对齐漂移。该框架定义了信号A和信号B之间的区别，解释了漂移如何通过反馈循环和子模式选择发展，将过程分为三个交互区域，并确定了控制漂移的边界条件。通过将对齐漂移框定为递归交互过程而非孤立的模型侧失败，本文为研究长期人-系统交互提供了概念基础。

Original abstract: Long-term interaction with LLM-based systems may produce alignment drift: a gradual process in which system outputs become less constrained by the user's current message and more shaped by prior interaction history, while still appearing helpful, coherent, and responsive. This process is difficult to detect because the user's subjective experience may improve as the system becomes more familiar, useful, and attuned. Existing research on human-LLM interaction has largely focused on short-term task performance, isolated outputs, or single-instance alignment problems, leaving slow and cumulative interaction-level dynamics undercharacterized. This paper proposes a mechanism-oriented framework for describing alignment drift. The framework defines the distinction between signal A and signal B, explains how drift develops through feedback loops and sub-pattern selection, divides the process into three interactional regimes, and identifies boundary conditions for controlling drift. By framing alignment drift as a recursive interactional process rather than an isolated model-side failure, the paper provides a conceptual basis for studying long-term human-system interaction.

</details>


### [48] [Toward Template-Free Explainability for Monte Carlo Tree Search](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16524v2)
*Siqi Lu,Mirsaleh Bahavarnia,Hiba Baroud,Yixuan Zhang,Hemant Purohit,Ayan Mukhopadhyay*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: 用LLM生成MCTS解释框架，涉及证据生成与树扩展，可迁移至agent可解释性

TL;DR: 提出一个利用LLM从MCTS搜索轨迹生成决策解释的端到端框架，无需手工规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MCTS解释方法需要手工构造形式逻辑约束，难以适应问题变化；用户难以直接从树统计信息理解决策。

Method: 框架将自然语言问题映射到意图类别，检查树中证据充分性，按需扩展树，并利用访问次数、值估计和风险信息生成解释。

Result: 实验首次证明LLM能端到端地解释概率搜索，无需中间形式表示。

Conclusion: LLM可作为有效的MCTS解释器，简化解释生成过程，提高适应性。

中文摘要：概率搜索算法，例如蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS），在解决不确定性下的序列决策任务中已被证明非常有效。然而，对于仅基于原始树统计信息的最终用户来说，解释结合了基于置信区间上界（bandit-based）树遍历和基于模拟的值估计的非对称搜索树是困难的。虽然先前的工作需要手工制作的正式逻辑约束，且当问题变化时必须更新，但我们提出了一个框架，使大型语言模型（LLMs）能够以端到端的方式从记录的搜索轨迹中生成基于证据的MCTS决策解释。我们的框架将自然语言问题映射到一组结构化的意图类别，确定现有树是否包含足够的证据，在需要时触发目标扩展，并使用树统计信息（如访问次数、值估计和风险信息）生成解释。实验结果首次证明，LLMs可以作为概率搜索的端到端解释器，无需中间形式表示。

Original abstract: Probabilistic search algorithms, such as Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS), have proven very effective in solving sequential decision-making tasks under uncertainty. However, interpreting asymmetric search trees that incorporate bandit-based tree traversal and simulation-based value estimation is difficult for end users based solely on raw tree statistics. While prior work requires hand-crafted formal logic constraints that must be updated when the problem changes, we present a framework that enables large language models (LLMs) to generate evidence-grounded explanations of MCTS decisions from recorded search traces in an end-to-end manner. Our framework maps natural-language questions to a structured set of intent categories, determines whether the existing tree contains sufficient evidence, triggers targeted expansion when needed, and generates explanations using tree statistics such as visit counts, value estimates, and risk information. Experimental results provide the first evidence that LLMs can serve as end-to-end explainers for probabilistic search, without requiring intermediate formal representations.

</details>

### [49] [paper.json: A Coordination Convention for LLM-Agent-Actionable Papers](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16194v1)
*Arquimedes Canedo*

Main category: cs.DL

Selection reason: 论文JSON规范便于agent读取，agent接口设计启发

TL;DR: 提出paper.json作为PDF的伴侣JSON文件，通过五个轻量级约定解决LLM代理阅读学术论文时的子声明引用、范围过度扩展和图表命令问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准散文论文导致LLM代理在阅读时出现子声明无法引用、范围过度扩展、图表命令隐藏在代码库中的问题。

Method: 提出paper.json格式，包含五个约定：C1稳定声明ID、C2明确不声明列表、C3每个图表的精确shell命令、C4最小可行合规性（手写JSON）、C5稳定定义ID。

Result: 作者自己的论文符合paper.json规范，并通过验证命令`uv run validator.py paper.json --against paper.typ`。

Conclusion: 这些约定是开放邀请，代理读取合规论文并行动会产生支持或反对证据，鼓励社区采用和验证。

中文摘要：LLM代理通常充当学术论文的第一（有时也是唯一）读者，浏览以获取子声明、提取可复现步骤并概括范围。标准散文论文在此角色中会产生反复出现的失败：无法以子论文粒度引用的子声明、超出论文测试范围的范围过度扩展、以及埋在代码库中而非论文本身的图表命令。我们提出`paper.json`，一个伴随PDF的JSON文件，通过轻量级约定解决每个失败：稳定的声明ID（C1）、明确的不声明列表（C2）、每个图表的精确shell命令（C3）和稳定的定义ID（C5）。第五个约定（C4）认为，最低可行合规性，即手写JSON与PDF并存，对于一篇完成的论文可以在不到一小时内实现，无需触及人类可读输出。C1、C2、C3和C5是开放邀请：读取合规论文并对其采取行动的代理会产生支持或反对它们的证据。本文本身是合规的：`uv run validator.py paper.json --against paper.typ`通过。仓库：https://github.com/arquicanedo/paper-json

Original abstract: LLM agents routinely serve as first (and sometimes only) readers of academic papers, skimming for sub-claims, extracting reproducibility steps, and generalizing scope. Standard prose papers produce recurring failures in this role: sub-claims that cannot be cited at sub-paper granularity, scope overextension beyond what the paper tests, and figure commands buried in codebases rather than the paper itself. We propose `paper.json`, a companion JSON file that travels with the PDF and addresses each failure with a lightweight convention: stable claim IDs (C1), an explicit does-not-claim list (C2), exact per-figure shell commands (C3), and stable definition IDs (C5). A fifth convention (C4) holds that minimum viable compliance, hand-written JSON alongside the PDF, is achievable in under an hour for a finished paper without touching the human-readable output. C1, C2, C3, and C5 are open invitations: an agent that reads a compliant paper and acts on it produces evidence for or against them. This paper is itself compliant: `uv run validator.py paper.json --against paper.typ` passes. Repo: https://github.com/arquicanedo/paper-json

</details>

# cs.IR [[Back]](#toc)

### [50] [LERA: LLM-Enhanced RAG for Ad Auction in Generative Chatbots](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16474v1)
*Haoran Sun,Xinrui Song,Xinyu Zhang,Zhaohua Chen,Xu Chu,Zhilin Zhang,Chuan Yu,Jian Xu,Bo Zheng,Xiaotie Deng*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: LLM增强RAG用于广告拍卖，含检索与排序，对agent工具使用有微弱启发但边界。

TL;DR: 提出LERA，一种两阶段检索-生成广告拍卖框架，通过嵌入粗过滤和LLM精排结合支付规则，提升广告选择准确性和多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有检索-生成范式中仅依赖文本嵌入相似度，导致商业误解和重复插入等问题，缺乏对广告有机相关性的精细评估。

Method: 两阶段框架：第一阶段嵌入相似度粗过滤候选；第二阶段用LLM生成logits作为精细相关性分数，结合出价和关键值支付规则确保真实性。

Result: 在合成基准上，LERA显著提高了广告选择准确性和插入多样性，且延迟开销可控。

Conclusion: LERA有效平衡了LLM聊天机器人中广告的商业化与用户体验，为动态对话中的多广告插入提供了可行方案。

中文摘要：将广告拍卖机制整合到基于大型语言模型（LLM）的聊天机器人中，为商业化提供了重要机遇，但在平衡相关性、效率和用户体验方面带来了独特挑战。最近，Feizi等人（2023）和Hajiaghayi等人（2024）提出了一种检索-然后生成范式，将检索和生成解耦，实现了轻量级广告插入和支付确定。然而，当前的检索仅依赖于文本嵌入相似度，可能导致商业误解和重复插入等问题。在本文中，我们提出了LERA，一种为LLM聊天机器人量身定制的两阶段检索-然后生成拍卖框架。在第一阶段，基于嵌入的粗过滤预选出一小部分候选广告商。在第二阶段，LLM本身通过精心设计的提示进行查询，生成候选上的logits，作为精细化的有机相关性分数。这些分数与出价相结合，一个关键值支付规则同时考虑了粗过滤和精细排名的阈值，确保了追求效用最大化的广告商的真实性。该框架自然地扩展到动态对话流和长回复中的多次广告插入。在合成广告商-查询基准上的实验表明，LERA在仅带来可控延迟开销的情况下，显著提高了广告选择准确性和插入多样性。

Original abstract: The integration of advertising auction mechanisms into large language model (LLM)-based chatbots presents a significant opportunity for commercialization, yet poses unique challenges in balancing relevance, efficiency, and user experience. Recently, Feizi et al.~\citep{feizi2023online} and Hajiaghayi et al.~\citep{hajiaghayi2024ad} outlined a retrieve-then-generate paradigm that decouples retrieval and generation, offering lightweight ad insertion and payment determination. However, current retrieval relies solely on text embedding similarity, which may lead to commercial misinterpretation and issues such as repetitive insertions. In this paper, we propose LERA, a two-stage retrieve-then-generate auction framework tailored for LLM chatbots. In the first stage, embedding-based coarse filtering pre-selects a small set of candidate advertisers. In the second stage, the LLM itself is queried with a carefully designed prompt to produce logits over candidates, which serve as refined organic relevance scores. These scores are combined with bids, and a critical-value payment rule accounts for both the coarse-filtering and fine-ranking thresholds, ensuring truthfulness for utility-maximizing advertisers. The framework naturally extends to multiple ad insertions within dynamic dialogue flows and long responses. Experiments on a synthetic advertiser-query benchmark show that LERA substantially improves ad selection accuracy and insertion diversity while incurring only controllable latency overhead.

</details>

# cs.NI [[Back]](#toc)

### [51] [Optimization-as-a-Service via Multi-Agent Large Language Model for Radio Access Networks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20590v1)
*Chaoqun You,Yueyue Dai,Xingqiu He,Yue Gao,Rahim Tafazolli,Yong Liang Guan*

Main category: cs.NI

Selection reason: 多智能体LLM用于RAN优化，含反射蒸馏，通用多agent方法。

TL;DR: 提出基于LLM多智能体系统的OaaS框架，通过场景理解、目标生成、求解器和反思智能体实现PRB分配，并引入一次性反思蒸馏降低延迟，实现接近最优分配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统PRB分配方法（手动或AI）无法适应6G RAN的高动态性和多样性，需要灵活自适应的通用解决方案。

Method: 构建LLM-MA系统，包含场景理解、目标生成、求解器和反思智能体，采用一次性反射蒸馏训练轻量级学生模型替代迭代反射。

Result: 实现接近最优的资源分配，且推理延迟极低。

Conclusion: 基于LLM-MA的OaaS框架能有效应对6G RAN的挑战，提供自适应、低延迟的资源分配方案。

中文摘要：在无线接入网络（RAN）中，物理资源块（PRB）的分配传统上依赖于逐案例的手动问题构建，或者最近依赖于基于学习的人工智能（AI）方法。然而，第六代（6G）RAN环境面临着前所未有的服务多样性和指数级动态变化，包括活跃基站（BS）、用户规模的剧烈波动以及严格的服务质量（QoS）要求。在这种条件下，手动模型和标准AI算法都显得僵化，缺乏适应和自我演化的灵活性。为了提供一种通用的解决方案，我们提出将PRB分配问题视为一种由大型语言模型多智能体（LLM-MA）系统提供的优化即服务（OaaS）。这通过利用智能体动态构建优化问题并自动确定适应实时场景的目标，从根本上重塑了RAN资源分配。我们的闭环架构集成了场景理解、目标生成、求解器和反思智能体，实现了上下文感知、自我纠正的公式化。为了消除迭代反思的计算延迟，我们引入了一种一次性反思蒸馏机制，训练一个轻量级学生模型直接预测精炼的目标参数。我们从理论上界定了这种一次性策略的性能差距。实验结果表明，我们的框架实现了接近最优的资源分配，且推理延迟极低。

Original abstract: The physical resource block (PRB) allocation in Radio Access Networks (RANs) traditionally relies on case-by-case manual problem construction or, more recently, learning-based artificial intelligence (AI) methods. However, the sixth-generation (6G) RAN environments confront unprecedented service diversity and exponential dynamics, featuring volatile fluctuations in active base stations (BSs), user scale, and stringent Quality-of-Service (QoS) requirements. Faced with such conditions, both manual models and standard AI algorithms remain fundamentally rigid, lacking the flexibility to adapt and self-evolve. To provide a one-size-fits-all solution, we propose treating the PRB allocation problem as an Optimization-as-a-Service (OaaS) provided by a large language model multi-agent (LLM-MA) system. This fundamentally reshapes RAN resource allocation by utilizing agents to dynamically construct optimization problems and automatically determine objectives tailored to real-time scenarios. Our closed-loop architecture, integrating scene understanding, objective generation, solver, and reflection agents, enables context-aware, self-correcting formulation. To eliminate the computational latency of iterative reflection, we introduce a one-shot reflection distillation mechanism, training a lightweight student model to directly predict refined objective parameters. We theoretically bound the performance gap of this one-shot policy. Experimental results demonstrate our framework achieves near-optimal resource allocation with ultra-low inference latency.

</details>

# cs.MA [[Back]](#toc)

### [52] [GRASP: Graph Agentic Search over Propositions for Multi-hop Question Answering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16598v1)
*Stockton Jenkins,Ramya Korlakai Vinayak,Junjie Hu*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多跳问答的agentic检索系统，含规划和效率优化，可迁移到coding agent。

TL;DR: GRASP通过分层图智能搜索，在多跳问答中同时实现了高准确率和低令牌消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能检索结合知识图谱的方法在索引构建和推理令牌使用上成本高昂，需要一种更高效的方案来平衡准确率和成本。

Method: GRASP将多跳问题分解为依赖感知的计划，动态调整子智能体数量，每个子智能体使用三层层次图（实体、命题、段落），通过实体层进行目标遍历，并通过命题层的倒数排名投票实现高召回率段落检索。

Result: 在开放检索设置下，GRASP在MuSiQue和2Wiki上达到最高准确率，令牌使用比IRCoT+HippoRAG2减少40-50%；在LongBench设置下，GRASP在所有三个数据集上EM和F1领先，令牌比次优方法减少30%。

Conclusion: 提出成功经济性指标（按难度加权的每正确回答摊销令牌成本），并倡导将效率感知评估作为智能问答的标准实践。

中文摘要：智能检索通过赋予语言模型自主迭代收集证据的能力，改进了多跳问答。最近的工作通过知识图谱增强这些系统以进行结构化遍历，但这种组合引入了显著的成本：索引时昂贵的图构建和推理时不断增加的令牌使用。我们提出了基于命题的图智能搜索（GRASP），这是一个在多跳问答中同时优化高精度和最小令牌使用的智能系统。GRASP不是执行僵硬的单一查询，而是通过将多跳查询分解为依赖感知的计划来主动协调其检索策略。这使得GRASP能够根据问题的复杂程度动态调整子智能体的数量。每个子智能体通过探索一个新颖的三层层次图（实体、命题和段落）来解决其单跳查询，利用实体层进行目标遍历，利用命题层通过倒数排名投票进行高召回率的段落检索。我们在MuSiQue、2WikiMultihopQA和HotpotQA上评估了GRASP，在开放语料库检索和扩展上下文推理（LongBench）两种设置下。在开放检索设置下，GRASP在MuSiQue和2Wiki上实现了最高的QA准确率，同时使用的令牌比IRCoT+HippoRAG2少40-50%。此外，在LongBench设置下，GRASP在所有三个数据集上的EM和F1指标上领先，同时使用的令牌比次优方法少30%。最后，我们引入了成功经济性——每个正确答案的摊销令牌成本，按难度加权——并倡导将效率感知评估作为智能问答的标准实践。

Original abstract: Agentic retrieval improves multi-hop question answering by giving language models autonomy to iteratively gather evidence. Recent work augments these systems with knowledge graphs for structured traversal, but this combination introduces significant cost: expensive graph construction at index time and compounding token usage at inference time. We introduce Graph Agentic Search over Propositions (GRASP), an agentic system that simultaneously optimizes for high accuracy and minimal token usage in multi-hop question answering. Rather than executing a rigid, singular query, GRASP actively coordinates its retrieval strategy by decomposing multi-hop queries into dependency-aware plans. This enables GRASP to dynamically scale the number of sub-agents according to the complexity of the problem. Each sub-agent resolves its single-hop query by exploring a novel three-layer hierarchical graph of entities, propositions, and passages, using the entity layer for targeted traversal and the proposition layer for high-recall passage retrieval via reciprocal-rank voting. We evaluate GRASP on MuSiQue, 2WikiMultihopQA, and HotpotQA under two settings: open-corpus retrieval and extended context reasoning (LongBench). GRASP achieves the highest QA accuracy in the open retrieval setting on MuSiQue and 2Wiki while using 40-50 percent fewer tokens than IRCoT+HippoRAG2. Furthermore, GRASP leads on EM and F1 across all three datasets in the LongBench setting while using 30 percent fewer tokens than the next most accurate method. Finally, we introduce success economy - the amortized token cost per correct answer, weighted by difficulty - and advocate for efficiency-aware evaluation as a standard practice for agentic QA.

</details>

### [53] [Detecting Privilege Escalation in Polyglot Microservices via Agentic Program Analysis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15569v1)
*Penghui Li,Hong Yau Chong,Yinzhi Cao,Junfeng Yang*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出Neo框架，结合LLM和经典程序分析，通过智能体动态规划与代码搜索，有效检测微服务权限提升漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微服务架构导致复杂权限控制，跨服务、多语言交互使现有检测方法难以高效发现权限提升漏洞。

Method: 基于LLM智能体动态生成分析计划，结合代码搜索原语实现跨服务、跨语言的灵活代码探索与语义验证。

Result: 在25个微服务应用（620万行代码，7种语言）中检测出24个零日漏洞，精确率81%，召回率85%，优于现有方法。

Conclusion: Neo能有效检测微服务权限提升漏洞，且具有良好可扩展性，可推广至其他领域和漏洞类型。

中文摘要：由于可扩展性和容错性，微服务在现代云系统中被广泛采用。然而，微服务架构在权限和许可控制方面引入了显著的复杂性，产生了权限提升的风险，攻击者可以未经授权访问资源或操作。由于复杂的跨服务交互、多语言代码库以及多样化的特权操作和权限检查，检测此类漏洞具有挑战性。我们提出了Neo，一个结合大语言模型（LLM）与经典程序分析的智能程序分析框架，以应对这些挑战。Neo利用基于LLM的智能体动态生成分析计划、调整代码搜索策略并验证语义。我们开发了代码搜索原语，使Neo能够在跨服务和跨语言之间进行可扩展且灵活的代码探索。我们在涵盖7种编程语言和620万行代码的25个开源微服务应用上评估了Neo。Neo发现了24个零日权限提升漏洞，并在真实数据集上实现了81.0%的精确率和85.0%的召回率。与现有的程序分析和智能体解决方案相比，Neo在检测准确性和可扩展性方面都有显著改进。我们还通过将Neo应用于其他应用领域和漏洞类型，展示了其可扩展性，进一步发现了18个额外的零日漏洞。

Original abstract: Microservices are widely adopted in modern cloud systems due to their scalability and fault tolerance. However, microservice architectures introduce significant complexity in privilege and permission control, creating risks of privilege escalation where attackers can gain unauthorized access to resources or operations. Detecting such vulnerabilities is challenging due to complex cross-service interactions, polyglot codebases, and diverse privileged operations and permission checks. We present Neo, an agentic program analysis framework that combines large language models (LLMs) with classic program analysis to address these challenges. Neo leverages an LLM-based agent that dynamically generates analysis plans, adapts code search strategies, and validates semantics. We develop code search primitives that enable Neo to perform scalable and flexible code exploration across services and languages. We evaluated Neo on 25 open-source microservice applications spanning 7 programming languages and 6.2 million lines of code. Neo uncovered 24 zero-day privilege escalation vulnerabilities and achieved 81.0% precision and 85.0% recall on a ground-truth dataset. Compared to existing program analysis and agentic solutions, Neo demonstrated significant improvements in both detection accuracy and scalability. We further showcased Neo's extensibility by applying it to other application domains and vulnerability types, uncovering 18 additional zero-day vulnerabilities.

</details>


### [54] [Compositional Jailbreaking: An Empirical Analysis of Mutator Chain Interactions in Aligned LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15598v1)
*Reinelle Jan Bugnot,Soohyeon Choi,Hoon Wei Lim,Yue Duan*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文系统研究越狱攻击中突变子链接的相互作用，发现大部分组合效果不佳，但少数产生协同效应，并揭示安全对齐的结构特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究忽略了简单攻击之间的组合交互，本文旨在探索弱越狱变换的顺序组合如何影响攻击效果。

Method: 实现12个基线突变子，在有害提示基准上对三种LLM评估所有有序对，并引入完整性和有效性指标。

Result: 大多数组合表现出破坏性干扰或结构不兼容，少数组合产生协同效应提高攻击成功率；失败模式揭示了安全对齐的结构特性。

Conclusion: 研究发现对抗性提示组合的微妙动态，为构建更稳健的安全防御提供新见解。

中文摘要：针对大语言模型的越狱攻击通过生成有害或受限内容对AI安全构成了重大威胁。虽然先前的工作已经探索了手工制作和自动化的越狱策略，但简单攻击之间的组合交互潜力仍未得到充分探索。本文对突变子链进行了系统研究，其中弱越狱变换被顺序应用以表征它们如何相互作用：是相互增强、破坏性干扰还是不产生有意义的变化。我们实现了十二个基线突变子，并在一个包含有害提示的基准上对三种流行的大语言模型评估了所有有序对。我们的框架引入了完整性和有效性指标，同时捕获了变换的持久性和攻击的有效性。结果表明，交互格局高度不均匀，大多数组合未能优于单个突变子，表现出破坏性干扰或结构不兼容，而一小部分产生了协同效应，提高了攻击成功率。同样重要的是，普遍的失败模式揭示了安全对齐的结构特性，这些特性在单策略评估中并不明显。这些发现突显了对抗性提示组合的微妙动态，并为构建更稳健的安全防御提供了新见解。

Original abstract: Jailbreaking attacks on large language models pose a significant threat to AI safety by enabling the generation of harmful or restricted content. While prior work has explored both handcrafted and automated jailbreak strategies, the potential for compositional interaction between simple attacks remains underexplored. This paper presents a systematic study of mutator chaining, in which weak jailbreak transformations are applied sequentially to characterize how they interact: whether they reinforce one another, interfere destructively, or produce no meaningful change. We implement twelve baseline mutators and evaluate all ordered pairs on a benchmark of harmful prompts against three popular LLM models. Our framework introduces metrics for completeness and validity that capture both transformation persistence and attack effectiveness. Results reveal that the interaction landscape is highly non-uniform, while most combinations fail to outperform individual mutators, exhibiting destructive interference or structural incompatibility, a small fraction produce synergistic effects that improve attack success rates. Equally important, the prevalent failure modes reveal structural properties of safety alignment that are not apparent from single-strategy evaluations. These findings highlight the nuanced dynamics of adversarial prompt composition and offer new insights for building more robust safety defenses.

</details>


### [55] [Who Owns This Agent? Tracing AI Agents Back to Their Owners](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16035v1)
*Ruben Chocron,Doron Jonathan Ben Chayim,Eyal Lenga,Gilad Gressel,Alina Oprea,Yisroel Mirsky*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 研究AI agent归属追踪与安全协议，直接涉及agent安全控制，可迁移到coding agent的安全性设计。

TL;DR: 提出了首个AI代理归因协议，通过注入金丝雀将代理交互链接到部署账户，即使面对对抗性操作者也具有鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI代理自主行动时缺乏归因机制，导致良性误配置和恶意攻击都无法追踪到责任账户，造成问责缺口。

Method: 基于金丝雀的协议：授权方在代理交互流中注入不可压制且不影响任务性能的金丝雀，供应商通过搜索会话日志恢复账户。

Result: 在各种场景（包括真实世界代理）中验证了方法可靠、鲁棒且可扩展，对抗性环境下仍有效。

Conclusion: 该归因协议能有效弥补AI代理的问责缺口，适合供应商端部署，且防御者具有形式上的不对称优势。

中文摘要：AI代理越来越多地被部署到世界中自主行动，但至今仍没有可靠的方法将有害代理追溯到部署它的账户。这在意图范围的两端都造成了同样的问责差距：良性操作者可能部署配置错误或过于宽泛的代理，无意中造成伤害，而恶意操作者可能故意将代理武器化用于诈骗、骚扰或网络攻击。在许多情况下，这些代理由供应商托管的模型驱动，即使是复杂的对手（例如进行网络操作的国家行为者）也依赖于此。无论哪种情况，受影响方可以观察到行为，但无法通知负责任的操作者、停止会话或识别账户进行调查。我们将这一差距形式化为代理归因问题：将观察到的代理交互链接到托管供应商处的责任账户。据我们所知，这是首次定义该问题并提出实用解决方案的工作。我们的协议基于金丝雀：授权方将金丝雀注入代理的交互流中，供应商在会话日志的狭窄窗口中搜索以恢复原始会话和账户。在非对抗性环境下，简单的金丝雀就足够了。对于过滤或改写传入内容的对抗性操作者，我们开发了稳健的金丝雀构造，这些构造无法在不降低代理自身任务性能的情况下被压制，从而在防御者一方形成了正式的不对称。我们评估了包括真实世界代理在内的各种场景，并表明我们的归因方法可靠、稳健且可扩展，适合供应商端部署。

Original abstract: AI agents are increasingly deployed to act autonomously in the world, yet there is still no reliable way to trace a harmful agent back to the account that deployed it. This creates the same accountability gap across both ends of the intent spectrum: benign operators may deploy misconfigured or overbroad agents that cause harm unintentionally, while malicious operators may deliberately weaponize agents for scams, harassment, or cyber attacks. In many cases, these agents are powered by vendor-hosted models, a dependency that holds even for sophisticated adversaries such as state actors conducting cyber operations. In either case, affected parties can observe the behavior but cannot notify the responsible operator, stop the session, or identify the account for investigation.
  We formalize this gap as the problem of agent attribution: linking an observed agent interaction to the responsible account at the hosting vendor. To our knowledge, this is the first work to define the problem and present a practical solution. Our protocol is canary-based: an authorized party injects a canary into the agent's interaction stream, and the vendor searches a narrow window of session logs to recover the originating session and account. Simple canaries suffice in non-adversarial settings. For adversarial operators who filter or paraphrase incoming content, we develop robust canary constructions that cannot be suppressed without degrading the agent's own task performance, yielding a formal asymmetry in the defender's favor. We evaluate a variety of scenarios including real-world agents and show that our attribution method is reliable, robust, and scalable for vendor-side deployment.

</details>


### [56] [From Backup Restoration to Minimum Viable Factory Recovery: A Systematization of Ransomware Recovery in Manufacturing Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16167v1)
*Chun Yin Chiu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过PRISMA引导的多声音回顾识别出九个恢复失败模式，并提出MVF恢复概念作为分析目标，为关键制造基础设施的勒索软件恢复提供了证据校准的基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 勒索软件恢复不仅是备份问题，还涉及生产系统中多个耦合系统的依赖关系，现有方法忽视了这一复杂性。

Method: 采用PRISMA引导的多声音回顾方法，综合分析学术文献、标准、政府指南、威胁框架、公开事件及证据锚点。

Result: 识别出九个恢复失败模式，并定义了最小可行工厂恢复（MVF恢复）的概念。

Conclusion: 本文为关键制造基础设施中基于能力的勒索软件恢复提供了证据校准的基础，并推导出恢复生命周期和基准测试方向。

中文摘要：在关键制造基础设施中，勒索软件恢复不仅仅是一个备份恢复问题。生产能力依赖于信息-技术、操作-技术、物理过程、质量、物流、身份和供应商系统的耦合。遭受勒索软件攻击后，工厂可能重建了服务器，但仍然无法安排工作、认证操作员、信任工程工作站、发布产品、重新连接OT资产或协调供应商。本文将制造勒索软件恢复重新定义为关键基础设施连续性和相互依赖性问题。我们进行了一项PRISMA引导的多声音回顾，涉及学术文献、标准和政府指南、威胁框架、公开事件材料以及经过验证的全文/源页面证据锚点。回顾识别出九个证据支持的恢复失败模式：依赖盲区、不信任的恢复点和备份过度信任、身份信任崩溃、缺乏恢复证明、不安全的OT重连、分段假设失效、能力不匹配、未管理的降级运行以及供应商依赖失效。然后我们引入了最小可行工厂恢复（MVF恢复）：在当前的依赖、证据、身份、数据、网络、OT和供应商约束下，可以恢复的最小的安全、可信且具有操作意义的生产能力。MVF恢复是一个分析目标，而不是完全恢复、实施或安全认证的声明。本文推导出恢复生命周期和基准测试方向作为次要输出。贡献是为关键制造基础设施中基于能力的勒索软件恢复提供了一个经过证据校准的基础。

Original abstract: Ransomware recovery in critical manufacturing infrastructure is not only a backup-restoration problem. Production capability depends on coupled information-technology, operational-technology, physical-process, quality, logistics, identity, and supplier systems. After ransomware, a plant may rebuild servers yet remain unable to schedule work, authenticate operators, trust engineering workstations, release product, reconnect OT assets, or coordinate suppliers. This paper reframes manufacturing ransomware recovery as a critical-infrastructure continuity and interdependency problem. We conduct a PRISMA-guided multivocal review of academic literature, standards and government guidance, threat frameworks, public incident material, and verified full-text/source-page evidence anchors. The review identifies nine evidence-backed recovery failure modes: dependency blindness, untrusted restore point and backup over-trust, identity trust collapse, lack of proof-of-recovery, unsafe OT reconnection, segmentation assumption failure, capability mismatch, unmanaged degraded operation, and supplier dependency failure. We then introduce Minimum Viable Factory Recovery (MVF Recovery): the smallest safe, trusted, and operationally meaningful production capability that can be resumed under current dependency, evidence, identity, data, network, OT, and supplier constraints. MVF Recovery is an analytical objective rather than a claim of full recovery, implementation, or safety certification. The paper derives a recovery lifecycle and benchmarking directions as secondary outputs. The contribution is an evidence-calibrated foundation for capability-centric ransomware recovery in critical manufacturing infrastructure.

</details>


### [57] [SLEIGHT-Bench: A Benchmark of Evasion Attacks Against Agent Monitors](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16626v2)
*Elle Najt,Colin Toft,Tyler Tracy,Fabien Roger,Joe Benton*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: LLM agent监控逃避攻击的benchmark，直接涉及agent安全与评估。

TL;DR: 提出了SLEIGHT-Bench基准，评估LLM监控器对编码智能体有害行为的检测能力，发现现有监控器在低误报率下对一半攻击无法捕获，并揭示了多种规避策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主编码智能体可能产生危险的不一致行为，需用LLM监控其行动；但监控器面对多样化攻击策略的局限性尚不明确，因此需要系统评估。

Method: 构建包含11类40个合成攻击交互记录的SLEIGHT-Bench基准，测试Opus 4.6监控器在不同条件下的检测效果，并实验比较编码智能体作为监控器与常规提示监控器的性能。

Result: 40个攻击中20个在1%误报率下从未被捕获，总体捕获率32%；识别出利用模型先验、指令模糊性和状态操纵等规避策略；编码智能体作为监控器表现更好，针对性提示可提高部分策略的捕获率。

Conclusion: 现有前沿监控器对编码智能体的隐蔽攻击检测能力有限，需进一步研究更强监控器和防御策略；数据集和框架已开源。

中文摘要：由于自主编码智能体以高容量生成复杂行为，我们可能希望使用其他大语言模型来监控其行动，以减少危险的不一致行为带来的风险。为了更好地理解此类监控器在面对编码智能体可能使用的多样化攻击策略时的局限性，我们提出了SLEIGHT-Bench（微妙低迭代洞察引导的有害交互记录），这是一个包含40个攻击（分为11个类别）的合成交互记录基准，每个攻击展示了一个编码智能体暗中追求有害目标（例如权重泄露、凭据窃取、未监控的恶意部署）。我们发现，在Opus 4.6监控器（具有扩展思维功能）以1%误报率进行10次试验中，40个攻击中有20个从未被捕获，而总体捕获率为32%。我们识别了几种规避策略，例如利用模型先验、用户指令模糊性和状态操纵，这些策略有助于创建能够避开前沿监控器的攻击。我们还发现，使用编码智能体作为监控器相比常规提示监控器能获得更强的监控性能，并且针对某些规避策略，使用有针对性的监控提示能提高捕获率。我们的数据集和评估框架可在https://github.com/safety-research/sleight-bench和https://huggingface.co/datasets/sleightbench/SLEIGHT-Bench获取。

Original abstract: Since autonomous coding agents generate complex behaviors at high-volume, we may want to use other LLMs to monitor actions to reduce the risk from dangerous misaligned behavior. To better understand the limitations of such monitors against the diverse attack strategies that a coding agent could use, we present SLEIGHT-Bench (Subtle Low-itEration Insight-Guided Harmful Transcripts), a benchmark of synthetic transcripts containing 40 attacks across 11 categories, each showing a coding agent covertly pursuing a harmful objective (e.g. weight exfiltration, credential theft, unmonitored rogue deployment). We find that 20 of 40 attacks are never caught by an Opus 4.6 monitor with extended thinking across 10 trials at a 1% false-positive rate, while the overall catch rate is 32%. We identify several evasion strategies such as exploiting model priors, user instruction ambiguity, and state manipulation, which facilitate creating attacks that evade frontier monitors. We also elicit stronger monitor performance using coding agents as monitors versus regular prompted monitors, and for some evasion strategies show improved catch rates with targeted monitor prompts. Our dataset and evaluation framework are available at https://github.com/safety-research/sleight-bench and https://huggingface.co/datasets/sleightbench/SLEIGHT-Bench.

### [58] [PrivScope: Task-scoped Disclosure Control for Hybrid Agentic Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16630v2)
*Shafizur Rahman Seeam,Zhengxiong Li,Zhiyuan Yu,Yimin,Chen,Yidan Hu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 混合agent系统的隐私控制框架，涉及任务范围披露，可迁移。

TL;DR: PrivScope是一个设备上的负载控制器，通过任务范围披露在不影响云任务成功率的前提下，显著降低用户信息过度披露和重识别风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合本地-云代理在向云语言模型发送请求时，会暴露不必要的敏感信息（过度披露），现有方案无法有效处理本地-云组装的负载范围。

Method: PrivScope在设备上提取披露单元，保留直接标识符和账户关联值，对必须上云的单元进行云必要性控制和最低特异性抽象。

Result: 在100个医疗预约工作流程中，消除个人资料泄漏（0.0% vs. 17.7%），重识别率从64.3%降至23.1%，保持高候选召回率且任务成功率接近基线，仅增加数秒延迟。

Conclusion: PrivScope能有效控制本地-云边界的信息披露，兼顾隐私保护和任务效用，且无需修改云侧。

中文摘要：混合本地-云代理在将能力密集型子任务委托给云语言模型（CLM）之前，用持久工作状态的上下文丰富用户请求。虽然这种丰富可以提高任务成功率，但它也会在发送到云的负载中暴露不必要的信息，包括与任务无关的上下文、先前工作流程遗留的信息以及过于具体的敏感细节，从而导致“过度披露”。现有解决方案要么隔离工作流程以限制跨工作流程泄漏，要么应用通用净化，但无法对本地-云组装的负载范围进行推理。我们提出了PrivScope，一个受信任的设备上负载控制器，它在本地-CLM边界强制实施“任务范围披露”，而无需云侧更改。其关键思想是：敏感信息仅在委托子任务需要时才应到达云，并且仅以保持效用的最低揭示形式呈现。PrivScope从组装的负载中提取披露单元，并将直接标识符和账户关联值保留在设备上。其余单元经过云必要性控制，确定实际需要的内容；必须到达云的单元被抽象为足以完成任务的最低特异性表示。在三个商业CLM上的100个医疗预约工作流程中，PrivScope消除了个人资料泄漏（0.0% vs. 17.7%），使攻击者重识别率降低超过一半（23.1% vs. 64.3%），并在每个测试的CLM上实现了最高的候选召回率，同时在GPT-4o-mini和Gemini 2.5 Flash上将任务成功率保持在接近未受保护基线的水平。这些收益在五个本地骨干模型上均成立，并且在商用硬件上仅增加了几秒的设备延迟。

Original abstract: Hybrid local--cloud agents enrich user requests with context from persistent working state before delegating capability-intensive subtasks to a cloud language model (CLM). While this enrichment can improve task success, it also exposes unnecessary information in the cloud-bound payload, including task-irrelevant context, carryover from prior workflows, and overly specific sensitive details, resulting in \emph{over-disclosure}. Existing solutions either isolate workflows to limit cross-workflow leakage or apply general-purpose sanitization that does not reason over LC-assembled payload scope.
  We present \textsc{PrivScope}, a trusted on-device payload governor that enforces \emph{task-scoped disclosure} at the local--CLM boundary, without requiring cloud-side changes. Its key idea: sensitive information should reach the cloud only when required for the delegated subtask, and then only in the least revealing form preserving utility. \textsc{PrivScope} extracts disclosure units from the assembled payload and keeps direct identifiers and account-linked values on device. The remaining units pass through cloud-necessity control, which determines what is actually needed; units that must reach the cloud are abstracted to the least-specific representation sufficient for the task. On 100 medical-booking workflows across three commercial CLMs, \textsc{PrivScope} eliminates profile leakage (0.0\% vs.\ 17.7\%), more than halves attacker re-identification (23.1\% vs.\ 64.3\%), and achieves the highest candidate recall on every CLM tested while preserving task success close to the unprotected baseline on GPT-4o-mini and Gemini 2.5 Flash. Gains hold across five local backbones and add only seconds of on-device latency on commodity hardware.

</details>
