### [59] [RoPE Distinguishes Neither Positions Nor Tokens in Long Contexts, Provably](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15514v1)
*Yufeng Du,Phillip Harris,Minyang Tian,Eliu A Huerta,Srikanth Ronanki,Subendhu Rongali,Aram Galstyan,Hao Peng*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: RoPE位置编码极限分析，对长上下文agent架构有理论指导价值

TL;DR: RoPE在长上下文中失去局部性和一致性，性能趋近随机；调整基参数无法兼顾位置与标记区分，需要新机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长上下文模型中RoPE存在局限性，需理论分析其根本原因。

Method: 理论分析（抽象上下文内容，仅依赖长度）；证明RoPE失效的数学性质；实证验证多头多层架构无法克服。

Result: 随上下文增长，RoPE注意力不可预测，失去局部性偏差和一致性，失败概率接近0.5；位置与标记区分无法同时优化；增大基参数仅改善标记区分但牺牲位置区分。

Conclusion: 未来长上下文模型需要根本性的位置编码新机制。

中文摘要：我们识别了基于Transformer的长上下文语言模型中旋转位置嵌入（RoPE）的内在局限性。我们的理论分析抽象掉上下文的具体内容，仅依赖于其长度。我们证明，随着上下文长度增加，基于RoPE的注意力变得不可预测，并失去两个对其有效性至关重要的特性。第一，它失去局部性偏差：RoPE不再更倾向于更近的位置而非远得多的位置。第二，它失去标记相关性的一致性：在同一位置获得比另一个更高注意力分数的关键向量可能在另一位置获得较低分数。在两种情况下，失败概率接近0.5，与随机猜测无异。我们进一步证明，当关键标记被移动到不同位置，甚至被不同标记替换时，注意力分数可以保持不变，表明无法区分位置或标记。调整RoPE基会在区分位置和区分标记之间权衡，但无法同时保留两者。增加RoPE基超参数（当前长上下文模型的常见做法）有助于区分不同标记，但不可避免地牺牲区分位置的能力。我们的实证分析表明，多头、多层架构不足以克服这些局限性。我们的研究结果表明，未来的Transformer长上下文语言模型可能需要根本性的位置和标记顺序编码新机制。

Original abstract: We identify intrinsic limitations of Rotary Positional Embeddings (RoPE) in Transformer-based long-context language models. Our theoretical analysis abstracts away from the specific content of the context and depends only on its length. We prove that as context length increases, RoPE-based attention becomes unpredictable and loses two properties that are central to its effectiveness. First, it loses its locality bias: RoPE is no more likely to favor nearer positions than substantially farther ones. Second, it loses consistency in token relevance: a key vector that receives a higher attention score than an alternative at one position may receive a lower score at another. In both cases, the probability of failure approaches 0.5, no better than random guessing. We further prove that the attention score can remain unchanged when a key token is moved to a different position, or even replaced by a different token, indicating a failure to distinguish positions or tokens. Adjusting the RoPE base trades off distinguishing positions against distinguishing tokens but cannot preserve both at the same time. Increasing the RoPE base hyperparameter, a common practice in today's long-context models, helps distinguish different tokens, but inevitably sacrifices the ability to distinguish positions. Our empirical analysis shows that multi-head, multi-layer architectures are insufficient to overcome these limitations. Our findings suggest that fundamentally new mechanisms for encoding position and token order may be needed in future Transformer long-context language models.

</details>


### [60] [Process Rewards with Learned Reliability](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15529v1)
*Jinyuan Li,Langlin Huang,Chengsong Huang,Shaoyang Xu,Donghong Cai,Yuyi Yang,Wenxuan Zhang,Jiaxin Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 过程奖励模型可靠性学习，直接支持agent自我改进与推理优化

TL;DR: 提出BetaPRM，通过预测步骤奖励的可靠性信号，结合自适应计算分配，提升推理效率和准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前PRM只输出单一点估计的奖励分数，没有可靠性指示，导致下游方法无法区分可靠与不可靠的步骤奖励，从而影响决策质量。

Method: 提出BetaPRM，利用Beta-Binomial分布建模步骤成功概率及其可靠性（预测成功率的同时给出置信度）；并基于此可靠性信号设计自适应计算分配（ACA），在推理过程中动态决定何时停止或继续计算。

Result: 在四个骨干网络和四个推理基准上，BetaPRM改进了PRM引导的Best-of-N选择；ACA相比固定预算Best-of-16减少了高达33.57%的令牌使用，同时提高了最终答案准确率。

Conclusion: BetaPRM通过提供可靠性信号增强了PRM的实用性，ACA在精度与效率之间实现了更好的权衡，展示了可靠性信号在下游任务中的价值。

中文摘要：过程奖励模型(PRMs)为推理提供步骤级反馈，但当前的PRMs通常只为每个步骤输出一个单一的奖励分数。因此，下游方法必须将不完美的步骤级奖励预测视为可靠的决策信号，而没有指示这些预测何时应该被信任。我们提出BetaPRM，一种分布式的PRM，它同时预测步骤级的成功概率和该预测的可靠性。给定来自蒙特卡洛延续的步骤成功监督，BetaPRM学习一个Beta信念，通过Beta-Binomial似然解释观察到的成功延续次数，而不是回归到有限样本成功比率作为点目标。这种学习到的可靠性信号指示何时应该信任步骤奖励，使得下游应用能够区分可靠的奖励和不确定的奖励。作为一项应用，我们引入了用于PRM引导的Best-of-N推理的自适应计算分配(ACA)。ACA使用学习到的可靠性信号，在可靠的高奖励解时停止，并在不确定的候选前缀上花费额外的计算。在四个骨干网络和四个推理基准上的实验表明，BetaPRM改进了PRM引导的Best-of-N选择，同时保留了标准的步骤级错误检测。基于此信号，ACA改进了与固定预算Best-of-16相比的准确率-令牌权衡，减少了高达33.57%的令牌使用，同时提高了最终答案的准确率。

Original abstract: Process Reward Models (PRMs) provide step-level feedback for reasoning, but current PRMs usually output only a single reward score for each step. Downstream methods must therefore treat imperfect step-level reward predictions as reliable decision signals, with no indication of when these predictions should be trusted. We propose BetaPRM, a distributional PRM that predicts both a step-level success probability and the reliability of that prediction. Given step-success supervision from Monte Carlo continuations, BetaPRM learns a Beta belief that explains the observed number of successful continuations through a Beta-Binomial likelihood, rather than regressing to the finite-sample success ratio as a point target. This learned reliability signal indicates when a step reward should be trusted, enabling downstream applications to distinguish reliable rewards from uncertain ones. As one application, we introduce Adaptive Computation Allocation (ACA) for PRM-guided Best-of-N reasoning. ACA uses the learned reliability signal to stop when a high-reward solution is reliable and to spend additional computation on uncertain candidate prefixes. Experiments across four backbones and four reasoning benchmarks show that BetaPRM improves PRM-guided Best-of-N selection while preserving standard step-level error detection. Built on this signal, ACA improves the accuracy--token tradeoff over fixed-budget Best-of-16, reducing token usage by up to 33.57% while improving final-answer accuracy.

</details>


### [61] [H-Mem: A Novel Memory Mechanism for Evolving and Retrieving Agent Memory via a Hybrid Structure](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15701v1)
*Jiawei Yu,Yixiang Fang,Xilin Liu,Yuchi Ma*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: LLM agent混合记忆机制，直接相关于agent记忆与检索，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: H-Mem是一种混合结构记忆机制，通过时间语义树和知识图谱有效建模记忆演变并实现高效检索，在三个基准上达到SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法缺乏有效建模记忆随时间演化和高效检索的机制，导致记忆利用性能差。

Method: 提出H-Mem，构建时间和语义树结构使短期记忆演变为长期记忆，同时构建知识图谱捕捉实体关系，并提供基于混合结构的检索方法。

Result: 在三个智能体记忆基准上，H-Mem在问答任务上达到最先进性能。

Conclusion: H-Mem通过混合结构有效提升记忆建模和检索，为智能体QA任务提供了新方案。

中文摘要：在基于大型语言模型（LLM）的智能体（例如OpenClaw和Manus）中，记忆数据无处不在。最近的一些工作尝试利用智能体的记忆来提升其在问答（QA）任务上的性能，但缺乏有效建模记忆数据随时间演变和高效检索记忆数据的原理性机制，导致记忆利用性能不佳。为填补这一空白，我们提出H-Mem，一种通过混合结构实现的新颖记忆机制，它不仅能有效建模智能体记忆在长时间跨度内的演变，还能提供高效的记忆检索方法。具体来说，H-Mem构建了一个时间和语义树结构，使得短期记忆数据能够逐步演变为长期记忆数据，后者提供前者的摘要信息，同时构建知识图谱以捕捉记忆中实体之间的关系。此外，它通过利用树和图结构的混合体，提供了一种有效的记忆检索方法。在三个智能体记忆基准上的广泛实验表明，H-Mem在问答任务上达到了最先进的性能。

Original abstract: Memory data are ubiquitous in Large Language Model (LLM)-based agents (e.g., OpenClaw and Manus). A few recent works have attempted to exploit agents'memory for improving their performance on the question-answering (QA) task, but they lack a principled mechanism for effectively modeling how memory data evolves over time and retrieving memory data effectively, leading to poor performance in memory utilization. To fill this gap, we present H-Mem, a novel memory mechanism via a hybrid structure that can not only effectively model the evolution of agent memory over a long period of time, but also provide an efficient memory retrieval approach. Particularly, H-Mem builds a temporal and semantic tree structure that allows the short-term memory data to evolve progressively into long-term memory data, where the latter provides summarized information about the former, while simultaneously constructing a knowledge graph to capture the relationships between entities in memory. Moreover, it offers an effective memory retrieval approach by exploiting the hybrid structure of the tree and graph structures. Extensive experiments on three agent memory benchmarks show that H-Mem achieves state-of-the-art performance on the QA task.

</details>


### [62] [RecMem: Recurrence-based Memory Consolidation for Efficient and Effective Long-Running LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16045v1)
*Zijie Dai,Shiyuan Deng,Sheng Guan,Yizhou Tian,Xin Yao,Xiao Yan,James Cheng*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出递归记忆巩固方法优化LLM agent长期运行效率，直接属于通用agent记忆与效率改进，可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出RecMem，通过延迟内存合并和利用交互重复性来降低LLM的token消耗，同时提升内存准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有内存系统对每个交互都调用LLM进行记忆提取，导致大量token浪费。

Method: RecMem使用轻量级嵌入模型将交互存储在潜意识层，仅在检测到语义相似的交互重复出现时才调用LLM提取情节和语义记忆，并加入语义细化机制恢复遗漏细节。

Result: 在三个SOTA系统上，内存构建token成本降低高达87%，且准确性超越它们。

Conclusion: RecMem通过重新设计内存合并时机，显著降低token消耗并提升准确性，是一种高效的内存管理方案。

中文摘要：内存系统通常将用户-智能体交互组织为可检索的外部记忆，对于长期运行的智能体至关重要，因为它们可以克服LLM有限的上下文窗口。然而，现有的内存系统会调用LLM处理每一个传入的交互以进行记忆提取，这种急切的内存合并方案导致了大量的token消耗。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了RecMem，重新思考何时应该进行内存合并。RecMem将传入的交互存储在一个潜意识记忆层中，并使用轻量级嵌入模型进行编码以用于检索。只有在观察到语义相似的交互持续重复出现时，才会调用LLM来提取情节记忆和语义记忆。这种基于重复的合并之所以有效，是因为这些交互对应于一个信息丰富的语义簇，因此值得提取和总结。为了提高准确性，RecMem还引入了一个语义细化机制，用于恢复记忆提取中遗漏的细粒度事实。实验表明，RecMem在三种最先进的内存系统上将内存构建的token成本降低了高达87%，同时超过了它们的准确性。

Original abstract: Memory systems often organize user-agent interactions as retrievable external memory and are crucial for long-running agents by overcoming the limited context windows of LLMs. However, existing memory systems invoke LLMs to process every incoming interaction for memory extraction, and such an eager memory consolidation scheme leads to substantial token consumption. To tackle this problem, we propose RecMem by rethinking when memory consolidation should be conducted. RecMem stores incoming interactions in a subconscious memory layer and encode them using lightweight embedding models for retrieval. LLMs are only invoked to extract episodic and semantic memory when sustained recurrence are observed for semantically similar interactions. Such recurrence-based consolidation works because these interactions correspond to a semantic cluster with rich information and thus are worth extraction and summarization. To improve accuracy, RecMem also incorporates a semantic refinement mechanism that recovers the fine-grained facts omitted by memory extraction. Experiments show that RecMem reduces the memory construction token cost of three SOTA memory systems by up to 87% while exceeding their accuracy.

</details>


### [63] [DebiasRAG: A Tuning-Free Path to Fair Generation in Large Language Models through Retrieval-Augmented Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16113v1)
*Rui Chu,Bingyin Zhao,Thanh Quoc Hung Le,Duy Cao Hoang,Huawei Lin,Ping Li,Weijie Zhao,Khoa D Doan,Yingjie Lao*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 基于RAG的LLM去偏框架，涉及检索增强与公平性控制，对agent可靠性与安全有参考。

TL;DR: 本文提出DebiasRAG，一种基于检索增强生成的无调优、动态查询特定去偏见框架，通过自诊断偏见上下文和梯度更新重排序来减轻LLM的社会偏见，同时保持模型原有能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有去偏见方法需要额外训练或领域知识，可能降低LLM性能且忽视动态去偏见需求；因此需要一种无需调优、动态且保持模型能力的去偏见方法。

Method: DebiasRAG包含三个步骤：1) 生成查询特定的去偏见候选；2) 构建上下文候选池；3) 使用梯度更新进行去偏见引导的上下文片段重排序。

Result: 通过去偏见上下文作为公平性约束，DebiasRAG在提高公平性的同时保留了LLM的表示能力，且无需额外调优。

Conclusion: DebiasRAG是一种有效的无调优动态去偏见框架，解决了现有方法需要额外资源和忽视动态性的问题，为LLM公平推理提供了新途径。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）因其卓越的生成能力而取得了前所未有的成功。然而，由于它们依赖于从训练语料中封装的知识，可能会产生幻觉、刻板印象和社会偏见内容。特别是，LLM容易产生涉及种族、性别和年龄的偏见回应，这些统称为社会偏见。先前的研究使用微调和提示工程来减轻LLM中的此类偏见，但这些方法需要额外的训练资源或领域知识来设计框架。此外，它们可能会降低LLM的原有能力，并且常常忽视在更公平推理中动态去偏见上下文的需求。在本文中，我们提出了DebiasRAG，一种基于检索增强生成（RAG）的新型无调优、动态查询特定的去偏见框架。DebiasRAG在提高公平性的同时保留了LLM的内在特性，如表示能力。DebiasRAG包括三个阶段：（1）查询特定的去偏见候选生成；（2）上下文候选池构建；以及（3）梯度更新的去偏见引导的上下文片段重排序。首先，DebiasRAG通过常规检索利用与查询相关的自我诊断偏见上下文，其中偏见上下文由DebiasRAG提供者离线准备。给定查询特定的偏见上下文，DebiasRAG反向生成去偏见上下文，作为LLM输出的额外公平性约束。其次，常规的RAG检索过程从常规的RAG文档数据库（如分块的维基百科数据集）中生成与查询相关的上下文。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have achieved unprecedented success due to their exceptional generative capabilities. However, because they depend on knowledge encapsulated from training corpora, they may produce hallucinations, stereotypes, and socially biased content. In particular, LLMs are prone to prejudiced responses involving race, gender, and age, which are collectively referred to as social biases. Prior studies have used fine-tuning and prompt engineering to mitigate such biases in LLMs, but these methods require additional training resources or domain knowledge to design the framework. Moreover, they may degrade the original capabilities of LLMs and often overlook the need for dynamic debiasing contexts for fairer inference. In this paper, we propose DebiasRAG, a novel tuning-free and dynamic query-specific debiasing framework based on retrieval-augmented generation (RAG). DebiasRAG improves fairness while preserving the intrinsic properties of LLMs, such as representation ability. DebiasRAG consists of three stages: (1) query-specific debiasing candidate generation; (2) context candidate pool construction; and (3) gradient-updated debiasing-guided context piece reranking. First, DebiasRAG leverages self-diagnosed bias contexts relevant to the query through regular retrieval, where the bias contexts are prepared offline by the DebiasRAG provider. Given the query-specific bias contexts, DebiasRAG reversely produces debiasing contexts, which are provided as additional fairness constraints for LLM outputs. Second, a regular RAG retrieval process produces query-related contexts from the regular RAG document database, such as a chunked Wikipedia dataset.

### [64] [Argus: Evidence Assembly for Scalable Deep Research Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16217v3)
*Zhen Zhang,Liangcai Su,Zhuo Chen,Xiang Lin,Haotian Xu,Simon Shaolei Du,Kaiyu Yang,Bo An,Lidong Bing,Xinyu Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多agent协作深度研究系统，RL训练导航器，通用agent架构

TL;DR: 提出Argus，通过协作搜索与导航机制，将深度研究转化为拼图式证据收集，利用强化学习训练导航者，显著提升并行搜索效率和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度研究智能体在并行搜索中常重复而非互补证据，导致收益递减且上下文受限，需更高效的协同方式。

Method: 设计Searcher收集子查询证据，Navigator维护证据图、验证缺失、调度搜索并推理合成；Navigator用强化学习训练，Searcher保持标准ReAct。

Result: 35B-A3B MoE模型上，单Searcher提升5.5分，8并行提升12.7分；64 Searcher在BrowseComp达86.2，超专有模型，Navigator上下文<21.5K tokens。

Conclusion: Argus有效解决了并行搜索中的重复和上下文瓶颈，通过协作与强化学习实现了高效、可扩展的深度研究。

中文摘要：深度研究智能体在复杂信息查找任务上取得了显著进展。即使是长ReAct风格的展开，也只探索单一轨迹，而最近的最先进系统通过并行搜索和聚合来扩展推理时间计算。然而，深度研究的答案由互补的证据片段组成，并行展开常常重复而非补充这些片段，导致收益递减，同时将聚合上下文推向模型的极限。我们提出了Argus，一种智能体系统，在该系统中，搜索者（Searcher）和导航者（Navigator）协作，将深度研究视为拼图游戏，从互补的证据片段中组装答案，而不是暴力并行生成整个答案。搜索者通过ReAct风格的交互为给定的子查询收集证据轨迹。导航者维护一个共享的证据图，验证哪些片段仍然缺失，派遣搜索者收集它们，并在完整的图上推理以生成带有来源追踪的最终答案。我们使用强化学习训练导航者来验证、派遣和综合，同时独立训练搜索者使其保持标准的ReAct智能体。由此产生的导航者支持与单个搜索者或多个并行搜索者的展开，且无需重新训练。搜索者和导航者均基于35B-A3B MoE骨干网络构建，Argus在八个基准测试上平均提升了5.5分（单个搜索者）和12.7分（8个并行搜索者）。使用64个搜索者时，它在BrowseComp上达到86.2分，超过了我们基准测试的所有专有智能体，而导航者的推理上下文保持在21.5K tokens以下。

Original abstract: Deep research agents have achieved remarkable progress on complex information seeking tasks. Even long ReAct style rollouts explore only a single trajectory, while recent state of the art systems scale inference time compute via parallel search and aggregation. Yet deep research answers are composed of complementary pieces of evidence, which parallel rollouts often duplicate rather than complete, yielding diminishing returns while pushing the aggregation context toward the model's limit. We propose Argus, an agentic system in which a Searcher and a Navigator cooperate to treat deep research as assembling a jigsaw from complementary evidence pieces, rather than brute forcing the whole answer in parallel. The Searcher collects evidence traces for a given sub-query through ReAct-style interaction. The Navigator maintains a shared evidence graph, verifying which pieces are still missing, dispatching Searchers to gather them, and reasoning over the completed graph to produce a source-traced final answer. We train the Navigator with reinforcement learning to verify, dispatch, and synthesize, while independently training the Searcher to remain a standard ReAct agent. The resulting Navigator supports rollouts with a single Searcher or many in parallel without retraining. With both Searcher and Navigator built on a 35B-A3B MoE backbone, Argus gains 5.5 points with a single Searcher and 12.7 points with 8 parallel Searchers, averaged over eight benchmarks. With 64 Searchers it reaches 86.2 on BrowseComp, surpassing every proprietary agent we benchmark, while the Navigator's reasoning context stays under 21.5K tokens.

### [65] [The Scaling Laws of Skills in LLM Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16508v1)
*Charles Chen,Qiming Yu,Yuhang Gu,Zhuoye Huang,Hanjing Li,Hongyu Liu,Simin Liu,Jinhao Liu,Dengyun Peng,Jiangyi Wang,Zheng Yan,Fanqing Meng,Ethan Qin,Carl Che,Mengkang Hu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 直接研究LLM agent技能缩放定律，分析路由与执行，对coding agent技能库优化有直接指导

TL;DR: 发现了智能体系统中技能库规模的两个耦合缩放定律（路由和对数衰减、执行乘法提升），并通过参数b连接，优化后显著提升了路由精度和执行效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解智能体系统中技能库规模增长时的缩放规律，以指导大型技能库的设计和优化。

Method: 在15个LLM、1141个技能和超过300万次决策上，分析路由精度与库大小的关系，以及执行对下游决策的影响，识别出两个定律及其耦合参数b，并进行定律引导的优化实验。

Result: 路由精度随库大小对数衰减（R²>0.97），正确执行改善下游决策约4倍；优化后路由精度从71.3%提升至91.7%，劫持率从22.4%降至4.1%，ClawBench通过率从49.3%提升至61.6%，ClawMark从28.4%提升至34.5%。

Conclusion: 智能体性能不仅依赖于模型能力，还受技能库的结构、粒度和暴露策略影响；所发现的缩放定律和优化方法具有实用价值。

中文摘要：随着智能体系统的扩展，技能积累成大型可复用库，但其缩放定律仍不为人知。通过15个前沿LLM、1141个真实世界技能及超过300万次路由或执行决策，我们识别出两个耦合的定律。路由定律：单步路由精度随库规模对数衰减（所有模型的R²>0.97），错误从局部技能竞争发展到跨族漂移，并被过度通用的“黑洞技能”捕获。执行定律：在状态实现前，联合路由近似乘法，而正确执行可将困难下游决策改善约4倍。单个参数——路由对数衰减斜率b——耦合了两个定律：路由侧拟合可预测跨模型的执行侧救援，表明同一库属性同时控制执行前崩溃和下游可恢复性。这些定律是可操作的：定律引导优化将保留路由精度从71.3%提升至91.7%，劫持率从22.4%降至4.1%，并定向迁移至下游ClawBench和ClawMark执行设置，将平均通过率从49.3%提升至61.6%（ClawBench）及从28.4%提升至34.5%（ClawMark）。这些结果表明，智能体性能不仅取决于模型能力，还取决于技能库的结构、粒度和暴露策略。

Original abstract: As agent systems scale, skills accumulate into large reusable libraries, yet their scaling laws remain poorly understood. Across 15 frontier LLMs, 1,141 real-world skills, and over 3M routing or execution decisions, we identify two coupled laws. Routing law: single-step routing accuracy decays logarithmically with library size ($R^2{>}0.97$ for all models), with errors progressing from local skill competition to cross-family drift and capture by overly general "black-hole skills". Execution law: before state realization, joint routing is approximately multiplicative, whereas correct execution can improve difficult downstream decisions by about $4{\times}$. A single parameter, the routing logarithmic decay slope $b$, couples the two laws: routing-side fits predict execution-side rescue across models, showing that the same library property controls both pre-execution collapse and downstream recoverability. The laws are actionable: law-guided optimization raises held-out routing accuracy from 71.3% to 91.7%, reduces hijack from 22.4% to 4.1%, and transfers directionally to downstream ClawBench and ClawMark execution settings, improving mean pass rate from 49.3% to 61.6% on ClawBench and from 28.4% to 34.5% on ClawMark. These results show that agent performance depends not only on model capability, but also on the structure, granularity, and exposure policy of the skill library.

</details>


### [66] [SKG-Eval: Stateful Evaluation of Multi-Turn Dialogue via Incremental Semantic Knowledge Graphs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16650v1)
*Avijit Shil,Suman Samui*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多轮对话的语义知识图谱评估框架，可迁移至agent评测。

TL;DR: 提出SKG-Eval框架，通过语义知识图谱建模对话，结合局部相关性、历史一致性和逻辑连贯性三个信号，实现准确定性和可解释的多轮对话评估，提高长期不一致检测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动评估器在处理多轮对话中的长期依赖（如矛盾、主题漂移、实体不一致）效果不佳，因为它们依赖扁平或孤立轮次表示。

Method: 提出SKG-Eval框架，将对话建模为演进语义知识图谱，通过结构化三元组提取逐步更新，计算三个互补信号（局部相关性、历史一致性、逻辑连贯性），并自适应融合为长度不变的会话得分。

Result: 在多个基准测试中，SKG-Eval与人类判断相关性更高，显著提高对长期不一致的检测，并产生可审计的确定性得分。

Conclusion: 通过语义知识图谱的结构化外部化状态跟踪为LLM对话评估提供可扩展替代方案。

中文摘要：评估多轮对话系统仍然具有挑战性，因为响应质量不仅取决于当前提示，还取决于先前建立的实体、声明和对话承诺。现有的自动评估器，包括LLM-as-a-judge框架和基于嵌入的指标，很大程度上依赖于扁平化或孤立轮次的表示，因此在检测长期问题（如矛盾、主题漂移和实体不一致）方面效果较差。为了解决这个问题，我们提出SKG-Eval，一个准确定性和可解释的框架，将对话建模为一个跨轮次的实体、关系和承诺的演进语义知识图谱（SKG）。该框架通过结构化三元组提取逐步更新图谱，并计算三个互补信号：（i）局部相关性，衡量与当前提示和可选参考的对齐程度；（ii）历史一致性，利用基于图谱和嵌入驱动的信号评估新引入信息如何与先前的对话上下文连接；（iii）逻辑连贯性，通过几何矛盾引擎评估，该引擎检测跨轮次冲突，无需依赖NLI模型或LLM判断。这些信号通过自适应融合和基于近期权重的趋势分析聚合成一个长度不变的会话得分。在多个基准测试中，SKG-Eval与人类判断的相关性更高，并显著提高了对扩展对话中长期不一致性的检测。此外，该框架为固定输入产生明确的矛盾证书和确定性得分，实现可重复和可审计的评估。总体而言，我们的结果表明，通过语义知识图谱的结构化外部化状态跟踪为基于LLM的对话评估器中的隐式推理提供了一种可扩展的替代方案。

Original abstract: Evaluating multi-turn dialogue systems remains challenging because response quality depends not only on the current prompt, but also on previously established entities, claims, and conversational commitments. Existing automatic evaluators, including LLM-as-a-judge frameworks and embedding-based metrics, largely rely on flat or turn-isolated representations, making them less effective at detecting long-range issues such as contradiction, topic drift, and entity inconsistency. To address this, we propose SKG-Eval, a quasi-deterministic and interpretable framework that models dialogue as an evolving Semantic Knowledge Graph (SKG) of entities, relations, and commitments across turns. The framework incrementally updates the graph through structured triple extraction and computes three complementary signals: (i) local relevance, measuring alignment with the current prompt and optional reference; (ii) historical consistency, evaluating how newly introduced information connects to prior conversational context using graph-based and embedding-driven signals; and (iii) logical coherence, assessed by a geometric contradiction engine that detects cross-turn conflicts without relying on NLI models or LLM judges. These signals are adaptively fused and aggregated into a length-invariant session score via recency-weighted trend analysis. Across multiple benchmarks, SKG-Eval achieves higher correlation with human judgments and substantially improves detection of long-range inconsistencies in extended conversations. In addition, the framework produces explicit contradiction certificates and deterministic scores for fixed inputs, enabling reproducible and auditable evaluation. Overall, our results suggest that structured externalized state tracking through semantic knowledge graphs provides a scalable alternative to implicit reasoning in LLM-based dialogue evaluators.

</details>


### [67] [CHI-Bench: Can AI Agents Automate End-to-End, Long-Horizon, Policy-Rich Healthcare Workflows?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16679v2)
*Haolin Chen,Deon Metelski,Leon Qi,Tao Xia,Joonyul Lee,Steve Brown,Kevin Riley,Frank Wang,T. Y. Alvin Liu,Hank Capps MD,Zeyu Tang,Xiangchen Song,Lingjing Kong,Fan Feng,Tianyi Zeng,Zhiwei Liu,Zixian Ma,Hang Jiang,Fangli Geng,Yuan Yuan,Chenyu You,Qingsong Wen,Hua Wei,Yanjie Fu,Yue Zhao,Carl Yang,Biwei Huang,Kun Zhang,Caiming Xiong,Sanmi Koyejo,Eric P. Xing,Philip S. Yu,Weiran Yao*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多角色、长程医疗工作流基准，包含工具使用和策略密度，可作为通用agent评测和架构参考。

TL;DR: χ-Bench基准测试揭示，在医疗保健领域，当前AI代理在处理策略密集、多角色和多边交互的长时域工作流时性能极差（最佳28%，严格指标低于20%），表明其在类似企业任务中存在显著差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试未能充分评估医疗运营自动化所需的策略密度、多角色组合和多边交互能力，因此需要构建更逼真的基准来暴露当前AI代理在这些方面的不足。

Method: 构建χ-Bench基准，包含三个领域（预授权、利用率管理、护理管理）的多个任务，每个任务在高保真模拟器（20个医疗应用、87个MCP工具）中运行，代理需依据包含1290+文档的操作手册完成任务，并评估30种代理配置/模型配置的性能。

Result: 最佳代理仅完成28.0%任务，严格pass^3指标低于20%，多任务单会话性能降至3.8%。

Conclusion: 当前AI代理在处理政策密集、角色组合、不可逆的企业任务中存在显著差距，此假设可能扩展到其他类似领域。

中文摘要：现实医疗运营的端到端自动化强调当前基准测试中代表性不足的三项能力：策略密度，决策必须基于庞大的医疗、保险和运营规则库；多角色组合，单个任务要求代理扮演多个角色并进行交接；以及多边交互，中间工作流步骤是多轮对话，如同行评审和患者外展。我们引入了χ-Bench，一个涵盖三个领域（提供者预授权、支付方利用率管理、护理管理）的长时域医疗工作流基准测试。每个任务向代理提供一个临床案例，该案例在一个由20个医疗应用（通过87个MCP工具暴露）组成的高保真模拟器中运行，代理必须通过工具调用和撰写角色工件将其驱动到终端状态，并依据包含1290多份文档的管理式医疗运营手册技能。在30个代理配置/模型配置中，最佳代理仅解决了28.0%的任务，没有代理在严格pass^3指标上超过20%，而在单个会话中执行所有任务的性能骤降至3.8%。这些结果提出了一个假设：类似的差距可能在其他策略密集、角色组合、不可逆的企业领域中浮现。

Original abstract: End-to-end automation of realistic healthcare operations stresses three capabilities underrepresented in current benchmarks: policy density, decisions must be grounded in a large library of medical, insurance, and operational rules; Multi-role composition: a single task requires the agent to play multiple roles with handoffs; and multilateral interaction: intermediate workflow steps are multi-turn dialogs, such as peer-to-peer review and patient outreach. We introduce $χ$-Bench, a benchmark of long-horizon healthcare workflows across three domains: provider prior authorization, payer utilization management, and care management. Each task hands the agent a clinical case in a high-fidelity simulator of 20 healthcare apps exposed via 87 MCP tools, which it must drive to a terminal status through tool calls and writing the role's artifacts, guided by a 1,290+ document managed-care operations handbook skill. Across 30 agent harness/models configurations, the best agent resolves only 28.0% of tasks, no agent clears 20% on strict pass^3, and executing all tasks in a single session slumps the performance to 3.8%. These results raise the hypothesis that similar gaps are likely to surface in other policy-dense, role-composed, irreversible enterprise domains.

</details>

### [68] [ITHICA: Intra-Thread Instruction Checking Approach for Defect-Induced Silent Data Corruptions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15638v1)
*Ioanna Vavelidou,Subho S. Banerjee,Eric X. Liu,Mike Fuller,Subhasish Mitra,Caroline Trippel*

Main category: cs.AR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: ITHICA通过指令复制和输出比较自动生成功能测试，利用不一致错误检测CPU缺陷，在3000多台服务器上比原生检查多检测39%的缺陷服务器，并挑战了先前研究结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超大规模报告中的静默数据损坏（SDC）被认为由制造缺陷引起，需要有效的功能测试来检测有缺陷的CPU。

Method: ITHICA通过插入线程内、指令级错误检查（指令复制和输出比较）从任意程序生成功能测试，利用不一致错误（相同输入不同执行上下文产生不同输出）来检测缺陷。

Result: 在超过3000台CPU服务器上评估，ITHICA错误检查比原生检查多检测39%的有缺陷服务器，并揭示了挑战先前机群研究的缺陷行为新发现。

Conclusion: ITHICA能有效生成功能测试并检测更多缺陷服务器，且其对缺陷行为的新发现质疑了先前研究的结论。

中文摘要：超大规模报告中的静默数据损坏（SDC）被认为是由硅制造缺陷引起的，这促使开发用于检测有缺陷CPU的功能测试。我们提出了ITHICA，一种通过插入线程内、指令级错误检查（主要利用指令复制和输出比较）从任意程序自动生成用于检测缺陷引起的错误的功能测试的方法。我们的关键见解是，最有害的缺陷会导致不一致的错误：同一线程内两次执行相同指令，给定相同输入，根据执行的上下文不同，可能产生不同的架构输出。通过利用这一见解，ITHICA使任意程序能够作为测试，并在检测到错误时识别受影响的指令。我们使用ITHICA将工业超大规模测试程序（我们的基线）、数据中心工作负载和常见库转换为功能测试，并在超过3000台CPU服务器上对其进行评估。从基线程序派生出的ITHICA测试中，ITHICA错误检查检测到的有缺陷服务器比原生检查多39%，并在缺陷行为上揭示了新的发现，这些发现挑战了先前超大规模机群研究得出的结论。

Original abstract: Hyperscaler reports of silent data corruptions (SDCs), presumed to be caused by silicon manufacturing defects, have motivated the development of functional tests for detecting defective CPUs. We present ITHICA, an approach for automatically generating functional tests for defect-induced errors from arbitrary programs by inserting intra-thread, instruction-level error checks, primarily leveraging instruction duplication and output comparison. Our key insight is that the most pernicious defects cause inconsistent errors: two executions of the same instruction within the same thread, given the same inputs, can produce different architectural outputs depending on the execution context in which they run. By exploiting this insight, ITHICA enables arbitrary programs to serve as tests and identifies affected instructions upon error detections. We use ITHICA to transform industrial hyperscaler test programs (our baseline), datacenter workloads, and common libraries into functional tests, and evaluate them on over 3,000 CPU servers. ITHICA error checks detect 39% more defective servers than native checks within the ITHICA tests derived from our baseline programs, and enable novel findings on defect behavior that challenge conclusions drawn by prior hyperscaler fleet studies.

</details>

### [69] [DeepArrhythmia: Segment-Contextualized ECG Arrhythmia Classification via Selective Evidence Acquisition](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16441v1)
*Jiahui Li,Ruili Fang,Zishuai Liu,WenZhan Song,Jin Lu,Fei Dou*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 医疗诊断agent框架，包含工具使用与选择性证据获取，有通用agent方法贡献

TL;DR: 提出DeepArrhythmia，一种基于工具的多模态框架，通过结合信号和图像、利用专门工具进行节律-形态分析，并动态选择证据，实现段上下文的逐拍ECG心律失常分类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有系统将心跳视为孤立实例，忽略多拍节律上下文（如时序、代偿间歇和形态一致性），导致分类性能受限。

Method: DeepArrhythmia框架接收多拍ECG段，融合原始信号和渲染波形图像，定位R波识别心跳；使用心跳定位、数值节律-形态提取和形态文本分析工具解耦测量与整合；根据段级置信度在最小和丰富证据状态间路由，实现选择性证据获取。

Result: 框架设计实现了段上下文的逐拍分类，通过动态证据路由适应不同样本需求。

Conclusion: 该智能体设计有效整合节律上下文、生理依据和选择性证据，为ECG心律失常识别提供了更准确的决策基础。

中文摘要：逐拍级心电图（ECG）心律失常检测旨在为记录中的每个心跳分配一个心律失常类别，然而许多现有系统将心跳视为孤立的局部实例。这是有局限性的，因为心跳标签通常依赖于多拍节律上下文，包括时间、代偿性间歇和逐拍形态一致性。我们提出了DeepArrhythmia，一个基于工具的多模态框架，用于段上下文化的逐拍级心电图心律失常分类。给定一个多拍心电图段，DeepArrhythmia结合原始心电图信号和渲染的波形图像，定位R波以识别心跳实例，并生成结构化的逐拍级预测。该框架通过专门用于心跳定位、数值节律-形态提取和形态聚焦文本分析的工具，将生理测量与证据整合解耦。DeepArrhythmia使用段级置信度在最小和丰富证据状态之间路由，因为更丰富的生理证据并非总是有用。这种智能体设计整合了节律上下文、明确的生理依据和选择性证据获取用于决策。

Original abstract: Beat-level Electrocardiography (ECG) arrhythmia detection aims to assign an arrhythmia class to each beat in a recording, yet many existing systems treat beats as isolated local instances. This is limiting because beat labels often depend on multi-beat rhythm context, including timing, compensatory pauses, and beat-to-beat morphological consistency. We present DeepArrhythmia, a tool-grounded multimodal framework for segment-contextualized beat-level ECG arrhythmia classification. Given a multi-beat ECG segment, DeepArrhythmia combines the raw ECG signal and a rendered waveform image, localizes R peaks to identify beat instances, and produces structured beat-level predictions. The framework decouples physiological measurement from evidence integration using specialized tools for beat localization, numerical rhythm--morphology extraction, and morphology-focused textual analysis. DeepArrhythmia uses segment-level confidence to route between minimal and rich evidence states, since richer physiological evidence is not uniformly useful. This agentic design integrates rhythm context, explicit physiological grounding, and selective evidence acquisition for decision making.

### [70] [AstraFlow: Dataflow-Oriented Reinforcement Learning for Agentic LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15565v1)
*Haizhong Zheng,Yizhuo Di,Jiahui Wang,Shuowei Jin,Xueshen Liu,Yongji Wu,Z. Morley Mao,Ion Stoica,Jiawei Zhao,Beidi Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 面向agentic LLM的强化学习系统，支持多策略训练，直接相关agent系统架构。

TL;DR: 提出AstraFlow，一种数据流导向的RL系统，通过解耦组件抽象支持多策略智能体RL和异构资源，训练速度提升2.7倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM RL系统以训练器为中心，扩展困难，缺乏组件抽象，导致每次新功能需专用工程。

Method: 采用数据流导向架构，将推出服务、数据流管理和训练解耦为自治组件，支持多策略协作与弹性异构计算。

Result: 在数学、代码、搜索和AgentBench任务上，无需代码更改即支持多策略训练等，训练速度提升2.7倍且准确率相当或更好。

Conclusion: AstraFlow通过原则性抽象有效简化了智能体RL系统的扩展，支持复杂工作负载和资源利用。

中文摘要：强化学习（RL）越来越多地被用于提升大型语言模型的推理、编码和工具使用能力，但智能体RL仍然昂贵得令人望而却步。将RL扩展到智能体LLM需要支持复杂的工作负载，包括多策略协作训练，同时高效地使用弹性、异构和跨区域的计算资源。现有的LLM RL系统支持其中一些能力，但每个新的扩展往往需要专门的系统工程。这种负担源于以训练器为中心的控制架构以及缺乏RL系统组件的原则性抽象。为了解决这些限制，我们提出了AstraFlow，一种数据流导向的RL系统，它用原则性的组件抽象取代了传统的以训练器为中心的控制。在AstraFlow中，推出服务、数据流管理和训练被解耦为自治组件，使得系统能够原生支持复杂的多策略智能体RL工作负载，并有效利用多样化的计算资源。我们在数学、代码、搜索和AgentBench工作负载上评估了AstraFlow，结果显示，相同的系统无需系统级代码更改即可支持多策略训练、弹性扩展、异构跨区域执行和可组合数据算法。在多策略协作训练中，AstraFlow在达到与现有RL系统相当或更好的准确率的同时，将训练速度提升了2.7倍。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) is increasingly used to improve the reasoning, coding, and tool-use capabilities of large language models, but agentic RL remains prohibitively expensive. Scaling RL to agentic LLMs requires supporting complex workloads, including multi-policy collaborative training, while efficiently using elastic, heterogeneous, and cross-region compute resources. Existing LLM RL systems support some of these capabilities, but each new extension often requires dedicated system engineering. This burden arises from trainer-centered control architectures and the lack of principled abstractions for RL system components. To address these limitations, we propose AstraFlow, a dataflow-oriented RL system that replaces conventional trainer-centered control with principled component abstractions. In AstraFlow, rollout services, dataflow management, and training are decoupled into autonomous components, enabling the system to natively support complex multi-policy agentic RL workloads and efficiently exploit diverse compute resources. We evaluate AstraFlow across math, code, search, and AgentBench workloads, showing that the same system supports multi-policy training, elastic scaling, heterogeneous cross-region execution, and composable data algorithms without system-level code changes. In multi-policy collaborative training, AstraFlow achieves comparable or better accuracy than existing RL systems while speeding up training time by 2.7x.

### [71] [SAGE: Shaping Anchors for Guided Exploration in RLVR of LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18864v1)
*Chanuk Lee,Minki Kang,Sung Ju Hwang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: RLVR探索机制提升LLM推理，可启发agent自我改进的训练方法。

TL;DR: 提出SAGE框架，通过引导函数重塑反向KL锚分布，在提升pass@1的同时显著改善pass@k，平衡效率与覆盖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RLVR在推理任务中提升pass@1但pass@k改进有限，现有方法因反向KL正则化导致探索不足，且简单移除或替换KL项会破坏效率-覆盖权衡。

Method: 提出SAGE框架，使用引导函数q(x,y)动态重塑反向KL的锚分布，实现可控的经验支持扩展，在不牺牲稳定性的前提下促进探索。

Result: 在数学推理基准上，SAGE在pass@1和pass@k上均取得一致且显著的改进。

Conclusion: 通过重塑反向KL锚分布，SAGE有效解决了RLVR中探索与覆盖的冲突，使模型同时提升单次和多次采样性能。

中文摘要：近期研究表明，带有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）能可靠地提升推理任务上的pass@1指标，但在pass@k上往往未能取得类似的改进，这引发了一个问题：RLVR是否真正使大型语言模型获得新的推理能力，还是仅仅提高了基础模型中已存在的推理模式的采样效率？先前的分析大多支持后一种观点，将其归因于标准RLVR目标的结构特性导致的探索压力不足。在这项工作中，我们认为一个核心的结构约束来自反向KL正则化，它稳定了训练，但本质上将策略锚定在参考分布上，从而抑制了替代推理模式的涌现。然而，我们表明，移除KL项或将其替换为前向KL都无法提供令人满意的解决方案，因为两者都会通过诱发奖励破解或将概率质量分配给目标外区域而破坏效率-覆盖范围的权衡。为了解决这一矛盾，我们提出了SAGE，一个原则性框架，通过引导函数q(x,y)重塑反向KL锚定分布本身，实现可控的经验支持扩展，在具有挑战性的数学推理基准上，在pass@1和pass@k上均取得一致改进。我们的代码可在https://github.com/tally0818/SAGE获取。

Original abstract: Recent studies observe that reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) reliably improves pass@1 on reasoning tasks, yet often fails to yield comparable gains in pass@k, raising the question of whether RLVR genuinely enables large language models to acquire novel reasoning abilities or merely enhances the efficiency of sampling reasoning modes already present in the base model. Prior analyses largely support the latter view, attributing this limitation to structural properties of standard RLVR objectives that result in insufficient exploration pressure. In this work, we argue that a central structural constraint arises from reverse-KL regularization, which stabilizes training but inherently anchors the policy to the reference distribution, thereby suppressing the emergence of alternative reasoning modes. However, we show that neither removing the KL term nor replacing it with forward-KL provides a satisfactory solution, as both disrupt the efficiency-coverage trade-off by either inducing reward hacking or allocating probability mass to off-target regions. To resolve this tension, we propose SAGE, a principled framework that enables controllable empirical support expansion by reshaping the reverse-KL anchor distribution itself through a guide function q(x,y), achieving consistent improvements in both pass@1 and pass@k across challenging mathematical reasoning benchmarks. Our code is available at https://github.com/tally0818/SAGE.

</details>


### [72] [EVA-0: Test-Time Model Evolution with Only Two Forward Passes per Sample](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18867v1)
*Guohao Chen,Shuaicheng Niu,Geng Li,Yunbei Zhang,Shilin Shan,Chunyan Miao,Jianfei Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 测试时模型进化，无需反向传播的适应机制，可启发agent的自我改进。

TL;DR: 提出EVA-0，一种无需反向传播的零阶测试时适应框架，仅需两次前向传播，在ImageNet-C上超越现有方法并实现14倍加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试时模型演化方法依赖反向传播，内存开销大，难以部署在边缘设备或黑盒模型上，且在两前向预算下零阶优化存在捷径解、权重漂移和方向估计不准确的问题。

Method: 提出EVA-0框架，包括：1) 损失尺度不变性防止捷径解；2) 锚定引导优化减轻权重漂移；3) 样本级对称双侧扰动估计更新方向。推理和适应仅需两次前向传播。

Result: 在ImageNet-C和ViT-Base上，EVA-0优于基于BP的DeYO和无BP的FOA，且比FOA快14倍。

Conclusion: EVA-0是一种高效、无反向传播的测试时适应方法，适合资源受限场景，在性能和速度上均具优势。

中文摘要：测试时模型演化为已部署模型提供了一种有前景的方式，使其能够从未标记的测试时经验中改进，然而大多数现有方法依赖于反向传播（BP），这会带来显著的内存开销，并使其难以部署在边缘设备、量化模型、专用加速器或黑盒模型上。在这项工作中，我们研究在严格的两前向预算下的测试时模型演化，这一设置推动适应向高效的实际部署发展。我们揭示了零阶测试时优化中的三个关键障碍：对捷径解的敏感性、不受控制的权重漂移以及无效的更新方向估计。为了克服这些问题，我们提出了EVA-0，一个最小的零阶适应框架，它：1) 保持损失尺度不变以防止捷径解；2) 设计了一种锚定引导的优化策略来减轻权重漂移；3) 使用样本级对称双侧扰动进行更新方向估计和推理。EVA-0不需要BP，并且每个样本仅需两次前向传播即可完成推理和适应。在ImageNet-C和ViT-Base上的结果显示，EVA-0优于基于BP的DeYO和无BP的FOA，同时相对于FOA实现了14倍的速度提升。代码将发布。

Original abstract: Test-time model evolution offers a promising way for deployed models to improve from unlabeled test-time experience, yet most existing methods depend on backpropagation (BP), which incurs substantial memory overhead and makes them difficult to deploy on edge devices, quantized models, specialized accelerators, or black-box models. In this work, we study test-time model evolution under a strict two-forward budget, a setting that pushes adaptation toward highly efficient real-world deployment. We reveal three key obstacles in zeroth-order test-time optimization: susceptibility to shortcut solutions, uncontrolled weight drift, and ineffective update direction estimation. To overcome them, we propose EVA-0, a minimal zeroth-order adaptation framework that: 1) keeps the loss scale-invariant to prevent shortcut solutions; 2) devises an anchor-guided optimization strategy to alleviate weight drift; 3) uses sample-wise symmetric two-sided perturbation for update direction estimation and inference. EVA-0 requires no BP and performs both inference and adaptation within only two forward passes per sample. Results on ImageNet-C & ViT-Base show that EVA-0 outperforms both BP-based DeYO and BP-free FOA, while achieving a 14x speed-up over FOA. Code will be released.

</details>


### [73] [Predicting Performance of Symbolic and Prompt Programs with Examples](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21515v1)
*Chengqi Zheng,Keya Hu,Shuzhi Liu,Tao Wu,Kevin Ellis,Yewen Pu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 性能预测方法适用于LLM提示程序，对coding agent的可靠性评估有参考价值。

TL;DR: 基于贝叶斯模型和先验差异，提出RAP方法预测LLM提示程序性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM提示不可靠，可能通过测试但部署失败，需要准确预测其真实性能。

Method: 使用抛硬币模型将程序执行视为伯努利变量，性能由观察结果和先验决定；从语料库编译经验先验发现符号化程序与提示程序的先验差异；提出RAP方法，通过检索相似任务和提示程序构建代理先验进行性能预测。

Result: RAP在性能预测上取得了可靠的结果。

Conclusion: 符号化程序和提示程序性能先验的差异（全有全无 vs. 分散）解释了为何测试认证效果不同，且RAP方法能有效预测性能。

中文摘要：LLM提示被广泛用于自然语言表述的任务，然而它并不可靠——它可能在少数测试案例上成功，但在部署时失败。我们研究性能预测：给定一个程序，无论是符号化程序（如Python）还是在LLM上执行的提示，以及少量领域内示例，预测其在同一领域未见任务上的性能。我们采用一个简单的抛硬币模型，将每次通过/失败的程序执行视为伯努利随机变量，其成功概率即为程序未知的性能。在该模型中，性能完全取决于：1）在测试案例上观察到的执行结果，以及2）关于性能的先验。我们从一个包含多种程序和任务的语料库中编译经验性能先验，并发现符号化程序（如Python）的性能是“全有或全无”的，而提示程序的先验是分散的，存在大量近乎正确的程序。这一差异解释了为何少量通过测试可以认证符号化程序，却无法认证提示程序。基于这一见解，我们开发了RAP（检索近似先验），它从现有语料库中检索相似任务和提示程序以构建代理先验，然后用其预测性能。我们展示了RAP取得了可靠的性能。

Original abstract: LLM prompting is widely used for naturally stated tasks, yet it is unreliable it may succeed on a few test cases but fail at deployment time. We study performance prediction: given a program, either symbolic (e.g. Python) or a prompt executed on an LLM, and a few in-domain examples, predict its performance on unseen tasks from the same domain. We use a simple coin-flip model, treating each pass/fail program execution as a Bernoulli random variable, whose success probability is the programs unknown performance. In this model, performance depends entirely on: 1) the observed execution outcomes on test cases, and 2) a prior over performances. We compile empirical performance priors from a corpus of diverse programs and tasks, and find that performance for symbolic programs (e.g., Python) are all or nothing, while prompt programs have a diffuse prior with many nearly-correct programs. This difference explains why a few passing tests can certify symbolic programs but not prompt programs. Building on this insight, we develop RAP (Retrieved Approximate Prior), which retrieves similar tasks and prompt programs from an existing corpus to construct a proxy prior, which is then used to predict performance. We show RAP achieves solid performances.

</details>


### [74] [Harnesses for Inference-Time Alignment over Execution Trajectories](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21516v1)
*Boyuan Wang,Bochao Li,Minghan Wang,Yuxin Tao,Fang Kong*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: Harness设计用于推断时轨迹对齐，直接研究任务分解与引导执行对LLM agent的影响，核心相关。

TL;DR: 从轨迹对齐视角分析提示工程，将提示分为任务分解和引导执行，揭示了性能极限和失败模式，并发现部分提示比完全结构化更有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有提示设计缺乏统一理论理解，增加分解或引导有时反而降低性能，需要量化分析其影响和失败模式。

Method: 通过推理时轨迹对齐视角，将提示分为任务分解和引导执行两种机制，并量化工作流粒度、重试预算、动作重新加权的影响，结合合成实验和真实基准验证。

Result: 发现了过度分解、过度剪枝和幻觉执行等失败模式，并验证了部分提示（仅初始步骤）比完全结构化工作流获得更高通过率。

Conclusion: 提示设计应权衡分解与引导，部分提示在特定任务中更优，为高效提示工程提供了理论指导。

中文摘要：提示工程已成为大型语言模型代理的一种重要的推理时技术，旨在通过任务分解和引导执行来提升长期性能。然而，更精细的提示并不总是更好：增加分解或引导有时能提升执行效果，但也可能降低最终任务成功率。我们通过推理时轨迹对齐的视角研究提示设计。该视角将提示分为两种机制：任务分解（将任务结构化为子目标）和引导执行（在执行期间重塑局部动作分布）。这种分解使我们能够量化工作流粒度、重试预算和引导引发的动作重新加权如何影响提示设计的性能极限。它进一步揭示了具体的失败模式，包括过度分解、过度剪枝和幻觉执行。我们通过受控合成实验和真实终端代理基准验证了这些预测。受理论启发，我们进一步表明，有效的提示可以是部分的：仅指定初始步骤，将剩余执行留给代理，可以实现比完全结构化工作流更高的通过率。

Original abstract: Harness engineering has emerged as an important inference-time technique for large language model (LLM) agents, aiming to improve long-term performance through task decomposition and guided execution. However, more elaborate harnesses are not uniformly better: increasing decomposition or guidance can sometimes improve execution, but can also reduce final task success. We study harness design through the lens of inference-time trajectory alignment. This perspective separates harness into two mechanisms: task decomposition, which structures a task into sub-goals, and guided execution, which reshapes local action distributions during execution. This decomposition allows us to quantify how workflow granularity, retry budgets, and guidance-induced action reweighting shape the performance limits of harness design. It further reveals concrete failure modes, including over-decomposition, over-pruning, and hallucinated execution. We validate these predictions through controlled synthetic experiments and real terminal agent benchmarks. Inspired by the theory, we further show that effective harnesses can be partial: specifying only the initial steps and leaving the remaining execution to agent can achieve higher pass rate than fully structured workflows.

### [75] [MO-CAPO: Multi-Objective Cost-Aware Prompt Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18869v1)
*Jan Büssing,Moritz Schlager,Timo Heiß,Tom Zehle,Matthias Feurer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MO-CAPO是一种联合优化性能和推理成本的多目标提示优化算法，利用预算分配实现成本高效的优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动提示优化方法主要只关注性能，忽略推理成本等竞争目标；而多目标方法依赖低效的现成NSGA-II，缺乏优化效率。

Method: 提出MO-CAPO算法，联合优化性能和推理成本，采用部署导向的成本目标和预算分配策略来提高优化效率。

Conclusion: MO-CAPO能够高效地发现多个提示，提供不同的性能-成本权衡，使从业者能够根据需求灵活选择，并首次在评估中考虑了泛化性和鲁棒性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在广泛的任务中表现出色，但对提示设计高度敏感，这促使了自动提示优化的需求。现有方法主要只关注性能，忽略了诸如推理成本或延迟等竞争目标。同时，现有的多目标提示优化工作依赖于现成的NSGA-II，忽略了优化效率。为了解决这一问题，我们引入了MO-CAPO，一种新颖的多目标提示优化算法，该算法联合优化性能和推理成本，同时利用预算分配实现成本高效的优化。我们进一步提出了一个面向部署的成本目标，该目标捕获了LLM推理的完整计算概况。我们在四个任务和三个LLM上评估了我们的方法，并将其与基于NSGA-II的多目标方法和最先进的单目标提示优化器进行了比较。结果表明，MO-CAPO在保持成本效益的同时，始终能够识别出强大、稳健且多样化的帕累托前沿近似。在嘈杂R2指标上，它在12个案例中的8个上优于NSGA-II基线，并且通常已经在相当低的预算下实现了竞争性能。所发现的解集涵盖了多样化的性能-成本权衡，这些权衡被单目标优化器忽略，但顶级性能候选者仍然与单目标解决方案具有竞争力。此外，我们进行了首次考虑泛化性和鲁棒性的多目标机器学习实验评估，通过嘈杂R2和近似差距，实现了对解质量更现实的评估。MO-CAPO使从业者能够从高效发现的多个提示集中进行选择，这些提示在性能和成本之间提供了不同的权衡。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) achieve strong performance across a wide range of tasks but are highly sensitive to prompt design, motivating the need for automatic prompt optimization. Existing methods predominantly focus on performance alone, ignoring competing objectives such as inference cost or latency. At the same time, existing work on multi-objective prompt optimization relies on off-the-shelf NSGA-II, ignoring optimization efficiency. As a remedy, we introduce MO-CAPO, a novel multi-objective prompt optimization algorithm that jointly optimizes performance and inference cost while leveraging budget allocation for cost-efficient optimization. We further propose a deployment-oriented cost objective that captures the full computational profile of LLM inference. We evaluate our approach across four tasks and three LLMs and compare it to an NSGA-II-based multi-objective method and state-of-the-art single-objective prompt optimizers. Results show that MO-CAPO consistently identifies strong, robust, and diverse Pareto front approximations while maintaining cost-efficiency. It outperforms the NSGA-II baseline on 8 out of 12 cases in terms of the noisy R2 metric and achieves competitive performances often already at a considerably lower budget. The discovered solution sets span diverse performance-cost trade-offs that are omitted by single-objective optimizers, yet the top-performance candidates remain competitive with single-objective solutions. Additionally, we conduct the first evaluation of multi-objective machine learning experiments that considers generalization and robustness through noisy R2 and approximation gap, enabling a more realistic assessment of solution quality. MO-CAPO enables practitioners to select from an efficiently discovered set of multiple prompts offering different trade-offs between performance and cost.

Method: 提出统一框架，理论证明从观测小时间块可识别潜在过程；基于此设计Ada-Diffuser因果扩散模型，同时学习观测时间结构和潜在动态，并用于规划与控制。

Original abstract: Recent work has framed decision-making as a sequence modeling problem using generative models such as diffusion models. Although promising, these approaches often overlook latent factors that exhibit evolving dynamics, elements that are fundamental to environment transitions, reward structures, and high-level agent behavior. Explicitly modeling these hidden processes is essential for both precise dynamics modeling and effective decision-making. In this paper, we propose a unified framework that explicitly incorporates latent dynamic inference into generative decision-making from minimal yet sufficient observations. We theoretically show that under mild conditions, the latent process can be identified from small temporal blocks of observations. Building on this insight, we introduce Ada-Diffuser, a causal diffusion model that learns the temporal structure of observed interactions and the underlying latent dynamics simultaneously, and furthermore, leverages them for planning and control. With a modular design, Ada-Diffuser supports both planning and policy learning tasks, enabling adaptation to latent variations in dynamics, rewards, and latent actions. Experiments on simulated control and robotic benchmarks demonstrate its effectiveness in accurate latent inference and adaptive policy learning.

### [77] [Surrogate Neural Architecture Codesign Package (SNAC-Pack)](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16138v2)
*Jason Weitz,Dmitri Demler,Benjamin Hawks,Aaron Wang,Nhan Tran,Javier Duarte*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 硬件感知NAS框架，含agentic前端，可迁移至自动代码优化

TL;DR: SNAC-Pack是一个用于硬件感知神经架构协同设计的开源AutoML框架，通过多目标搜索和代理建模实现高效的FPGA部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有NAS方法仅优化准确率或使用与硬件成本相关性差的代理指标，尤其在FPGA部署中资源约束多维，亟需一种硬件感知的自动化协同设计方法。

Method: SNAC-Pack结合Optuna和NSGA-II进行多目标全局搜索，利用硬件代理模型估计资源与延迟，随后进行包含量化感知训练和迭代剪枝的局部压缩循环，最终通过hls4ml综合到FPGA。

Result: 在喷注分类和量子比特读出任务中，SNAC-Pack发现的紧凑架构在任务指标上匹配或超越基线，同时降低FPGA资源消耗，并将设计探索时间从数月缩短至数小时。

Conclusion: SNAC-Pack实现了FPGA部署中硬件高效的神经架构自动化协同设计，显著加速了设计空间探索。

中文摘要：神经架构搜索（NAS）是一种自动化模型设计的强大方法，但现有方法通常仅优化准确性或依赖于与硬件成本相关性较差的代理指标（如比特操作数BOPs）。这一差距在FPGA部署中尤为突出，因为成本由查找表、DSP、触发器、BRAM和延迟等多维预算主导。我们提出了代理神经架构协同设计包（SNAC-Pack），这是一个用于硬件感知神经架构协同设计和端到端FPGA部署的开源AutoML框架。SNAC-Pack使用Optuna和NSGA-II进行多目标全局搜索，将试验加载到共享的SQLite存储中，从而支持跨计算节点的并行工作。硬件代理模型输出每次试验的资源与延迟估计，避免了在搜索循环中占主导的综合成本。然后，局部搜索阶段应用量化感知训练（QAT）与迭代幅度剪枝相结合的组合压缩循环，之后最终模型通过hls4ml Python库综合到FPGA固件。YAML配置和可选的代理前端允许用户在新数据集上运行流水线，而无需修改框架。我们在大型强子对撞机的喷注分类和超导量子比特读出任务上展示了SNAC-Pack，发现了紧凑的架构，其在任务指标上匹配或超越强基线，同时降低FPGA资源利用率，并且在量子比特读出案例中，将设计空间探索过程从数月的手动微调减少为数小时的自动搜索。

Original abstract: Neural architecture search (NAS) is a powerful approach for automating model design, but existing methods often optimize for accuracy alone or rely on proxy metrics such as bit operations (BOPs) that correlate poorly with hardware cost. This gap is particularly large for FPGA deployment, where cost is dominated by a multi-dimensional budget of lookup tables, DSPs, flip-flops, BRAM, and latency. We present the Surrogate Neural Architecture Codesign Package (SNAC-Pack), an open-source AutoML framework for hardware-aware neural architecture codesign and end-to-end FPGA deployment. SNAC-Pack runs a multi-objective global search with Optuna and NSGA-II, loading trials to a shared SQLite store that enables parallel workers across compute nodes. A hardware surrogate model outputs per-trial resource and latency estimates, avoiding the synthesis cost that would otherwise dominate the search loop. A local search stage then applies quantization-aware training (QAT) together with iterative magnitude pruning in a combined compression loop, after which the final model is synthesized to FPGA firmware via the hls4ml Python library. A YAML configuration and an optional agentic frontend let users run the pipeline on new datasets without modifying the framework. We demonstrate SNAC-Pack on jet classification at the Large Hadron Collider and superconducting qubit readout, discovering compact architectures that match or exceed strong baselines on the task metric while reducing FPGA resource utilization and, in the qubit readout case, reducing the design space exploration process from months of manual fine-tuning to hours of automated search.

### [78] [Distributional Energy-Based Models for Uncertainty-Aware Structured LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18871v1)
*Shireen Kudukkil Manchingal,Abhey Kalia,Fernanda Gonçalves,Shebin Rawther*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 结构化LLM输出验证方法，可用于agent输出可靠性

TL;DR: 提出一种分解能量函数，结合学习型质量评分器和确定性约束惩罚，用于验证结构化LLM输出。149M参数的验证器协调开源生成器，在五个基准上超越或匹配更大模型，并显著减少约束违反。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型生成结构化输出时，个体步骤看似正确但整体可能违反约束，现有方法难以有效验证。需要一种结合学习与确定性约束的验证机制。

Method: 使用冻结编码器上的异质低秩适配器集成作为质量评分器，结合确定性约束惩罚构成分解能量函数。通过两遍推理循环利用不确定性驱动目标性重新生成或弃权。

Result: 在五个基准上，149M验证器协调7-26B生成器优于单次Qwen-72B，匹配Claude Sonnet 4.6，减少约束违反53%。跨数据集分析显示真正质量区分，并发现代码捷径可通过重训练缓解。

Conclusion: 结构验证与预训练先验互补：约束可检查时验证器强，不可检查时先验强。困难数据训练的评分器可零样本迁移，验证器能捕捉前沿模型无法自检的信号。

中文摘要：当大型语言模型生成结构化输出（如旅行计划、代码解决方案或多步骤证明）时，各个推理步骤可能看起来正确，但整体输出却违反预算、未通过测试用例或与之前的推导相矛盾。我们提出了一种分解能量函数，将学习的质量评分器与确定性分析约束惩罚相结合，用于验证结构化LLM输出。质量评分器是单个冻结编码器上异质低秩适配器集成（3%可训练参数）；集成均值对候选进行排名，而标准差量化认知不确定性，驱动两遍推理循环，触发目标性重新生成或弃权。在五个基准（GSM8K、MuSR、TravelPlanner、TACO、Knights & Knaves）上，我们149M参数的验证器协调一个7-26B开源生成器池，在每个基准上均优于单次Qwen-72B，在MuSR上与Claude Sonnet 4.6持平（67.7% vs. 68.0%），并在TravelPlanner上相对于Opus 4.6将约束违反减少53%（oracle 0.028, random 0.231）。这两种途径是互补的：当约束可检查时，结构验证胜出（验证器捕捉到前沿模型无法自我检测的信号），而当约束不可检查时（叙事推理、代码语义），预训练规模先验胜出。跨数据集混杂分析确认了四个推理任务上的真正质量区分，并识别出代码上的模型身份捷径，通过最后一层重训练得以缓解。在困难数据上训练的评分器零样本迁移：在MuSR上训练的评分器在GSM8K上达到93.9%，且未见过数学问题。

Original abstract: When Large Language Models produce structured outputs such as travel plans, code solutions, or multi-step proofs, individual reasoning steps may appear correct while the output as a whole violates budgets, fails test cases, or contradicts earlier deductions. We propose a decomposed energy function that combines a learned quality scorer with deterministic analytical constraint penalties for verifying structured LLM outputs. The quality scorer is a heterogeneous ensemble of low-rank adapters on a single frozen encoder (3% trainable parameters); the ensemble mean ranks candidates while the standard deviation quantifies epistemic uncertainty, driving a two-pass inference loop that triggers targeted regeneration or abstention. Across five benchmarks (GSM8K, MuSR, TravelPlanner, TACO, Knights & Knaves), our 149M-parameter verifier orchestrating a pool of 7-26B open generators outperforms single-shot Qwen-72B on every benchmark, matches Claude Sonnet 4.6 on MuSR (67.7% vs. 68.0%), and reduces constraint violations by 53% relative to Opus 4.6 on TravelPlanner (oracle 0.028, random 0.231). The two routes are complementary: structural verification wins when constraints are checkable (the verifier captures signal frontier models cannot self-detect), while pretraining-scale priors win where they are not (narrative inference, code semantics). A cross-dataset confounding analysis confirms genuine quality discrimination on four reasoning tasks and identifies a model-identity shortcut on code, mitigated via last-layer retraining. Scorers trained on difficult data transfer zero-shot: a MuSR-trained scorer achieves 93.9% on GSM8K without seeing a math problem.

### [79] [EUPHORIA: Efficient Universal Planning via Hybrid Optimization for Robust Industrial Robotic Assembly](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18872v1)
*Shih-Yu Lai,Chia-Ching Yen,Yang-Ting Shen,Peter Yichen Chen,Yu-Lun Liu,Bing-Yu Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 机器人装配规划框架，含元学习、物理注意力、残差优化，可迁移至自动化代码优化agent

TL;DR: 提出EUPHORIA统一框架，通过元几何编码器、物理信息图变换器和残差稳定性校正，实现建筑机器人装配的少样本适应性和高效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有规划器要么需针对新几何形状重新训练，要么将结构排序与运动规划分离导致效率低下。

Method: 结合基于图超网络的元几何编码器、基于SAC的物理信息图变换器（含物理偏置注意力）、运动学感知排序和残差稳定性校正。

Result: 在未见过的非标准几何形状上显著降低能耗，并取得最高成功率，仅需少量少样本示例。

Conclusion: EUPHORIA通过融合元学习、物理信息注意力和残差优化，实现了通用且高效的建筑装配规划。

中文摘要：建筑结构中的机器人装配面临一个持续的瓶颈：现有的规划器要么高度专门化，需要对每个新的几何设计进行代价高昂的重新训练，要么操作效率低下，将结构排序和运动规划视为分离的过程。我们提出了EUPHORIA，一个统一的框架，通过混合优化策略实现通用的少样本适应性和动态效率。为了克服重新训练的瓶颈，我们提出了一种基于图超网络的元几何编码器：与仅进行特征级识别的标准对比学习不同，我们的超网络从最小支持集动态生成策略参数，实现对复杂拓扑（如穹顶、拱形）的参数级适应，无需基于梯度的重新训练。对于结构推理，我们引入了一个通过柔性演员-评论家（SAC）训练的物理信息图变换器，其中包含物理偏置注意力机制，该机制使用离散元模型（DEM）模拟中的接触力来调节注意力分数，从而引导规划器关注结构关键连接。我们进一步通过运动学感知排序确保操作效率，其中SAC目标函数惩罚高能量转换。最后，我们通过残差稳定性校正来弥合Sim2Real差距，这是一个可微优化层，在执行前通过最小化联合能量-稳定性成本来微调粗装配动作。实验表明，EUPHORIA在解耦基线上显著降低了能耗，并在未见过的非标准几何形状上以最少的少样本示例实现了最先进的成功率，将元学习、物理信息注意力和残差优化融合成一个统一的通用规划器。

Original abstract: Robotic assembly in architectural construction faces a persistent bottleneck: existing planners are either highly specialized, requiring prohibitive retraining for every new geometric design, or operationally inefficient, treating structural sequencing and kinematic motion as disjoint processes. We present EUPHORIA, a unified framework that achieves universal few-shot adaptability and dynamic efficiency through a hybrid optimization strategy. To overcome the retraining bottleneck, we propose a Meta-Geometric Encoder based on Graph Hypernetworks: unlike standard contrastive learning, which performs only feature-level recognition, our hypernetwork dynamically generates policy parameters from a minimal support set, enabling parameter-level adaptation to complex topologies (e.g., domes, arches) without gradient-based retraining. For structural reasoning, we introduce a Physics-Informed Graph Transformer trained via Soft Actor-Critic (SAC), with a Physics-Bias Attention mechanism that modulates attention scores using contact forces from Discrete Element Model (DEM) simulations, guiding the planner toward structurally critical connections. We further ensure operational efficiency through Kinematics-Aware Sequencing, where the SAC objective penalizes high-energy transitions. Finally, we bridge the Sim2Real gap via Residual Stability Correction, a differentiable optimization layer that fine-tunes coarse assembly actions by minimizing a joint energy-stability cost prior to execution. Experiments show that EUPHORIA significantly reduces energy consumption over decoupled baselines and achieves state-of-the-art success rates on unseen, non-standard geometries with minimal few-shot examples, fusing meta-learning, physics-informed attention, and residual optimization into a cohesive, generalized planner.

</details>


### [80] [Learning How to Cube](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16632v1)
*Ferhat Erata,Sam Kouteili,Thanos Typaldos,Timos Antonopoulos,Robert B. Jones,Byron Cook,Ruzica Piskac*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 用MCTS和LLM训练学习SAT cubing，展示可迁移的训练框架。

TL;DR: 提出神经符号后训练框架，通过MCTS数据整理和SFT+DPO两阶段训练，使4B Transformer模型在SAT立方启发式任务上达到pass@5=53，与最佳符号方法持平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Cube-and-Conquer有效，但此前没有Transformer模型能学习有效的立方启发式，需要新的训练方法。

Method: 设计MCTS数据整理流程生成偏好数据，采用监督微调（SFT）和直接偏好优化（DPO）两阶段后训练。

Result: 4B模型在100个SAT竞赛基准上pass@5达53，超越Claude-Sonnet-4（50）并匹配最佳符号启发式（53）。

Conclusion: 证明Transformer可以通过后训练在传统由符号方法主导的SAT立方决策领域取得有效表现。

中文摘要：尽管立方与征服（C&C）在解决具有挑战性的布尔可满足性（SAT）问题方面非常有效，但此前没有研究表明基于transformer的模型可以学习有效的立方启发式。我们为此任务引入了一个神经符号的后训练框架。我们设计了一个基于MCTS的数据整理流程，利用符号启发式探索SAT竞赛公式上的分裂决策，产生基于求解器统计的偏好数据，并辅以来自教师模型的推理痕迹。我们的两阶段后训练——监督微调（SFT）后接直接偏好优化（DPO）——使一个4B参数模型在100个SAT竞赛基准测试上达到了53的pass@5分数，超越了前沿的大语言模型如Claude-Sonnet-4（50）并匹配了最佳符号启发式（53）。消融实验表明，仅SFT将pass@5从46提高到51，DPO额外增加了2个基准测试；在实现的首个立方决策上的熵/一致性消融进一步显示，SFT（而非DPO）是产生根级决策多样性的原因，从而在确定性符号方法上产生互补的每轮覆盖。这表明transformer可以被训练以在传统上由符号方法主导的领域中做出有效的立方决策。

Original abstract: Despite the effectiveness of Cube-and-Conquer (C&C) for solving challenging Boolean Satisfiability (SAT) problems, no prior work has shown that transformer-based models can learn effective cubing heuristics. We introduce a neuro-symbolic post-training framework for this task. We design an MCTS-based data curation pipeline that uses symbolic heuristics to explore splitting decisions over SAT competition formulas, producing preference data grounded in solver statistics and augmented with reasoning traces from a teacher model. Our two-stage post-training, supervised fine-tuning (SFT) followed by direct preference optimization (DPO), enables a 4B-parameter model to achieve a pass@5 score of 53 on 100 SAT competition benchmarks, surpassing frontier LLMs such as Claude-Sonnet-4 (50) and matching the best symbolic heuristic (53). Ablations show that SFT alone improves pass@5 from 46 to 51, with DPO adding 2 additional benchmarks; an entropy/agreement ablation on realized first-cube decisions further shows that SFT, not DPO, accounts for the root-level decision diversity that produces complementary per-run coverage over deterministic symbolic methods. This demonstrates that transformers can be trained to make effective cubing decisions in a domain traditionally dominated by symbolic methods.

</details>

### [81] [An Agentic Retrieval Framework for Autonomous Context-Aware Data Quality Assessment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13692v1)
*Hadi Fadlallah,Ibrahim Dhaini,Fatima Mubarak,Rima Kilany*

Main category: cs.DB

Selection reason: 多agent工作流进行数据质量评估，包含可行性验证，通用agent架构可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出了一个统一的智能体-检索框架，用于自主上下文感知的数据质量评估，通过多智能体工作流生成可执行验证逻辑，并引入可行性验证以确保可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据质量评估方法依赖静态规则或手动策略，缺乏对多样使用场景的适应性和大规模自动化能力，而大语言模型虽有潜力但存在可靠性和安全性问题。

Method: 构建一个统一智能体-检索框架，包括自然语言理解、上下文感知策略推导、多智能体工作流生成可执行验证逻辑，以及可行性验证阶段（评估规范的真实性和可执行性，支持迭代改进）。

Result: 在同一数据集上的多个使用场景中，评估结果根据预期用途自适应调整，可行性门控执行减少了不现实或不可执行的规则生成。

Conclusion: 该框架为现代数据驱动环境中部署自主但受控的数据质量评估提供了实用基础。

中文摘要：数据质量评估是有效的数据分析和数据驱动决策的关键前提，但由于数据质量固有的情境依赖性，它仍然是一项具有挑战性的任务。现有方法通常依赖于静态规则或手动评估策略，限制了其对不同使用场景的适应性，并制约了大规模自动化。人工智能的最新进展，特别是大语言模型，为自动化数据质量评估提供了新的机会，但也引发了与可靠性、基础性和执行安全性相关的担忧。在本文中，我们提出了一个统一的智能体-检索框架，用于自主的上下文感知数据质量评估。该框架解释预期数据使用的自然语言描述，推导上下文感知的评估策略，并通过多智能体工作流生成可执行的验证逻辑。为了确保操作可靠性，该框架引入了一个可行性验证阶段，在执行之前评估生成的评估规范的真实性和可执行性，从而在必要时进行迭代改进。接受的验证逻辑被确定性执行，以保证可重现和可审计的结果。我们将所提出的框架实现为一个端到端的原型，并在同一数据集的多个使用场景中对其进行评估。结果表明，评估结果会根据不同的预期用途进行有意义的调整，而可行性门控执行减少了不现实或不可执行的规则生成。所提出的方法为在现代数据驱动环境中部署自主但受控的数据质量评估提供了实用的基础。

Original abstract: Data quality assessment is a critical prerequisite for effective data analytics and data-driven decision-making, yet it remains a challenging task due to the inherently context-dependent nature of data quality. Existing approaches often rely on static rules or manual assessment strategies, limiting their adaptability to diverse usage scenarios and constraining automation at scale. Recent advances in artificial intelligence, particularly large language models, offer new opportunities for automating data quality assessment, but raise concerns related to reliability, grounding, and execution safety.
  In this paper, we propose a unified agentic-retrieval framework for autonomous context-aware data quality assessment. The framework interprets natural-language descriptions of intended data usage, derives context-aware assessment strategies, and generates executable validation logic through a multi-agent workflow. To ensure operational reliability, the framework introduces a feasibility validation stage that evaluates the realism and executability of generated assessment specifications before execution, enabling iterative refinement when necessary. Accepted validation logic is executed deterministically to guarantee reproducible and auditable results.
  We implement the proposed framework as an end-to-end prototype and evaluate it across multiple usage scenarios applied to the same dataset. The results demonstrate that assessment outcomes adapt meaningfully to different intended uses, while feasibility-gated execution reduces unrealistic or non-executable rule generation. The proposed approach provides a practical foundation for deploying autonomous yet controlled data quality assessment in modern data-driven environments.

### [82] [DiffVAS: Diffusion-Guided Visual Active Search in Partially Observable Environments](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15519v1)
*Anindya Sarkar,Srikumar Sastry,Aleksis Pirinen,Nathan Jacobs,Yevgeniy Vorobeychik*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 视觉主动搜索agent，包含目标条件规划和部分可观测环境推理，可迁移至visual coding agent

TL;DR: 提出DiffVAS，一种目标条件策略，利用扩散模型重建部分可观测环境，通过强化学习规划同时搜索多种目标，显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VAS方法假设搜索空间已知且只能搜索单一目标，不适用于现实中的部分可观测环境和多目标搜索需求。

Method: DiffVAS使用扩散模型从部分观测重建完整地理区域，并结合目标条件的强化学习规划模块指导搜索。

Result: 在多个数据集上，DiffVAS在搜索多样目标方面显著超越最先进方法。

Conclusion: DiffVAS能够有效应对部分可观测环境中的多目标搜索，推动了VAS在实际应用中的部署。

中文摘要：视觉主动搜索（VAS）已被引入作为一种建模框架，利用视觉线索引导空中（例如，基于无人机）探索，并在广阔的地理区域内精确定位感兴趣的区域。VAS的潜在应用包括检测稀有野生动物偷猎热点、辅助搜索救援任务以及发现非法武器贩运等。以往的VAS方法假设整个搜索空间是已知的，这通常不现实，因为存在视野受限和高获取成本等约束，并且它们通常学习针对特定目标对象的策略，这限制了同时搜索多个目标类别的能力。在这项工作中，我们提出DiffVAS，一种目标条件策略，能够根据任务需求在部分可观测环境中同时搜索多样化的对象，从而推动视觉主动搜索策略在现实世界应用中的部署。DiffVAS利用扩散模型从顺序观测的部分快照中重建整个地理区域，使得基于目标条件的强化学习规划模块能够有效地推理并指导后续搜索步骤。大量实验表明，DiffVAS在部分可观测环境中搜索多样化对象方面表现出色，在多个数据集上显著超越了最先进的方法。

Original abstract: Visual active search (VAS) has been introduced as a modeling framework that leverages visual cues to direct aerial (e.g., UAV-based) exploration and pinpoint areas of interest within extensive geospatial regions. Potential applications of VAS include detecting hotspots for rare wildlife poaching, aiding search-and-rescue missions, and uncovering illegal trafficking of weapons, among other uses. Previous VAS approaches assume that the entire search space is known upfront, which is often unrealistic due to constraints such as a restricted field of view and high acquisition costs, and they typically learn policies tailored to specific target objects, which limits their ability to search for multiple target categories simultaneously. In this work, we propose DiffVAS, a target-conditioned policy that searches for diverse objects simultaneously according to task requirements in partially observable environments, which advances the deployment of visual active search policies in real-world applications. DiffVAS leverages a diffusion model to reconstruct the entire geospatial area from sequentially observed partial glimpses, which enables a target-conditioned reinforcement learning-based planning module to effectively reason and guide subsequent search steps. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DiffVAS excels in searching diverse objects in partially observable environments, significantly surpassing state-of-the-art methods on several datasets.

</details>


### [83] [VideoSeeker: Incentivizing Instance-level Video Understanding via Native Agentic Tool Invocation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16079v1)
*Yiming Zhao,Yu Zeng,Wenxuan Huang,Zhen Fang,Qing Miao,Qisheng Su,Jiawei Zhao,Jiayin Cai,Lin Chen,Zehui Chen,Yukun Qi,Yao Hu,Xiaolong Jiang,Feng Zhao*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 视频理解agent，集成工具调用与RL训练，涉及agentic reasoning，可迁移到coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出VideoSeeker，通过视觉提示和代理推理实现实例级视频理解，利用四阶段数据合成和RL训练，在实例级任务上平均提升13.7%，超越GPT-4o和Gemini-2.5-Pro。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LVLMs在实例级视频理解中依赖文本提示，缺乏精确时空参考，且视觉感知与语言推理解耦，限制主动感知能力。

Method: 提出VideoSeeker范式，集成代理推理与实例级视频理解；构建四阶段自动化数据合成管道；通过冷启动监督和强化学习训练内化工具调用和主动感知能力。

Result: 在实例级视频理解任务上平均提升+13.7%，超越GPT-4o和Gemini-2.5-Pro，并在通用视频理解基准上有效迁移。

Conclusion: VideoSeeker通过视觉提示和代理推理有效提升实例级视频理解，数据合成和训练方法可扩展，性能优越。

中文摘要：大型视觉语言模型（LVLMs）在视频理解方面取得了显著进展，但在需要精确时空定位的实例级任务中仍面临巨大挑战。现有方法主要依赖文本提示进行人机交互，但这些提示难以提供精确的空间和时间参考，导致用户体验不佳。此外，当前方法通常将视觉感知与语言推理解耦，以语言为中心而非视觉内容进行推理，限制了模型主动感知细粒度视觉证据的能力。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了VideoSeeker，一种通过视觉提示进行实例级视频理解的新范式。VideoSeeker将代理推理与实例级视频理解任务无缝集成，使模型能够根据需要主动感知和检索相关视频片段。我们构建了一个四阶段全自动数据合成管道，以高效生成大规模、高质量的实例级视频数据。通过冷启动监督和强化学习训练，我们将工具调用和主动感知能力内化到模型中，构建了一个强大的视频理解模型。实验表明，我们的模型在实例级视频理解任务上平均比基线提升了+13.7%，超越了GPT-4o和Gemini-2.5-Pro等强大的闭源模型，同时在通用视频理解基准上也显示出有效的迁移能力。相关数据集和代码将公开发布。

Original abstract: Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) have shown significant progress in video understanding, yet they face substantial challenges in tasks requiring precise spatiotemporal localization at the instance level. Existing methods primarily rely on text prompts for human-model interaction, but these prompts struggle to provide precise spatial and temporal references, resulting in poor user experience. Furthermore, current approaches typically decouple visual perception from language reasoning, centering reasoning around language rather than visual content, which limits the model's ability to proactively perceive fine-grained visual evidence. To address these challenges, we propose VideoSeeker, a novel paradigm for instance-level video understanding through visual prompts. VideoSeeker seamlessly integrates agentic reasoning with instance-level video understanding tasks, enabling the model to proactively perceive and retrieve relevant video segments on demand. We construct a four-stage fully automated data synthesis pipeline to efficiently generate large-scale, high-quality instance-level video data. We internalize tool-calling and proactive perception capabilities into the model via cold-start supervision and RL training, building a powerful video understanding model. Experiments demonstrate that our model achieves an average improvement of +13.7% over baselines on instance-level video understanding tasks, surpassing powerful closed-source models such as GPT-4o and Gemini-2.5-Pro, while also showing effective transferability on general video understanding benchmarks. The relevant datasets and code will be released publicly.

</details>


### [84] [Visual Agentic Memory: Enabling Online Long Video Understanding via Online Indexing, Hierarchical Memory, and Agentic Retrieval](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16481v1)
*Aiden Yiliu Li,Nels Numan,Anthony Steed*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 提出视觉agent记忆框架，含在线索引、分层记忆和检索，通用agent记忆方法

TL;DR: VAM是一种无需训练的长视频理解框架，通过显式记忆机制显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长视频理解方法依赖大的上下文窗口或压缩潜在状态，缺乏可检查、可搜索的显式记忆机制，难以在长时间跨度内有效检索和利用视觉证据。

Method: 提出Visual Agentic Memory (VAM)，包含三个组件：在线索引（Online Indexing）支持流式数据下的选择性证据保留，分层记忆（Hierarchical Memory）以并行表示组织时空信息，代理检索（Agentic Retrieval）搜索、检查并验证候选证据后生成答案。

Result: 在OVO-Bench上VAM的RT+BT平均值为68.41，超越基线Gemini 3 Flash（67.46）；在MM-Lifelong月尺度划分上达到17.11%，仅次于使用GPT-5的ReMA（17.62%）。

Conclusion: 长时程视频理解应依赖显式、可检查和可查询的视觉记忆基板，而非仅靠压缩表示或大上下文窗口。

中文摘要：长视频理解需要的不仅仅是大的上下文窗口。它还需要一种记忆机制，来决定保留哪些视觉证据，使其在长时间跨度内可搜索，并将后续推理建立在可恢复的观察之上，而不仅仅是压缩的潜在状态。我们提出了视觉代理记忆（VAM），一个无需训练的框架，包含三个组件。在线索引支持在流式约束下选择性保留证据。分层记忆以并行表示组织保留的证据，将时间上下文与空间观察对齐。代理检索在生成有依据的答案之前搜索、检查和验证候选证据。在OVO-Bench上，VAM在所有报告基线中取得了最高的RT+BT平均值（68.41），相比直接使用相同底层MLLM（Gemini 3 Flash，67.46）有所提升。在MM-Lifelong的月尺度划分train@month（51天内105.6小时）上，VAM达到了17.11%，仅次于使用GPT-5的ReMA（17.62%）。这些结果表明，长时程视频理解受益于将视觉记忆视为显式、可检查和可查询的基板。代码可在https://github.com/yiliu-li/Visual-Agentic-Memory获取。

Original abstract: Long video understanding requires more than large context windows. It also needs a memory mechanism that decides what visual evidence to retain, keeps it searchable over long horizons, and grounds later reasoning in recoverable observations rather than compressed latent state alone. We propose Visual Agentic Memory (VAM), a training-free framework with three components. Online Indexing supports selective evidence retention under streaming constraints. Hierarchical Memory organises retained evidence in a Parallel Representation that aligns temporal context with spatial observations. Agentic Retrieval searches, inspects, and verifies candidate evidence before producing a grounded answer. On OVO-Bench, VAM achieves the highest RT+BT average (68.41) across all reported baselines, improving over end-to-end use of the same underlying MLLM (Gemini 3 Flash, 67.46). On the month-scale split of MM-Lifelong train@month (105.6 hours over 51 days), VAM reaches 17.11%, second only to ReMA with GPT-5 (17.62%). These results suggest that long-horizon video understanding benefits from treating visual memory as an explicit, inspectable, and queryable substrate. Code is available at https://github.com/yiliu-li/Visual-Agentic-Memory.

</details>

# cs.RO [[Back]](#toc)

### [85] [Hybrid LLM-based Intelligent Framework for Robot Task Scheduling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15486v1)
*Swayamjit Saha,Subhabrata Das,Haonan Duan,Xiao-Yang Liu*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 利用LLM agent进行机器人任务调度，涉及多agent协作与规划，方法可迁移至coding agent

TL;DR: 提出利用双LLM智能体（生成器+监督器）和NLP接口的框架，优化建筑机器人任务调度，平衡时间与资源，实验验证有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建筑机器人任务调度需高效且适应动态环境，现有方法不足，LLM可提供智能决策。

Method: 使用双LLM智能体（GPT-4生成器，Gemma3/Llama4/Mistral7b监督器），结合NLP接口和平衡分配策略。

Result: 在简单场景中评估，指标分数证明框架在时间效率和资源利用率上的有效性。

Conclusion: LLM在建筑机器人调度中发挥关键作用，能显著提升操作任务的效率与适应性。

中文摘要：本研究引入了利用大语言模型（LLMs）改进建筑机器人任务调度的智能框架。LLM被输入关于所需任务的关键数据，如智能体行动能力和期望达成的最终目标。开发了一种平衡的分配策略，优化了时间效率和资源利用率。我们的系统利用自然语言处理界面来简化与建筑专业人员的沟通，并实时适应意外的现场条件。我们同时使用两个LLM智能体，即生成器（GPT-4）和监督器（Gemma 3/Llama 4/Mistral 7b）LLM智能体，以提供更精确的任务调度。我们通过一个简单的场景评估所提出的方法，并提供指标分数来证明框架的有效性。我们的结果强调了LLM在包括机器人在内的建筑操作任务中的关键作用。

Original abstract: This study introduces intelligent frameworks that use Large Language Models (LLMs) to improve task scheduling for construction robots. The LLM is fed with key data about the desired task, such as agent action abilities, and the desired end goal to be achieved. A well-balanced allocation strategy is developed, optimizing both time efficiency and resource utilization. Our system utilizes a Natural Language Processing interface to streamline communication with construction professionals and adapt in real-time to unexpected site conditions. We concurrently use two LLM agents, specifically generator (GPT-4) and supervisor (Gemma 3/Llama 4/Mistral 7b) LLM agents to provide a more precise task schedule. We evaluate the proposed methodology using a straightforward scenario and provide metric scores to prove the efficacy of the frameworks. Our results highlight that the implementation of LLMs is crucial in construction operational tasks including robots.

</details>


### [86] [Feedback World Model Enables Precise Guidance of Diffusion Policy](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15705v1)
*Tuo An,Jindou Jia,Gen Li,Jingliang Li,Chuhao Zhou,Pengfei Liu,Bofan Lyu,Jiaqi Bai,Xinying Guo,Geng Li,Jianfei Yang*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 反馈世界模型改进机器人决策，虽垂直但提出了在线校正的通用范式，可启发agent中的预测与反馈机制。

TL;DR: 提出反馈世界模型，利用执行后的实时观测在线纠正预测，提高了分布偏移下的预测准确性和策略性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 世界模型在遇到分布外状态时预测不可靠，而执行后的真实观测未被充分利用。

Method: 维护一个轻量级反馈状态在线更新以迭代纠正预测，并引入动作感知引导以强调可控分量。

Result: 预测误差降低76.4%，OOD成功率提高30%。

Conclusion: 推理时实时反馈是静态世界建模的简单强大替代方案。

中文摘要：世界模型旨在通过预测动作的后果来改进机器人决策。然而，在实际应用中，一旦机器人遇到训练分布之外的状态，其预测往往变得不可靠，限制了部署时的有效性。我们观察到，执行本身提供了一个自然但未被充分利用的信号：每个动作之后，机器人直接观察到真实的下一个状态，揭示了预测与实际结果之间的不匹配。基于这一见解，我们提出了反馈世界模型（feedback world model），一种在推理时闭合预测与观测之间循环的新范式。我们的方法不是将世界模型视为静态的开环预测器，而是维护一个轻量级的反馈状态，该状态在线更新以迭代地纠正未来的预测，利用实时观测补偿模型误差，无需额外的训练数据或参数更新。我们证明，这一过程可以解释为潜在空间观测器，并在温和条件下具有收敛保证。我们进一步引入了动作感知引导（action-aware guidance），通过强调动作可控组件并抑制不相关的变化，更好地将纠正后的预测转化为控制。在LIBERO-Plus、Robomimic和实际操作任务上的实验表明，我们的方法在分布偏移下显著提高了预测准确性和策略性能。特别是，它将世界模型预测误差降低了高达76.4%，并将分布外（OOD）成功率提高了30%。这些结果表明，在推理时整合实时反馈为静态世界建模提供了一种简单而强大的替代方案。

Original abstract: World models aim to improve robotic decision making by predicting the consequences of actions. However, in practice, their predictions often become unreliable once the robot encounters states outside the training distribution, limiting their effectiveness at deployment. We observe that execution itself provides a natural but underutilized signal: after each action, the robot directly observes the true next state, revealing the mismatch between predicted and actual outcomes. Building on this insight, we propose feedback world model, a new paradigm that closes the loop between prediction and observation at inference time. Instead of treating the world model as a static open-loop predictor, our method maintains a lightweight feedback state that is updated online to iteratively correct future predictions, compensating for model errors using real-time observations without additional training data or parameter updates. We show that this process can be interpreted as a latent-space observer and admits convergence guarantees under mild conditions. We further introduce action-aware guidance to better translate corrected predictions into control by emphasizing action-controllable components while suppressing irrelevant variations. Experiments on LIBERO-Plus, Robomimic, and real-world manipulation tasks demonstrate that our method substantially improves both prediction accuracy and policy performance under distribution shift. In particular, it reduces world model prediction error by up to 76.4% and improves out-of-distribution (OOD) success rate by 30%. These results show that incorporating real-time feedback at inference time provides a simple yet powerful alternative to static world modeling.

</details>
